/* ---------- event wiring ---------- */
function attachHandlers(){
  const app = document.getElementById('app');
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-tab]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.inventorySupplierFilter = null; state.supplierFilterName = '';
    state.mobileMenuOpen = false;
    setTab(el.getAttribute('data-tab'));
  }); });
  const hamburgerBtn = document.getElementById('hamburgerBtn');
  if(hamburgerBtn) hamburgerBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.mobileMenuOpen = true; render(); });
  const railCloseBtn = document.getElementById('railCloseBtn');
  if(railCloseBtn) railCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.mobileMenuOpen = false; render(); });
  const railBackdrop = document.getElementById('railBackdrop');
  if(railBackdrop) railBackdrop.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.mobileMenuOpen = false; render(); });
  const logoutBtn = document.getElementById('logoutBtn');
  if(logoutBtn) logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){ await sb.auth.signOut(); state.stage='auth'; state.profile=null; render(); });

  const notifBellBtn = document.getElementById('notifBellBtn');
  if(notifBellBtn) notifBellBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal('notifSettings'); });

  const themeSettingsBtn = document.getElementById('themeSettingsBtn');
  if(themeSettingsBtn) themeSettingsBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal('themeSettings'); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-set-theme]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ setTheme(el.getAttribute('data-set-theme')); }); });
  
  const enablePushInline = document.getElementById('enablePushInline');
  if(enablePushInline) enablePushInline.addEventListener('click', enablePush);
  const enablePushBtn = document.getElementById('enablePushBtn');
  if(enablePushBtn) enablePushBtn.addEventListener('click', enablePush);
  const disablePushBtn = document.getElementById('disablePushBtn');
  if(disablePushBtn) disablePushBtn.addEventListener('click', disablePush);

  const gs = document.getElementById('globalSearch');
  if(gs){
    gs.addEventListener('input', function(e){
      state.searchQuery = e.target.value; render();
      const el = document.getElementById('globalSearch'); el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.searchQuery.length;
    });
  }
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-open-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.searchQuery='';
    const type = el.getAttribute('data-open-item-type')==='Laptop' ? 'editLaptop' : 'editPhone';
    openModal(type,{id:el.getAttribute('data-open-phone')});
  }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-open-modal]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal(el.getAttribute('data-open-modal'), {id:el.getAttribute('data-id')}); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-modal]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', closeModal); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-overlay]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', closeModal); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-stop]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-network-view]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.networkView = el.getAttribute('data-network-view'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-inventory-item-tab]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.inventoryItemTab = el.getAttribute('data-inventory-item-tab');
    state.selectedInventoryIds = [];
    state.inventorySupplierFilter = null; state.supplierFilterName = '';
    render();
  }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-type-filter]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.networkBroadcastTypeFilter = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-type-filter'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-network-category-filter]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.networkCategoryFilter = el.getAttribute('data-network-category-filter'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-toggle-status]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ toggleStatus(el.getAttribute('data-toggle-status')); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-stock-item]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    openModal('viewStockItem', { broadcastId: el.getAttribute('data-view-stock-item'), itemIndex: Number(el.getAttribute('data-item-index')) });
  }); });

  /* ---- Image gallery navigation (network item / stock item detail modals) ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-gallery-prev]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    e.stopPropagation();
    const total = Number(el.getAttribute('data-gallery-total'))||1;
    state.galleryIndex = ((state.galleryIndex||0) - 1 + total) % total;
    render();
  }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-gallery-next]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    e.stopPropagation();
    const total = Number(el.getAttribute('data-gallery-total'))||1;
    state.galleryIndex = ((state.galleryIndex||0) + 1) % total;
    render();
  }); });
  const galleryWrap = document.getElementById('galleryWrap');
  if(galleryWrap){
    let touchStartX = null;
    galleryWrap.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e){ touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX; }, {passive:true});
    galleryWrap.addEventListener('touchend', function(e){
      if(touchStartX==null) return;
      const dx = e.changedTouches[0].clientX - touchStartX;
      const total = Number(galleryWrap.getAttribute('data-gallery-total'))||1;
      if(Math.abs(dx) > 40 && total>1){
        state.galleryIndex = dx<0 ? ((state.galleryIndex||0)+1)%total : ((state.galleryIndex||0)-1+total)%total;
        render();
      }
      touchStartX = null;
    });
  }

  /* ---- "Owed to you" row click -> detail dialog ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    if(e.target.closest('button')) return;
    openModal('viewConsignment', { id: el.getAttribute('data-view-consignment') });
  }); });

  /* ---- Inventory selection + "send as broadcast" ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-select-inventory]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-select-inventory');
    const idx = state.selectedInventoryIds.indexOf(id);
    if(el.checked && idx===-1) state.selectedInventoryIds.push(id);
    else if(!el.checked && idx>-1) state.selectedInventoryIds.splice(idx,1);
    render();
  }); });
  const clearSelectionBtn = document.getElementById('clearSelectionBtn');
  if(clearSelectionBtn) clearSelectionBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.selectedInventoryIds = []; render(); });
  const selectAllInStockBtn = document.getElementById('selectAllInStockBtn');
  if(selectAllInStockBtn) selectAllInStockBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.selectedInventoryIds = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return p.status==='In Stock'; }).map(function(p){ return p.id; });
    render();
  });
  const broadcastSelectedBtn = document.getElementById('broadcastSelectedBtn');
  if(broadcastSelectedBtn) broadcastSelectedBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ openBroadcastComposer(state.selectedInventoryIds.slice()); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-single]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ openBroadcastComposer([el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-single')]); }); });

  /* ---- Broadcast composer (send stock as a broadcast) ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-target]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.broadcastComposer.target = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-target'); render();
  }); });
  const bcMessage = document.getElementById('bc-message');
  if(bcMessage) bcMessage.addEventListener('input', function(e){
    state.broadcastComposer.message = e.target.value; render();
    const el = document.getElementById('bc-message'); if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.broadcastComposer.message.length; }
  });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-contact]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-contact');
    const idx = state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.indexOf(id);
    if(el.checked && idx===-1) state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.push(id);
    else if(!el.checked && idx>-1) state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.splice(idx,1);
    render();
  }); });
  const sendNetworkBroadcastBtn = document.getElementById('sendNetworkBroadcastBtn');
  if(sendNetworkBroadcastBtn) sendNetworkBroadcastBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const ids = state.broadcastComposer.ids;
    const items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return ids.indexOf(p.id)>-1; });
    if(!items.length){ showToast('Nothing to broadcast', true); return; }
    const itemsPayload = items.map(function(p){ return {
      inventory_id:p.id, item_type:p.item_type||'Phone', model:p.model, brand:p.brand, storage:p.storage, color:p.color,
      condition:p.condition, price:p.price, cpu:p.cpu, ram:p.ram, screen_size:p.screen_size, gpu:p.gpu,
      image_url:p.image_url, image_urls: imagesFor(p)
    }; });
    const data = {
      dealer_id: state.profile.id, type:'Stock', status:'Open',
      model: items.length===1 ? items[0].model : (items.length+' items'),
      items: itemsPayload, message: state.broadcastComposer.message || null
    };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      state.selectedInventoryIds = []; state.broadcastComposer = {ids:[], target:'network', message:'', selectedContactIds:[]};
      closeModal(); showToast('Stock advert sent to the network');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Broadcast failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  });
  const logContactBroadcastBtn = document.getElementById('logContactBroadcastBtn');
  if(logContactBroadcastBtn) logContactBroadcastBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const ids = state.broadcastComposer.ids;
    const items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return ids.indexOf(p.id)>-1; });
    const contactIds = state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds;
    if(!contactIds.length){ showToast('Select at least one saved contact', true); return; }
    const names = contactIds.map(function(id){ const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; }); return s?s.name:''; }).filter(Boolean);
    const itemsPayload = items.map(function(p){ return {
      inventory_id:p.id, item_type:p.item_type||'Phone', model:p.model, brand:p.brand, storage:p.storage, color:p.color,
      condition:p.condition, price:p.price, cpu:p.cpu, ram:p.ram, screen_size:p.screen_size, gpu:p.gpu,
      image_url:p.image_url, image_urls: imagesFor(p)
    }; });
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('stock_broadcast_log').insert({
        dealer_id: state.profile.id, contact_names: names.join(', '), items: itemsPayload, message: state.broadcastComposer.message || null
      });
      if(error) throw error;
      showToast('Saved — tap each contact above to open WhatsApp with the message');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Could not save: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  });

  const dealerSearch = document.getElementById('dealerSearch');
  if(dealerSearch) dealerSearch.addEventListener('input', function(e){
    state.dealerSearchQuery = e.target.value; render();
    const el = document.getElementById('dealerSearch'); if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.dealerSearchQuery.length; }
  });

  const dealerFilterInput = document.getElementById('dealerFilterInput');
  if(dealerFilterInput){
    dealerFilterInput.addEventListener('focus', function(){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
      if(!state.dealerFilterOpen){
        state.dealerFilterOpen = true; render();
        const el = document.getElementById('dealerFilterInput');
        if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = el.value.length; }
      }
    });
    dealerFilterInput.addEventListener('input', function(e){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
      state.dealerFilterQuery = e.target.value; state.dealerFilterOpen = true; render();
      const el = document.getElementById('dealerFilterInput'); if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.dealerFilterQuery.length; }
    });
    dealerFilterInput.addEventListener('blur', function(){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer) clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer);
      dealerFilterBlurTimer = setTimeout(function(){ dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; state.dealerFilterOpen = false; render(); }, 150);
    });
  }
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-select-dealer-filter]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e){ e.preventDefault(); });
    el.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
      state.networkDealerFilter = el.getAttribute('data-select-dealer-filter');
      state.dealerFilterQuery = ''; state.dealerFilterOpen = false; render();
    });
  });
  const clearDealerFilterBtn = document.getElementById('clearDealerFilterBtn');
  if(clearDealerFilterBtn) clearDealerFilterBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
    state.networkDealerFilter = null; state.dealerFilterQuery = ''; render();

  if(fSupplierId) fSupplierId.addEventListener('change', function(){

    const fSupplier = document.getElementById('f-supplier');
    if(s && fSupplier) fSupplier.value = s.name;
  });
  const lSupplierId = document.getElementById('l-supplier-id');

    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === lSupplierId.value; });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-remove-existing-image]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    const url = el.getAttribute('data-remove-existing-image');
    state.photoModalRemovedUrls = state.photoModalRemovedUrls || [];
    state.photoModalRemovedUrls.push(url);
    render();
  }); });
  function wirePhotoPreview(inputId){
    const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
    if(!input) return;
    input.addEventListener('change', function(){
      const preview = document.getElementById('new-photo-preview');
      if(!preview) return;
      preview.innerHTML = '';
      Array.from(input.files||[]).forEach(function(file){
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        img.className = 'photo-preview'; img.style.width='72px'; img.style.height='72px';
        img.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);
        preview.appendChild(img);
      });
    });
  }
  wirePhotoPreview('f-images');
  wirePhotoPreview('l-images');

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-phone');
    const data = {
      item_type: 'Phone',
      imei: val('f-imei')||null, imei2: val('f-imei2')||null, model: val('f-model'), storage: val('f-storage'),
      color: val('f-color'), condition: val('f-condition'), battery: Number(val('f-battery')),
      supplier: val('f-supplier'), supplier_id: val('f-supplier-id')||null, purchase_date: todayISO(), cost: Number(val('f-cost')), price: Number(val('f-price')),
      status: val('f-status'), shelf: val('f-shelf'), notes: val('f-notes')
    };
    if(!data.model){ showToast('Phone model is required', true); return; }
    const existingPhone = id ? state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; }) : null;
    const existingImages = imagesFor(existingPhone);
    const removed = state.photoModalRemovedUrls || [];
    let keptImages = existingImages.filter(function(u){ return removed.indexOf(u)===-1; });
    const fImagesEl = document.getElementById('f-images');
    const newFiles = fImagesEl && fImagesEl.files ? Array.from(fImagesEl.files) : [];
    try{
      if(newFiles.length){
        showToast('Uploading '+newFiles.length+' photo'+(newFiles.length===1?'':'s')+'…');
        for(let i=0;i<newFiles.length;i++){
          const url = await uploadPhoneImage(newFiles[i]);
          keptImages.push(url);
        }
      }
      data.image_urls = keptImages;
      data.image_url = keptImages.length ? keptImages[0] : null;
      if(id){ const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').update(data).eq('id', id); if(error) throw error; }
      else{ data.dealer_id = state.profile.id; const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').insert(data); if(error) throw error; }
      await refreshAll();
      state.photoModalRemovedUrls = [];
      closeModal(); showToast(id?'Phone updated':'Phone added to inventory');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-laptop]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-laptop');
    const data = {
      item_type: 'Laptop',
      brand: val('l-brand')||null, model: val('l-model'), cpu: val('l-cpu')||null, ram: val('l-ram')||null,
      storage: val('l-storage'), screen_size: val('l-screen')||null, gpu: val('l-gpu')||null,
      color: val('l-color'), condition: val('l-condition'), battery: val('l-battery')?Number(val('l-battery')):null,
      supplier: val('l-supplier'), supplier_id: val('l-supplier-id')||null, purchase_date: todayISO(), cost: Number(val('l-cost')), price: Number(val('l-price')),
      status: val('l-status'), shelf: val('l-shelf'), notes: val('l-notes')
    };
    if(!data.model){ showToast('Laptop model is required', true); return; }
    const existingLaptop = id ? state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; }) : null;
    const existingImages = imagesFor(existingLaptop);
    const removed = state.photoModalRemovedUrls || [];
    let keptImages = existingImages.filter(function(u){ return removed.indexOf(u)===-1; });
    const lImagesEl = document.getElementById('l-images');
    const newFiles = lImagesEl && lImagesEl.files ? Array.from(lImagesEl.files) : [];
    try{
      if(newFiles.length){
        showToast('Uploading '+newFiles.length+' photo'+(newFiles.length===1?'':'s')+'…');
        for(let i=0;i<newFiles.length;i++){
          const url = await uploadPhoneImage(newFiles[i]);
          keptImages.push(url);
        }
      }
      data.image_urls = keptImages;
      data.image_url = keptImages.length ? keptImages[0] : null;
      if(id){ const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').update(data).eq('id', id); if(error) throw error; }
      else{ data.dealer_id = state.profile.id; const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').insert(data); if(error) throw error; }
      await refreshAll();
      state.photoModalRemovedUrls = [];
      closeModal(); showToast(id?'Laptop updated':'Laptop added to inventory');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-delete-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){

  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-sale]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const inventoryId = val('s-inventory-id');
    if(!inventoryId){ showToast('Select a phone to sell', true); return; }
    const price = Number(val('s-price'));
    if(!price){ showToast('Enter a sale price', true); return; }
    try{
      const { data, error } = await sb.rpc('sell_phone', {
        p_inventory_id: inventoryId, p_sale_price: price, p_customer_name: val('s-name'), p_customer_phone: val('s-phone'),
        p_payment_method: val('s-payment'), p_staff: val('s-staff'), p_warranty_days: Number(val('s-warranty'))||0,
        p_accessories: val('s-accessories'), p_notes: '',
        p_imei: val('s-imei')||null, p_quantity: Number(val('s-quantity'))||1
      });
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Sale logged — invoice downloading');
      const savedSale = Array.isArray(data) ? data[0] : data;
      if(savedSale) generateInvoicePDF(savedSale);
    } catch(e){ showToast('Sale failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-supplier]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-supplier');
    const name = val('sup-name');
    if(!name){ showToast('Name is required', true); return; }
    const data = { name:name, phone:val('sup-phone'), whatsapp:val('sup-phone'), location:val('sup-location'), supplies:val('sup-supplies'), owed:Number(val('sup-owed'))||0 };
    try{
      if(id){
        const { error } = await sb.from('suppliers').update(data).eq('id', id);
        if(error) throw error;
        closeModal(); showToast('Contact updated');
      } else {
        data.dealer_id = state.profile.id;
        const { error } = await sb.from('suppliers').insert(data);
        if(error) throw error;
        closeModal(); showToast('Contact added');
      }
      await refreshAll();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  /* ---- Consignments (phones out with colleagues on credit) ---- */
  const cnContactId = document.getElementById('cn-contact-id');
  if(cnContactId) cnContactId.addEventListener('change', function(){

    if(s){
      const nameEl = document.getElementById('cn-name'), phoneEl = document.getElementById('cn-phone');
      if(nameEl) nameEl.value = s.name;
      if(phoneEl) phoneEl.value = s.phone || '';
    }
  });
  const cnInventoryId = document.getElementById('cn-inventory-id');
  if(cnInventoryId) cnInventoryId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const p = state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id === cnInventoryId.value; });
    if(p){
      const set = function(id,v){ const el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.value = v||''; };
      set('cn-model', p.model); set('cn-storage', p.storage); set('cn-color', p.color); set('cn-imei', p.imei);
      if(!val('cn-price') && p.price) set('cn-price', p.price);
    }
  });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-consignment');
    const contactName = val('cn-name');
    const model = val('cn-model');
    if(!contactName){ showToast('Colleague name is required', true); return; }
    if(!model){ showToast('Phone model is required', true); return; }
    const data = {
      contact_id: val('cn-contact-id')||null, contact_name: contactName, contact_phone: val('cn-phone'),
      inventory_id: val('cn-inventory-id')||null, model: model, storage: val('cn-storage'), color: val('cn-color'), imei: val('cn-imei')||null,
      quantity: Number(val('cn-quantity'))||1, unit_price: Number(val('cn-price'))||0, amount_paid: Number(val('cn-paid'))||0,
      date_given: val('cn-date')||todayISO(), due_date: val('cn-due')||null, notes: val('cn-notes')
    };
    const total = data.unit_price*data.quantity;
    data.status = data.amount_paid<=0 ? 'Out' : (data.amount_paid>=total ? 'Settled' : 'Partially Paid');
    try{
      if(id){ const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').update(data).eq('id', id); if(error) throw error; }
      else { data.dealer_id = state.profile.id; const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').insert(data); if(error) throw error; }
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast(id?'Consignment updated':'Logged — you\'ll see it under Owed');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-delete-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-delete-consignment');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').delete().eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Consignment removed');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Delete failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-log-consignment-payment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-log-consignment-payment');
    const c = state.consignments.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
    if(!c) return;
    const amount = Number(val('cnp-amount'))||0;
    if(amount<=0){ showToast('Enter an amount received', true); return; }
    const newPaid = (Number(c.amount_paid)||0) + amount;
    const total = (Number(c.unit_price)||0)*(Number(c.quantity)||1);
    const newStatus = newPaid >= total ? 'Settled' : 'Partially Paid';
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').update({ amount_paid:newPaid, status:newStatus }).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      const { error: payErr } = await sb.from('consignment_payments').insert({
        consignment_id: id, dealer_id: state.profile.id, amount: amount, note: val('cnp-note')||null
      });
      if(payErr) throw payErr;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast(newStatus==='Settled' ? 'Fully paid — marked as settled' : 'Payment logged');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-mark-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const status = el.getAttribute('data-mark-consignment');
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-id');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').update({ status:status }).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Marked as '+status.toLowerCase());
    } catch(e){ showToast('Failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-print-invoice]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){

  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-broadcast]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const model = val('b-model');
    if(!model){ showToast('Enter a phone model', true); return; }
    const data = { dealer_id: state.profile.id, type:'Need', model:model, storage:val('b-variant'), urgency: val('b-urgency')||'Normal', status:'Open' };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Broadcast sent to the network');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Broadcast failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-broadcast]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-close-broadcast');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').update({status:'Closed'}).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      showToast('Broadcast closed'); render();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Update failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-accept-response]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const responseId = el.getAttribute('data-accept-response');
    const broadcastId = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').update({ accepted_response_id: responseId, status: 'Closed' }).eq('id', broadcastId);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      showToast('Marked as accepted — this dealer\'s reputation just went up'); render();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Could not accept: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-response]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const broadcastId = el.getAttribute('data-save-response');
    const price = Number(val('rb-price'));
    if(!price){ showToast('Enter your price', true); return; }
    const data = { broadcast_id: broadcastId, dealer_id: state.profile.id, price:price, quantity:Number(val('rb-qty'))||1, contact_phone: val('rb-phone') };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcast_responses').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Response sent');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  const biParseBtn = document.getElementById('bi-parse-btn');
  if(biParseBtn) biParseBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    const text = val('bi-text');
    state.bulkImportText = text;
    state.bulkImportCondition = val('bi-condition');
    state.bulkImportSupplier = val('bi-supplier');
    state.bulkImportSupplierId = val('bi-supplier-id') || null;
    const parsed = parseBulkStock(text);
    state.bulkImportRows = parsed.rows; state.bulkImportSkipped = parsed.skipped;
    if(!state.bulkImportRows.length){ showToast('No recognizable stock lines found in that paste', true); return; }
    render();
  });
  const biBackBtn = document.getElementById('bi-back-btn');
  if(biBackBtn) biBackBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.bulkImportRows = []; render(); });

  const biSupplierId = document.getElementById('bi-supplier-id');
  if(biSupplierId) biSupplierId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === biSupplierId.value; });
    const biSupplier = document.getElementById('bi-supplier');
    if(s && biSupplier) biSupplier.value = s.name;
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[data-bi-include]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.bulkImportRows[Number(el.getAttribute('data-bi-include'))].include = el.checked; });
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-bi-field]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('input', function(){
      const i = Number(el.getAttribute('data-bi-row')), f = el.getAttribute('data-bi-field');
      state.bulkImportRows[i][f] = el.value;
    });
  });

  const biImportBtn = document.getElementById('bi-import-btn');
  if(biImportBtn) biImportBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const toInsert = state.bulkImportRows.filter(function(r){ return r.include; }).map(function(r){
      return {
        dealer_id: state.profile.id, model: r.model, storage: r.storage, color: '',
        condition: state.bulkImportCondition, battery: state.bulkImportCondition==='Used' ? 100 : null,
        quantity: Number(r.quantity)||1, supplier: state.bulkImportSupplier || (r.sectionLabel||''),
        supplier_id: state.bulkImportSupplierId || null,
        purchase_date: todayISO(),
        cost: Number(r.price)||0, price: null, status: 'In Stock', shelf: '', notes: 'Bulk imported: '+r.raw
      };
    });
    if(!toInsert.length){ showToast('No rows selected to import', true); return; }
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').insert(toInsert);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      state.bulkImportRows = []; state.bulkImportText=''; state.bulkImportSupplierId='';
      closeModal(); showToast(toInsert.length+' phones imported');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Import failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  });

  ['calc-cost','calc-target','calc-min','calc-offer'].forEach(function(id){
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if(el) el.addEventListener('input', function(){
      state.calcInputs = { cost: val('calc-cost')||0, target: val('calc-target')||0, min: val('calc-min')||0, offer: val('calc-offer')||0 };
      render();
    });
  });

  window.addEventListener('hashchange', applyHashTab);
}

applyTheme();
init();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

supabase\functions\send-push\index.ts

// PhoneHub Pro — send-push Edge Function
//
// Receives a small JSON payload from a Postgres trigger (or the daily cron check)
// and delivers it as a real Web Push notification to every subscribed device for
// the relevant dealer(s). This is what makes the alert show up even if the
// Seller App isn't open.
//
// Deploy with:  supabase functions deploy send-push --no-verify-jwt
// (--no-verify-jwt because this is called by Postgres via pg_net, not a logged-in user)
//
// Required secrets (set with `supabase secrets set NAME=value`):
//   VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY       — same value pasted into seller/index.html
//   VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY      — keep this one secret, never put it in client code
//   VAPID_SUBJECT          — e.g. mailto:you@example.com
//   WEBHOOK_SECRET         — any random string; must match app_config.edge_function_secret
//   SUPABASE_URL / SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY — usually already present by default in Edge Functions

import webpush from "npm:web-push@3.6.7";
import { createClient } from "npm:@supabase/supabase-js@2";

const VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY = Deno.env.get("VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY") || "";
const VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY = Deno.env.get("VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY") || "";
const VAPID_SUBJECT = Deno.env.get("VAPID_SUBJECT") || "mailto:admin@example.com";
const WEBHOOK_SECRET = Deno.env.get("WEBHOOK_SECRET") || "";
const SUPABASE_URL = Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_URL")!;
const SERVICE_ROLE_KEY = Deno.env.get("SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY")!;

webpush.setVapidDetails(VAPID_SUBJECT, VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY, VAPID_PRIVATE_KEY);

const supabase = createClient(SUPABASE_URL, SERVICE_ROLE_KEY);

Deno.serve(async (req: Request) => {
  try {
    if (WEBHOOK_SECRET) {
      const got = req.headers.get("x-webhook-secret");
      if (got !== WEBHOOK_SECRET) {
        return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "unauthorized" }), { status: 401 });
      }
    }

    const payload = await req.json();
    const { type, dealer_id, exclude_dealer_id, title, body, url, tag } = payload || {};

    let query = supabase.from("push_subscriptions").select("*");
    if (dealer_id) query = query.eq("dealer_id", dealer_id);
    else if (exclude_dealer_id) query = query.neq("dealer_id", exclude_dealer_id);
    else {
      return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: "no dealer_id or exclude_dealer_id given" }), { status: 400 });
    }

    const { data: subs, error } = await query;
    if (error) return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: error.message }), { status: 500 });

    const notifPayload = JSON.stringify({
      title: title || "PhoneHub Pro",
      body: body || "",
      url: url || "./",
      type: type || "alert",
      tag: tag || undefined,
    });

    const results = await Promise.allSettled(
      (subs || []).map(async (s: any) => {
        try {
          await webpush.sendNotification(
            { endpoint: s.endpoint, keys: { p256dh: s.p256dh, auth: s.auth } },
            notifPayload
          );
        } catch (err: any) {
          // 404/410 means the browser/device unsubscribed or the subscription is stale — clean it up.
          if (err && (err.statusCode === 404 || err.statusCode === 410)) {
            await supabase.from("push_subscriptions").delete().eq("id", s.id);
          }
          throw err;
        }
      })
    );

    const sent = results.filter((r) => r.status === "fulfilled").length;
    const failed = results.length - sent;

    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ recipients: results.length, sent, failed }), {
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
    });
  } catch (e: any) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: e.message || String(e) }), { status: 500 });
  }
});

migration_optional_imei.sql

-- ============================================================
-- PhoneHub Pro — Migration: make IMEI optional
-- ============================================================
-- ONLY needed if you already ran an OLDER version of schema.sql that had
-- IMEI as NOT NULL. The schema.sql in this package already has IMEI as
-- optional and sell_phone() matching by inventory id — skip this file
-- entirely on a fresh project.
--
-- Run this once in Supabase: Dashboard > SQL Editor > New query > paste > Run.
-- Safe to re-run.
-- ============================================================

-- 1. Allow phones/sales to be saved without an IMEI (e.g. accessories,
--    or stock not yet logged with its IMEI).
alter table inventory alter column imei drop not null;
alter table sales alter column imei drop not null;

-- 2. Replace sell_phone() to match by the phone's internal id instead of
--    its IMEI. This avoids ambiguity now that IMEI can be blank (multiple
--    IMEI-less phones would otherwise be indistinguishable when selling).
drop function if exists sell_phone(text,numeric,text,text,text,text,int,text,text);

create or replace function sell_phone(
  p_inventory_id uuid, p_sale_price numeric, p_customer_name text, p_customer_phone text,
  p_payment_method text, p_staff text, p_warranty_days int, p_accessories text, p_notes text
)
returns sales
language plpgsql
as $$
declare
  v_phone inventory%rowtype;
  v_sale sales%rowtype;
begin
  select * into v_phone from inventory
    where id = p_inventory_id and dealer_id = auth.uid() and status = 'In Stock'
    limit 1;

  if v_phone.id is null then
    raise exception 'No in-stock phone found for that selection';
  end if;

  insert into sales (dealer_id, imei, model, cost, sale_price, customer_name, customer_phone,
                      payment_method, staff, warranty_days, accessories, notes)
  values (auth.uid(), v_phone.imei, v_phone.model, v_phone.cost, p_sale_price, p_customer_name, p_customer_phone,
          p_payment_method, p_staff, p_warranty_days, p_accessories, p_notes)
  returning * into v_sale;

  update inventory set status = 'Sold', updated_at = now() where id = v_phone.id;

  return v_sale;
end;
$$;
grant execute on function sell_phone(uuid,numeric,text,text,text,text,int,text,text) to authenticated;

phonehubfile.txt

combine_files.py

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Combines all files in a folder and its subfolders into a single unified .txt file.

Usage:
    python combine_files.py /path/to/your/project/folder
    python combine_files.py /path/to/your/project/folder -o output.txt

Edit EXTENSIONS below if you have other file types to include.
"""

import argparse
import os

# Which file extensions to include. Add/remove as needed.
EXTENSIONS = {".gs", ".html", ".js", ".json", ".sql", ".css", ".md", ".txt", ".ts", ".py"}


# Never walk into these - huge, binary-heavy, or not yours to index.
# This is what caused venv/site-packages to end up in a combined dump before.
EXCLUDE_DIRS = {"node_modules", ".git", "venv", ".venv", "env", "__pycache__",
                 "dist", "build", ".next", "chroma_db", "site-packages",
                 "target", "bin", "obj", "vendor", ".idea", ".vscode"}

SEPARATOR = "=" * 150


def combine_files(folder, output_path, subfolders=True):
    # Collect matching files.
    files = []
    if subfolders:
        for root, dirs, filenames in os.walk(folder):
            dirs[:] = [d for d in dirs if d not in EXCLUDE_DIRS and not d.startswith(".")]
            for filename in filenames:
                if os.path.splitext(filename)[1].lower() in EXTENSIONS:
                    relative_path = os.path.relpath(os.path.join(root, filename), folder)
                    files.append(relative_path)
    else:
        for filename in os.listdir(folder):
            filepath = os.path.join(folder, filename)
            if os.path.isfile(filepath) and os.path.splitext(filename)[1].lower() in EXTENSIONS:
                files.append(filename)

    if not files:
        print(f"No matching files found in {folder} (looking for {EXTENSIONS})")
        return

    # Put Code.gs first if present, then alphabetical for the rest.
    def sort_key(filepath):
        name = os.path.basename(filepath)
        return (0, "") if name.lower() == "code.gs" else (1, name.lower())

    files.sort(key=sort_key)

    with open(output_path, "w", encoding="utf-8") as out:
        for i, filename in enumerate(files):
            filepath = os.path.join(folder, filename)
            with open(filepath, "r", encoding="utf-8", errors="replace") as f: # filename is now a relative path
                content = f.read()

            out.write(f"{filename}\n\n")
            out.write(content.strip())
            out.write("\n\n")

            if i < len(files) - 1:
                out.write(f"{SEPARATOR}\n\n")

    print(f"Combined {len(files)} files into: {output_path}")
    for f in files:
        print(f"  - {f}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Combine project files into one txt file.")
    parser.add_argument("folder", help="Path to the folder containing your files")
    parser.add_argument("-o", "--output", default="combined_project.txt", help="Output file path")
    parser.add_argument("--subfolders", action="store_true", default=True, help="Include files in subfolders (default)")
    parser.add_argument("--no-subfolders", action="store_false", dest="subfolders", help="Exclude files in subfolders")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    combine_files(args.folder, args.output, subfolders=args.subfolders)

i need automation ideas and business improvement solutions for a phone sales business, in computer village ikeja, lagos nigeria, a very busy electronic gadget market. The business gets some phones from overseas, some from local vendors and some from colleagues, at times, when a customer comes into the store for a phone that isnt available, the owner can quickly reach out to a friend who has it, get it at first owners price, add his own profit and sell to the customer. friends and colleagues also get phone from him to sell

Why this is a strong opportunity

The business model you've described is common across many stores in Computer Village, Ikeja. Most traders still rely on phone calls, WhatsApp chats, notebooks, and memory to coordinate inventory and supplier networks. A lightweight system built with Google Sheets, Google Apps Script, AppSheet, Forms, and WhatsApp integrations, with a PHP/MySQL backend added later if needed, could solve real operational problems without requiring expensive software.

Such a platform could start with a single shop and later be adapted into a multi-store solution where trusted dealers share inventory securely while keeping their own business records private. That makes it both a practical automation project and a potential commercial product for one of Nigeria's busiest electronics markets.

"Yes, we can get it for you."

That single difference turns missed opportunities into completed sales and gives your business a significant competitive advantage.

I would also rename the entire project to something stronger than "Smart Phone Store Management System." Something like:

PhoneHub Pro (my favorite)
DealerLink
SmartDealer Network
PhoneConnect
PhoneTrade Pro
CV Connect (Computer Village Connect)
DealerSync
Phone Market OS
PhoneFlow
PhoneXchange

These names immediately emphasize that this isn't just inventory software—it's a network-powered sales platform, which is the feature most likely to make your client say, "I need this."

this is good, plus it eliminates the eliminates the issue of having to look for whatsapp contacts and group when whatsapp bans their account which happens very often due to broadcast message sending.





for IMEI tracking, is it possible to build an actual tracker that tracks the phone current location, in case of theft, also a means of registering the new user once they input their details on the phone in case of user to user sales

Short answer: not in the way most people imagine.

An independent phone store cannot build a system that tracks the live location of any phone by IMEI alone. That capability belongs to mobile network operators, phone manufacturers, and law enforcement through legal processes.

However, you can build something that provides significant business value and theft protection without making unrealistic claims.

Here's what is realistically possible.

Option 1: IMEI Registration & Ownership Database ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ (Highly Recommended)

Every phone sold is registered in your database with:

IMEI 1 & IMEI 2
Serial Number
Phone Model
Purchase Date
Warranty
Original Buyer
Receipt
Photos
Accessories
Payment Method

If someone walks into your shop with that phone months later, simply search the IMEI.

You'll instantly know:

Was it sold by you?
Who bought it?
Warranty status
Purchase history
Trade-in history
Repair history

This alone is extremely valuable.

Option 2: Digital Ownership Transfer ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

This is something most phone stores don't offer.

Imagine this scenario.

John buys an iPhone today.

A year later he sells it to Mary.

Instead of the phone permanently belonging to John in your records...

Mary scans a QR Code or visits your web portal.

She enters:

Name
Phone Number
Email
Receipt Number (optional)
OTP verification

Ownership is transferred.

Now your system shows

Current Owner:

Mary Johnson

Previous Owner:

John Doe

Transfer Date:

15 June 2027

You now have a complete ownership chain.

This is excellent for:

Warranty
Trade-ins
Resale trust
Stolen phone verification
Option 3: Theft Reporting System ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Customer reports

"My phone was stolen."

You click

Mark as Stolen.

Now if that IMEI ever appears in your:

Repair department
Trade-in desk
Buy-back service

The system immediately alerts staff.

This alone can recover many phones.

Option 4: Shared Blacklist Network ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

This is huge.

Imagine 200 phone shops using your software.

Once a phone is reported stolen...

Every participating shop receives the IMEI blacklist.

If the thief tries to:

Sell it

Trade it

Repair it

Unlock it

Any participating dealer immediately sees

⚠️ Reported Stolen

Original Owner

Report Date

Police Case Number (optional)

This could become the "Computer Village Anti-Theft Network."

That alone would be a massive selling point.

Option 5: Find My Phone Integration ⭐⭐⭐⭐☆

Instead of pretending you can locate the phone...

Your system stores links to:

Android

Find My Device

Apple

Find My

Samsung SmartThings Find

When customer reports theft

One click opens the official tracking service.

Professional.

Legal.

Reliable.

Option 6: Customer Registration App ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

When customer buys a phone

They receive

QR Code

Scan it.

Complete registration.

Now your database has

Current owner

Address

Email

Phone

Emergency contact

Purchase receipt

Warranty

Trade-in history

Repair history

Future transfers become easy.

Option 7: Device Check-In Verification ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐

Whenever someone wants to

Sell

Trade

Repair

Unlock

their phone

Staff scan IMEI.

System checks

✓ Stolen?

✓ Original owner?

✓ Warranty?

✓ Outstanding finance?

✓ Previous repairs?

Great fraud prevention.

About Live GPS Tracking

This is where many people misunderstand what IMEI can do.

You CANNOT
Track live GPS using IMEI.
See a phone's current location from your own software.
Turn on GPS remotely.
Access mobile network location data.
Locate a phone after the SIM card is changed.

Those capabilities require access to carrier infrastructure or the phone manufacturer's ecosystem.

What is possible with a companion app (if the customer opts in)

If you develop a companion Android application and the customer voluntarily installs it and grants the required permissions, you can offer features such as:

Sharing the phone's last known location with the owner.
Sending an alert if the SIM card is changed.
Recording the new SIM number (where platform permissions allow).
Detecting factory reset attempts (with limitations).
Periodically syncing location when the phone is online.
Displaying a message on the lock screen with contact information.

This would be an opt-in security service, not IMEI tracking.

Note: On iPhones, Apple imposes much stricter restrictions, so a third-party app cannot provide the same level of device monitoring.

A feature that could truly differentiate your platform

If your long-term goal is to build a product for Computer Village rather than just one shop, I'd position it as:

PhoneHub Secure™ – Dealer Anti-Theft Network

When a phone is sold:

Register its IMEI and ownership.
Generate a digital ownership certificate.
Allow ownership transfers through the platform.
Let owners report devices as stolen.
Instantly share stolen IMEI alerts with participating dealers.
Flag stolen devices during sales, repairs, or trade-ins.
Maintain a complete ownership history for every device.

This is a realistic, legally compliant feature that creates real value. As more dealers join the network, the platform becomes increasingly effective at discouraging the resale of stolen phones while giving legitimate buyers and sellers greater confidence.

<div id="app"><div class="loading-screen"><div class="spinner"></div>Setting up the shop…</div></div>

<script>
(function(){
const CONFIG_KEY = 'phonehub-supabase-config';
const MY_SHOP_KEY = 'phonehub-my-shop';
// If you've deployed this app for real, paste your Supabase project URL and anon key here.
// Doing so skips the "Connect" screen entirely for every customer who opens this app.
const HARDCODED_SUPABASE_URL = 'https://qqlykvrofoobowrsarxi.supabase.co';
const HARDCODED_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY = 'eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6InFxbHlrdnJvZm9vYm93cnNhcnhpIiwicm9sZSI6ImFub24iLCJpYXQiOjE3ODQwMDc0MzcsImV4cCI6MjA5OTU4MzQzN30.3G0yVZbfkoBexdWj_YM9lqC-u4SSQxVgQOxgN-RruAc';
let sb = null;

let state = {
  stage:'loading', // loading -> configure -> pickShop -> shop
  configError:null, configuring:false, urlInput:'', keyInput:'',
  shops:[], selectedShop:null,
  tab:'shop', inventory:[], q:'', condFilter:'All', maxPrice:'', categoryFilter:'All', modal:null, toast:null, toastErr:false,
  lookupPhone:'', lookupDone:false, lookupResults:[]
};

function naira(n){ n = Number(n)||0; return '₦'+n.toLocaleString('en-NG',{maximumFractionDigits:0}); }
function todayISO(){ return new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10); }
function daysBetween(a,b){ return Math.round((new Date(b)-new Date(a))/86400000); }
function escapeHtml(s){ return (s==null?'':String(s)).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function escapeAttr(s){ return (s||'').toString().replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }
function val(id){ const el=document.getElementById(id); return el?el.value:''; }

function loadConfig(){
  if(HARDCODED_SUPABASE_URL && HARDCODED_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY){
    return { url: HARDCODED_SUPABASE_URL, key: HARDCODED_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY };
  }
  try{ const raw = localStorage.getItem(CONFIG_KEY); return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null; }
  catch(e){ return null; }
}
function saveConfig(url,key){
  try{ localStorage.setItem(CONFIG_KEY, JSON.stringify({url:url,key:key})); } catch(e){ /* ignore */ }
}
function loadMyShop(){
  try{ const raw = localStorage.getItem(MY_SHOP_KEY); return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null; }
  catch(e){ return null; }
}
function saveMyShop(shop){
  try{ localStorage.setItem(MY_SHOP_KEY, JSON.stringify(shop)); } catch(e){ /* ignore */ }
}

async function init(){
  const cfg = await loadConfig();
  if(!cfg){ state.stage='configure'; render(); return; }
  await connectSupabase(cfg.url, cfg.key, false);
}

async function connectSupabase(url, key, persist){
  try{
    sb = window.supabase.createClient(url, key);
    const { error: pingErr } = await sb.from('public_shops').select('id').limit(1);
    if(pingErr) throw pingErr;
    if(persist) await saveConfig(url, key);
    const myShop = await loadMyShop();
    if(myShop){ state.selectedShop = myShop; await loadShopCatalog(); }
    else { await loadShopPicker(); }
  } catch(e){
    state.stage = 'configure'; state.configError = e.message || String(e); render();
  }
}

async function loadShopPicker(){
  try{
    const { data, error } = await sb.from('public_shops').select('*').order('shop_name');
    if(error) throw error;
    state.shops = data || [];
    state.stage = 'pickShop';
  } catch(e){
    state.stage = 'configure'; state.configError = e.message || String(e);
  }
  render();
}

async function loadShopCatalog(){
  state.stage = 'loading'; render();
  try{
    const { data, error } = await sb.from('public_catalog').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.selectedShop.id);
    if(error) throw error;
    state.inventory = data || [];
    state.stage = 'shop';
  } catch(e){
    state.stage = 'configure'; state.configError = e.message || String(e);
  }
  render();
}

function showToast(msg, err){ state.toast = msg; state.toastErr = !!err; render(); setTimeout(function(){ state.toast=null; render(); }, 3000); }
function setTab(t){ state.tab = t; state.modal=null; render(); }
function openModal(name, payload){ state.modal={name:name, payload:payload||{}}; render(); }
function closeModal(){ state.modal=null; render(); }

function catalog(){
  return state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return p.status==='In Stock'; }).filter(function(p){
    if(state.categoryFilter!=='All' && (p.item_type||'Phone')!==state.categoryFilter) return false;
    if(state.q){
      const q = state.q.toLowerCase();
      const hay = [p.model,p.color,p.brand,p.cpu].filter(Boolean).join(' ').toLowerCase();
      if(!hay.includes(q)) return false;
    }
    if(state.condFilter!=='All' && p.condition!==state.condFilter) return false;
    if(state.maxPrice && Number(p.price) > Number(state.maxPrice)) return false;
    return true;
  }).sort(function(a,b){ return (a.price||0)-(b.price||0); });
}

function render(){
  const app = document.getElementById('app');
  if(state.stage==='loading'){ app.innerHTML='<div class="loading-screen"><div class="spinner"></div>Setting up the shop…</div>'; return; }
  if(state.stage==='configure'){ app.innerHTML = renderConfigureScreen(); attachConfigureHandlers(); return; }
  if(state.stage==='pickShop'){ app.innerHTML = renderShopPicker(); attachShopPickerHandlers(); return; }

  app.innerHTML =
    '<div class="topbar"><div class="brand"><div class="mark">PH</div>PhoneHub</div>' +
      '<div class="shop-pill" id="switchShopBtn">'+escapeHtml(state.selectedShop.shop_name)+' · switch shop</div>' +
      '<div class="nav-tabs">' + navTab('shop','Shop') + navTab('request','Request a phone') + navTab('lookup','My purchases') + '</div>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="wrap">'+renderTab()+'</div>' +
    (state.modal ? renderModal() : '') +
    (state.toast ? ('<div class="toast '+(state.toastErr?'err':'')+'">'+escapeHtml(state.toast)+'</div>') : '');
  attachHandlers();
}

function renderConfigureScreen(){
  return '<div class="connect-wrap"><div class="connect-card">' +
    '<h2>Connect this app to Supabase</h2>' +
    '<p>Paste the same Supabase project URL and anon key used in the Seller App.</p>' +
    (state.configError ? ('<div class="connect-status err">'+escapeHtml(state.configError)+'</div>') : '') +
    '<input id="cfgUrl" placeholder="https://xxxxx.supabase.co" value="'+escapeAttr(state.urlInput)+'"/>' +
    '<input id="cfgKey" placeholder="anon public key (eyJ...)" value="'+escapeAttr(state.keyInput)+'"/>' +
    '<button class="btn btn-primary btn-block" id="cfgConnectBtn" '+(state.configuring?'disabled':'')+'>'+(state.configuring?'Connecting…':'Connect')+'</button>' +
  '</div></div>';
}
function attachConfigureHandlers(){
  const u = document.getElementById('cfgUrl'), k = document.getElementById('cfgKey');
  if(u) u.addEventListener('input', function(e){ state.urlInput = e.target.value; });
  if(k) k.addEventListener('input', function(e){ state.keyInput = e.target.value; });
  const btn = document.getElementById('cfgConnectBtn');
  if(btn) btn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const url = (document.getElementById('cfgUrl').value||'').trim();
    const key = (document.getElementById('cfgKey').value||'').trim();
    if(!url || !key){ state.configError='Please fill in both fields.'; render(); return; }
    state.configuring = true; state.configError=null; render();
    await connectSupabase(url, key, true);
    state.configuring = false;
  });
}

function renderShopPicker(){
  return '<div class="wrap"><div class="hero"><h1>Choose a shop</h1><p>Pick the phone shop you want to browse.</p></div>' +
    '<div class="shop-list">' +
      state.shops.map(function(s){ return '<div class="shop-item" data-pick-shop="'+s.id+'">' +
        '<div><div class="name">'+escapeHtml(s.shop_name)+'</div><div class="loc">'+escapeHtml(s.location||'')+'</div></div>' +
        '<div style="color:var(--accent);font-size:18px;">→</div></div>'; }).join('') +
    '</div>' +
    (!state.shops.length ? '<div class="empty"><div class="big">No shops registered yet</div>Check back soon.</div>' : '') +
  '</div>';
}
function attachShopPickerHandlers(){
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-pick-shop]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
      const id = el.getAttribute('data-pick-shop');
      const shop = state.shops.find(function(s){ return s.id===id; });
      state.selectedShop = shop;
      await saveMyShop(shop);
      await loadShopCatalog();
    });
  });
}

function navTab(key,label){ return '<div class="nav-tab '+(state.tab===key?'active':'')+'" data-tab="'+key+'">'+label+'</div>'; }

function renderTab(){
  if(state.tab==='shop') return renderShop();
  if(state.tab==='request') return renderRequestForm();
  if(state.tab==='lookup') return renderLookup();
  return '';
}

function renderShop(){
  const items = catalog();
  const catCounts = { All: state.inventory.filter(function(p){return p.status==='In Stock';}).length,
    Phone: state.inventory.filter(function(p){return p.status==='In Stock' && (p.item_type||'Phone')==='Phone';}).length,
    Laptop: state.inventory.filter(function(p){return p.status==='In Stock' && p.item_type==='Laptop';}).length };
  return '<div class="hero"><h1>Find your next phone or laptop</h1><p>Everything below is verified and in stock at '+escapeHtml(state.selectedShop.shop_name)+' right now.</p></div>' +
    '<div class="filter-row" style="margin-bottom:10px;">' +
      ['All','Phone','Laptop'].map(function(c){ return '<span class="nav-tab '+(state.categoryFilter===c?'active':'')+'" data-category-filter="'+c+'" style="cursor:pointer;">'+(c==='All'?'All':(c==='Phone'?'📱 Phones':'💻 Laptops'))+' ('+catCounts[c]+')</span>'; }).join('') +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="filter-row">' +
      '<input id="q" placeholder="Search model, brand, or color…" value="'+escapeHtml(state.q)+'"/>' +
      '<select id="cond"><option '+(state.condFilter==='All'?'selected':'')+'>All</option><option '+(state.condFilter==='New'?'selected':'')+'>New</option><option '+(state.condFilter==='Used'?'selected':'')+'>Used</option></select>' +
      '<input id="maxPrice" type="number" placeholder="Max budget (₦)" value="'+escapeHtml(state.maxPrice)+'"/>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="grid">' + items.map(function(p){
      const isLaptop = (p.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
      const spec = isLaptop ? [p.cpu,p.ram,p.storage].filter(Boolean).join(' · ') : [p.storage,p.color].filter(Boolean).join(' · ');
      return '<div class="tag-card" data-view-phone="'+p.id+'">' +
        (p.image_url ? ('<img class="tag-photo" src="'+escapeAttr(p.image_url)+'" loading="lazy" alt="'+escapeAttr(p.model)+'"/>') : '') +
        '<span class="tag-condition '+(p.condition==='New'?'new':'used')+'">'+escapeHtml(p.condition)+'</span>' +
        '<div class="tag-model">'+(isLaptop && p.brand ? escapeHtml(p.brand)+' ' : '')+escapeHtml(p.model)+'</div>' +
        '<div class="tag-spec">'+escapeHtml(spec)+'</div>' +
        '<div class="tag-price">'+naira(p.price)+'</div>' +
        (p.condition==='Used' && p.battery!=null ? ('<div class="tag-battery">Battery health '+p.battery+'%</div>') : '') +
      '</div>';
    }).join('') + '</div>' +
    (!items.length ? ('<div class="empty"><div class="big">Nothing matches right now</div>Try a wider budget, or tell us what you\'re looking for.<br/><br/>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-primary" data-tab="request">Request a phone</button></div>') : '');
}

function renderModal(){
  const p = state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id===state.modal.payload.id; });
  if(!p) return '';
  const isLaptop = (p.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="sheet" data-stop="1">' +
    '<button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button>' +
    (p.image_url ? ('<img class="sheet-photo" src="'+escapeAttr(p.image_url)+'" alt="'+escapeAttr(p.model)+'"/>') : '') +
    '<span class="tag-condition '+(p.condition==='New'?'new':'used')+'">'+escapeHtml(p.condition)+'</span>' +
    '<h2>'+(isLaptop && p.brand ? escapeHtml(p.brand)+' ' : '')+escapeHtml(p.model)+'</h2>' +
    '<div class="price-big">'+naira(p.price)+'</div>' +
    (isLaptop ? (
      '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Processor</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.cpu||'—')+'</span></div>' +
      '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">RAM</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.ram||'—')+'</span></div>' +
      '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Storage</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.storage||'—')+'</span></div>' +
      '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Screen</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.screen_size||'—')+'</span></div>' +
      (p.gpu ? ('<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Graphics</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.gpu)+'</span></div>') : '')
    ) : (
      '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Storage</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.storage)+'</span></div>'
    )) +
    '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Color</span><span class="v">'+escapeHtml(p.color)+'</span></div>' +
    (p.condition==='Used' && p.battery!=null ? ('<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Battery health</span><span class="v">'+p.battery+'%</span></div>') : '') +
    '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Warranty</span><span class="v">Included on purchase</span></div>' +
    '<div class="detail-row"><span class="k">Availability</span><span class="v" style="color:var(--success)">In stock now</span></div>' +
    '<button class="btn btn-primary btn-block" style="margin-top:18px;" data-tab="request" data-close-modal="1">Ask about this '+(isLaptop?'laptop':'phone')+'</button>' +
  '</div></div>';
}

function renderRequestForm(){
  return '<div class="hero"><h1>Can\'t find it?</h1><p>Tell '+escapeHtml(state.selectedShop.shop_name)+' what you want — they\'ll reach out the moment it\'s available, sometimes from their trusted dealer network.</p></div>' +
    '<div class="form-card">' +
      '<div class="two-col"><div class="field"><label>Your name</label><input id="r-name"/></div><div class="field"><label>Phone number</label><input id="r-phone"/></div></div>' +
      '<div class="two-col"><div class="field"><label>Phone or laptop model</label><input id="r-model" placeholder="e.g. Google Pixel 9, or HP EliteBook 840"/></div><div class="field"><label>Storage / color / spec (optional)</label><input id="r-variant" placeholder="256GB, Black, 16GB RAM…"/></div></div>' +
      '<div class="field"><label>Your budget (₦, optional)</label><input type="number" id="r-budget"/></div>' +
      '<div class="field"><label>Anything else?</label><textarea id="r-notes" rows="2"></textarea></div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-primary btn-block" id="submitRequestBtn">Send request</button>' +
    '</div>';
}

function renderLookup(){
  return '<div class="hero"><h1>My purchases</h1><p>Enter the phone number you bought with to see your purchase history and warranty status — across any shop on PhoneHub.</p></div>' +
    '<div class="form-card">' +
      '<div class="field"><label>Phone number</label><input id="lk-phone" placeholder="0803 123 4567" value="'+escapeHtml(state.lookupPhone)+'"/></div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-primary btn-block" id="lookupBtn">Check my purchases</button>' +
    '</div>' +
    (state.lookupDone ? ('<div class="lookup-result">' +
      (state.lookupResults.length ? state.lookupResults.map(function(s){
        const expiry = new Date(s.date); expiry.setDate(expiry.getDate()+Number(s.warranty_days||0));
        const daysLeft = daysBetween(todayISO(), expiry.toISOString().slice(0,10));
        const cls = !s.warranty_days ? '' : daysLeft<0 ? 'expired' : daysLeft<=7 ? 'soon' : 'active';
        const label = !s.warranty_days ? 'No warranty on file' : daysLeft<0 ? 'Warranty expired' : daysLeft<=7 ? ('Warranty ends in '+daysLeft+' day'+(daysLeft===1?'':'s')) : ('Warranty active — '+daysLeft+' days left');
        return '<div class="lookup-item"><div class="m">'+escapeHtml(s.model)+'</div>' +
          '<div style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:13px;">Bought at '+escapeHtml(s.shop_name)+' · '+escapeHtml(s.date)+' · '+naira(s.sale_price)+'</div>' +
          '<span class="warranty-pill '+cls+'">'+label+'</span></div>';
      }).join('') : '<div class="empty"><div class="big">No purchases found</div>Double-check the phone number used at checkout.</div>') +
    '</div>') : '');
}

function attachHandlers(){
  const app = document.getElementById('app');
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-tab]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ setTab(el.getAttribute('data-tab')); }); });
  const switchBtn = document.getElementById('switchShopBtn');
  if(switchBtn) switchBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    try{ localStorage.removeItem(MY_SHOP_KEY); } catch(e){ /* ignore */ }
    state.selectedShop = null; await loadShopPicker();
  });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal('view',{id:el.getAttribute('data-view-phone')}); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-category-filter]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.categoryFilter = el.getAttribute('data-category-filter'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-modal]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', closeModal); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-overlay]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', closeModal); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-stop]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); }); });

  const q = document.getElementById('q');
  if(q) q.addEventListener('input', function(e){ state.q=e.target.value; render(); focusEnd('q'); });
  const cond = document.getElementById('cond');
  if(cond) cond.addEventListener('change', function(e){ state.condFilter=e.target.value; render(); });
  const maxPrice = document.getElementById('maxPrice');
  if(maxPrice) maxPrice.addEventListener('input', function(e){ state.maxPrice=e.target.value; render(); focusEnd('maxPrice'); });

  const lkBtn = document.getElementById('lookupBtn');
  if(lkBtn) lkBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const phone = val('lk-phone');
    state.lookupPhone = phone;
    try{
      const { data, error } = await sb.rpc('lookup_my_purchases', { p_phone: phone });
      if(error) throw error;
      state.lookupResults = data || [];
    } catch(e){ state.lookupResults = []; showToast('Could not look up purchases: '+e.message, true); }
    state.lookupDone = true; render();
  });

  const reqBtn = document.getElementById('submitRequestBtn');
  if(reqBtn) reqBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const name = val('r-name'), phone = val('r-phone'), model = val('r-model');
    if(!name || !phone || !model){ showToast('Please fill in your name, phone, and the model you want', true); return; }
    const data = { dealer_id: state.selectedShop.id, customer_name:name, customer_phone:phone, model:model, storage:val('r-variant'), budget:val('r-budget')||null, status:'Pending', notes:val('r-notes') };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('requests').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      showToast('Request sent — we will reach out as soon as it is available');
      state.tab = 'request'; render();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Could not send request: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  });
}
function focusEnd(id){ const el=document.getElementById(id); if(el){ el.focus(); const v=el.value; el.value=''; el.value=v; } }

init();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

const CONFIG_KEY = 'phonehub-supabase-config';

const THEME_KEY = 'phonehub-theme';
function loadTheme(){
  try{ return localStorage.getItem(THEME_KEY) || 'dark'; } catch(e){ return 'dark'; }
}
function saveTheme(t){
  try{ localStorage.setItem(THEME_KEY, t); } catch(e){ /* ignore */ }
}
function effectiveTheme(t){
  if(t==='system') return (window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').matches) ? 'light' : 'dark';
  return t;
}
function applyTheme(){
  const eff = effectiveTheme(state.theme);
  document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', eff);
  const metaTheme = document.querySelector('meta[name="theme-color"]');
  if(metaTheme) metaTheme.setAttribute('content', eff==='light' ? '#F3F4F7' : '#10141C');
}
function setTheme(t){ state.theme = t; saveTheme(t); applyTheme(); render(); }
if(window.matchMedia){
  window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: light)').addEventListener('change', function(){
    if(state.theme==='system') applyTheme();
  });
}

function uid(){ return Date.now().toString(36)+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,7); }
function shuffleArray(arr){
  const a = arr.slice();
  for(let i=a.length-1;i>0;i--){ const j = Math.floor(Math.random()*(i+1)); const t=a[i]; a[i]=a[j]; a[j]=t; }
  return a;
}
// Keeps the network browse order stable across refreshes (so "Load more" doesn't
// jump around), while any newly-listed phones get slotted in at random.
function syncNetworkOrder(){
  const liveIds = {}; state.dealerNetwork.forEach(function(d){ liveIds[d.id] = true; });
  const kept = state.networkOrder.filter(function(id){ return liveIds[id]; });
  const keptSet = {}; kept.forEach(function(id){ keptSet[id] = true; });
  const freshIds = state.dealerNetwork.map(function(d){ return d.id; }).filter(function(id){ return !keptSet[id]; });
  state.networkOrder = kept.concat(shuffleArray(freshIds));
}
function naira(n){ n = Number(n)||0; return '₦'+n.toLocaleString('en-NG',{maximumFractionDigits:0}); }
// Short display label for an inventory row, whether it's a phone or a laptop —
// used anywhere a compact "which item is this" line is needed (sale picker,
// consignment picker, global search results).
function itemLabel(p){
  if((p.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop'){
    return [p.brand, p.model].filter(Boolean).join(' ') + (p.cpu ? (' · '+p.cpu) : '') + (p.ram ? (' · '+p.ram) : '') + (p.storage ? (' · '+p.storage) : '');
  }
  return [p.model, p.storage, p.color].filter(Boolean).join(' · ');
}
function todayISO(){ return new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10); }
function daysBetween(a,b){ return Math.round((new Date(b)-new Date(a))/86400000); }
function escapeAttr(s){ return (s||'').toString().replace(/"/g,'&quot;'); }
function escapeHtml(s){ return (s==null?'':String(s)).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;'); }
function val(id){ const el = document.getElementById(id); return el ? el.value : ''; }
function slugify(s){ return (s||'').toLowerCase().trim().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g,'-').replace(/(^-|-$)/g,''); }

/* ---------- phone photos ---------- */
function thumbHTML(url){
  if(url) return '<img class="thumb" src="'+escapeAttr(url)+'" loading="lazy" alt=""/>';
  return '<div class="thumb-placeholder">'+ICONS.inventory+'</div>';
}
// Returns the ordered list of image URLs for a phone/network-item/stock-item
// record, falling back to the legacy single image_url when image_urls is empty.
function imagesFor(obj){
  if(!obj) return [];
  if(Array.isArray(obj.image_urls) && obj.image_urls.length) return obj.image_urls;
  if(obj.image_url) return [obj.image_url];
  return [];
}
// Renders a swipeable/clickable image gallery for use inside view-detail modals.
// `images` is an ordered array of URLs; `idx` is the currently shown slide.
function renderImageGallery(images, idx){
  if(!images || !images.length){
    return '<div class="thumb-placeholder" style="width:100%;height:200px;border-radius:10px;margin-bottom:16px;">'+ICONS.inventory+'</div>';
  }
  idx = Math.max(0, Math.min(idx||0, images.length-1));
  return '<div id="galleryWrap" data-gallery-total="'+images.length+'" style="position:relative;margin-bottom:16px;">' +
    '<img src="'+escapeAttr(images[idx])+'" style="width:100%;max-height:320px;object-fit:cover;border-radius:10px;display:block;"/>' +
    (images.length>1 ? (
      '<button type="button" data-gallery-prev="1" data-gallery-total="'+images.length+'" aria-label="Previous photo" style="position:absolute;left:8px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);background:rgba(0,0,0,.55);color:#fff;border:none;border-radius:50%;width:32px;height:32px;cursor:pointer;font-size:16px;">‹</button>' +
      '<button type="button" data-gallery-next="1" data-gallery-total="'+images.length+'" aria-label="Next photo" style="position:absolute;right:8px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);background:rgba(0,0,0,.55);color:#fff;border:none;border-radius:50%;width:32px;height:32px;cursor:pointer;font-size:16px;">›</button>' +
      '<div style="position:absolute;bottom:8px;left:0;right:0;text-align:center;display:flex;justify-content:center;gap:5px;">' +
        images.map(function(_,i){ return '<span style="width:6px;height:6px;border-radius:50%;background:'+(i===idx?'#fff':'rgba(255,255,255,.45)')+';display:inline-block;"></span>'; }).join('') +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="position:absolute;top:8px;right:8px;background:rgba(0,0,0,.55);color:#fff;font-size:11px;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:10px;">'+(idx+1)+' / '+images.length+'</div>'
    ) : '') +
  '</div>';
}
// Shrinks a photo client-side before upload — most Computer Village connections
// are slow/data-capped, so a 12MB camera photo becomes a ~150-200KB JPEG here.
function resizeImageFile(file, maxDim, quality){
  maxDim = maxDim || 1000; quality = quality || 0.8;
  return new Promise(function(resolve, reject){
    const img = new Image();
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onerror = function(){ reject(new Error('Could not read that file')); };
    reader.onload = function(){
      img.onerror = function(){ reject(new Error('Could not read that image')); };
      img.onload = function(){
        let w = img.width, h = img.height;
        if(w > h && w > maxDim){ h = Math.round(h*(maxDim/w)); w = maxDim; }
        else if(h > maxDim){ w = Math.round(w*(maxDim/h)); h = maxDim; }
        const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
        canvas.width = w; canvas.height = h;
        canvas.getContext('2d').drawImage(img, 0, 0, w, h);
        canvas.toBlob(function(blob){
          if(!blob){ reject(new Error('Could not process that image')); return; }
          resolve(blob);
        }, 'image/jpeg', quality);
      };
      img.src = reader.result;
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  });
}
async function uploadPhoneImage(file){
  const blob = await resizeImageFile(file, 1000, 0.8);
  const path = state.profile.id + '/' + Date.now().toString(36) + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,7) + '.jpg';
  const { error } = await sb.storage.from('phone-images').upload(path, blob, { contentType:'image/jpeg', upsert:false });
  if(error) throw error;
  const { data } = sb.storage.from('phone-images').getPublicUrl(path);
  return data.publicUrl;
}

/* ---------- invoice / warranty card PDF ---------- */
function invoiceNumberFor(sale){
  const raw = sale && sale.id ? String(sale.id) : Date.now().toString(36);
  return 'INV-' + raw.replace(/-/g,'').slice(0,8).toUpperCase();
}
function generateInvoicePDF(sale){
  if(!window.jspdf || !window.jspdf.jsPDF){ showToast('PDF library still loading — try again in a moment', true); return; }
  const { jsPDF } = window.jspdf;
  const doc = new jsPDF({ unit:'pt', format:'a4' });
  const shop = state.profile || {};
  const left = 40, right = 555;
  let y = 54;

  doc.setFont('helvetica','bold'); doc.setFontSize(20); doc.setTextColor(30);
  doc.text(shop.shop_name || 'PhoneHub Pro', left, y);
  doc.setFont('helvetica','normal'); doc.setFontSize(10); doc.setTextColor(90);
  y += 18;
  if(shop.location){ doc.text(shop.location, left, y); y += 13; }
  if(shop.phone){ doc.text('Tel: '+shop.phone, left, y); y += 13; }

  doc.setTextColor(30);
  doc.setFont('helvetica','bold'); doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text('INVOICE', right, 54, {align:'right'});
  doc.setFont('helvetica','normal'); doc.setFontSize(10); doc.setTextColor(90);
  doc.text(invoiceNumberFor(sale), right, 70, {align:'right'});
  doc.text('Date: '+(sale.date || todayISO()), right, 84, {align:'right'});

  y = Math.max(y, 90) + 14;
  doc.setDrawColor(210); doc.line(left, y, right, y); y += 26;

  doc.setFont('helvetica','bold'); doc.setFontSize(11); doc.setTextColor(30);
  doc.text('Sold to', left, y); y += 15;
  doc.setFont('helvetica','normal'); doc.setFontSize(10); doc.setTextColor(70);
  doc.text('Name: '+(sale.customer_name || '—'), left, y); y += 14;
  doc.text('Phone: '+(sale.customer_phone || '—'), left, y); y += 26;

  doc.setFont('helvetica','bold'); doc.setFontSize(11); doc.setTextColor(30);
  doc.text('Item', left, y); y += 15;
  doc.setFont('helvetica','normal'); doc.setFontSize(10); doc.setTextColor(70);
  doc.text('Model: '+(sale.model || '—'), left, y); y += 14;
  if(sale.imei){ doc.text('IMEI: '+sale.imei, left, y); y += 14; }
  doc.text('Quantity: '+(sale.quantity || 1), left, y); y += 14;
  if(sale.accessories){ doc.text('Accessories: '+sale.accessories, left, y); y += 14; }
  doc.text('Payment method: '+(sale.payment_method || '—'), left, y); y += 14;
  if(sale.staff){ doc.text('Served by: '+sale.staff, left, y); y += 14; }
  y += 12;

  doc.setDrawColor(210); doc.line(left, y, right, y); y += 24;
  doc.setFont('helvetica','bold'); doc.setFontSize(15); doc.setTextColor(30);
  doc.text('Amount paid: '+naira(sale.sale_price), left, y); y += 32;

  doc.setFont('helvetica','bold'); doc.setFontSize(11);
  doc.text('Warranty', left, y); y += 15;
  doc.setFont('helvetica','normal'); doc.setFontSize(10); doc.setTextColor(70);
  if(sale.warranty_days){
    const expiry = new Date(sale.date || todayISO());
    expiry.setDate(expiry.getDate() + Number(sale.warranty_days));
    doc.text(sale.warranty_days+' days from purchase — valid until '+expiry.toISOString().slice(0,10)+'.', left, y); y += 14;
    doc.text('Bring this invoice (or the phone number used at purchase) for any warranty claim.', left, y); y += 14;
  } else {
    doc.text('No warranty included on this sale.', left, y); y += 14;
  }

  y += 24;
  doc.setDrawColor(225); doc.line(left, y, right, y); y += 18;
  doc.setFont('helvetica','normal'); doc.setFontSize(9); doc.setTextColor(140);
  doc.text('Thank you for your purchase. Keep this document as proof of purchase and for warranty claims.', left, y);

  doc.save(invoiceNumberFor(sale)+'.pdf');
}

/* ---------- push notifications ---------- */
function isIOSDevice(){
  return /iP(hone|od|ad)/.test(navigator.userAgent) ||
    (navigator.platform === 'MacIntel' && navigator.maxTouchPoints > 1); // iPadOS reports as Mac
}
function isStandaloneDisplay(){
  return (window.matchMedia && window.matchMedia('(display-mode: standalone)').matches) || window.navigator.standalone === true;
}
function shouldShowIosInstallBanner(){
  return isIOSDevice() && !isStandaloneDisplay();
}
function renderIosInstallBanner(){
  if(!shouldShowIosInstallBanner()) return '';
