  return '<div id="iosInstallBanner" style="position:fixed;left:0;right:0;bottom:0;z-index:150;background:var(--panel-2);border-top:1px solid var(--accent);padding:12px 16px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;box-shadow:0 -8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.4);">' +
    '<div style="flex:1;font-size:12.5px;color:var(--text);">' +
      '<strong>Install PhoneHub on this iPhone</strong><br>' +
      '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);">Tap the Share icon <span style="display:inline-block;transform:translateY(2px)">'+ICONS_SHARE+'</span> below, then "Add to Home Screen" to receive phone and order requests. This also turns on notifications.</span>' +
    '</div>' +
  '</div>';
}
const ICONS_SHARE = '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="14" height="14" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" style="vertical-align:-2px"><path d="M12 3v12"/><path d="M8 7l4-4 4 4"/><path d="M5 12v7a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-7"/></svg>';
function urlBase64ToUint8Array(base64String){
  const padding = '='.repeat((4 - base64String.length % 4) % 4);
  const base64 = (base64String + padding).replace(/-/g, '+').replace(/_/g, '/');
  const rawData = atob(base64);
  const outputArray = new Uint8Array(rawData.length);
  for (let i = 0; i < rawData.length; ++i) outputArray[i] = rawData.charCodeAt(i);
  return outputArray;
}

async function initPush(){
  if(!('serviceWorker' in navigator) || !('PushManager' in window)){
    state.pushStatus = 'unsupported'; render(); return;
  }
  try{
    const reg = await navigator.serviceWorker.register('./sw.js');
    const existing = await reg.pushManager.getSubscription();
    if(existing && Notification.permission==='granted'){ state.pushStatus = 'on'; }
    else if(Notification.permission==='denied'){ state.pushStatus = 'denied'; }
    else { state.pushStatus = 'off'; }
  } catch(e){ state.pushStatus = 'unsupported'; }
  render();
}
async function initRealtime(){
  if(!sb || !state.profile) return;
  try{
    const channel = sb.channel('public-broadcasts');
    channel.on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'broadcasts' }, function(){
      refreshBroadcastsData();
    }).on('postgres_changes', { event: '*', schema: 'public', table: 'broadcast_responses' }, function(){
      refreshBroadcastsData();
    }).subscribe();
  } catch(e){ console.warn('Realtime init failed:', e); }
}
async function refreshBroadcastsData(){
  if(!state.profile) return;
  const [bc, br] = await Promise.all([
    sb.from('broadcasts').select('*').order('created_at',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('broadcast_responses').select('*')
  ]);
  state.broadcasts = bc.data || [];
  state.broadcastResponses = br.data || [];
  if(state.tab === 'network' && state.networkView === 'broadcasts'){
    render();
  }
}

async function enablePush(){
  if(!('serviceWorker' in navigator) || !('PushManager' in window)){
    showToast('Push notifications are not supported in this browser', true); return;
  }
  state.pushStatus = 'prompting'; render();
  try{
    const perm = await Notification.requestPermission();
    if(perm !== 'granted'){
      state.pushStatus = perm==='denied' ? 'denied' : 'off';
      showToast(perm==='denied' ? 'Notifications blocked — enable them in your browser/site settings' : 'Notifications not enabled', true);
      render(); return;
    }
    const reg = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    let sub = await reg.pushManager.getSubscription();
    if(!sub){
      sub = await reg.pushManager.subscribe({
        userVisibleOnly: true,
        applicationServerKey: urlBase64ToUint8Array(VAPID_PUBLIC_KEY)
      });
    }
    const json = sub.toJSON();
    const { error } = await sb.from('push_subscriptions').upsert({
      dealer_id: state.profile.id,
      endpoint: json.endpoint,
      p256dh: json.keys.p256dh,
      auth: json.keys.auth
    }, { onConflict: 'endpoint' });
    if(error) throw error;
    state.pushStatus = 'on';
    showToast('Notifications enabled — you\'ll get alerts even with the app closed');
  } catch(e){
    state.pushStatus = 'off';
    showToast('Could not enable notifications: '+(e.message||e), true);
  }
  render();
}

async function disablePush(){
  try{
    const reg = await navigator.serviceWorker.ready;
    const sub = await reg.pushManager.getSubscription();
    if(sub){
      await sb.from('push_subscriptions').delete().eq('endpoint', sub.endpoint);
      await sub.unsubscribe();
    }
    state.pushStatus = 'off';
    showToast('Notifications turned off for this device');
  } catch(e){ showToast('Could not disable: '+(e.message||e), true); }
  render();
}

/* ---------- bulk import parser ---------- */
function extractPrice(line){
  var m, lastN=null, lastK=null, lastC=null;
  var reN = /\bN\s?(\d[\d,]*)/gi;
  while((m = reN.exec(line))){ lastN = m; }
  if(lastN){
    var digitsN = lastN[1].replace(/,/g,'');
    if(digitsN.length) return { value: parseInt(digitsN,10), start: lastN.index, end: lastN.index + lastN[0].length };
  }
  var reK = /(\d+(?:[.,]\d{1,3})?)\s*k\b/gi;
  while((m = reK.exec(line))){ lastK = m; }
  if(lastK){
    var raw = lastK[1];
    var sepMatch = raw.match(/^(\d+)[.,](\d{1,3})$/);
    var value;
    if(sepMatch){
      var padded = (sepMatch[2] + '000').slice(0,3);
      value = parseInt(sepMatch[1]+padded, 10) * 1000;
    } else { value = parseFloat(raw) * 1000; }
    return { value: Math.round(value), start: lastK.index, end: lastK.index + lastK[0].length };
  }
  var reComma = /(\d{1,3}(?:,\d{3})+)/g;
  while((m = reComma.exec(line))){ lastC = m; }
  if(lastC){
    return { value: parseInt(lastC[1].replace(/,/g,''),10), start: lastC.index, end: lastC.index+lastC[0].length };
  }
  var mb = line.match(/(\d{3,})\s*$/);
  if(mb){ return { value: parseInt(mb[1],10), start: mb.index, end: mb.index+mb[0].length }; }
  return null;
}

function stripConnectivity(text){
  var tags = [['wifi','WiFi'],['sim','SIM']];
  var found = null;
  var out = text;
  for(var i=0;i<tags.length;i++){
    var re = new RegExp(tags[i][0], 'i');
    if(re.test(out)){ found = tags[i][1]; out = out.replace(re, ''); break; }
  }
  return { text: out, tag: found };
}

function toTitleCase(s){
  return s.replace(/\w\S*/g, function(t){
    if(t.length<=4 && t===t.toUpperCase() && /[A-Z]/.test(t)) return t;
    return t.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+t.substr(1).toLowerCase();
  });
}

function cleanSeparators(s){
  return s.replace(/^[\s\-\u2013\u2014_.:]+|[\s\-\u2013\u2014_.:]+$/g, '').trim();
}

function extractSlashStorage(text){
  var m = text.match(/(\d+)\s*\/\s*(\d+)\s*(t|tb|g|gb)?/i);
  if(!m) return null;
  var unit = m[3] ? (/^t/i.test(m[3]) ? 'TB' : 'GB') : 'GB';
  return { storage: m[2]+unit, start: m.index, end: m.index+m[0].length };
}
function extractUnitStorage(text){
  var re = /(\d{2,4})\s*(gb|tb|g|t)\b/gi;
  var m, last=null;
  while((m = re.exec(text))){ last = m; }
  if(!last) return null;
  var unit = /^t/i.test(last[2]) ? 'TB' : 'GB';
  return { storage: last[1]+unit, start: last.index, end: last.index+last[0].length };
}

const IPHONE_VARIANTS = [['promax','Pro Max'],['pro max','Pro Max'],['pro','Pro'],['plus','Plus'],['mini','Mini'],['air','Air']];
const IPHONE_SPECIALS = [['xsmax','XS Max'],['xs max','XS Max'],['xs','XS'],['xr','XR'],['se','SE'],['x','X']];

function tryIphone(compact){
  var body = compact;
  var strippedPrefix = false;
  if(/^ip(?!ad)/.test(body)){ body = body.replace(/^ip(hone)?/,''); strippedPrefix = true; }
  else if(/^iphone/.test(body)){ body = body.replace(/^iphone/,''); strippedPrefix = true; }
  for(var i=0;i<IPHONE_SPECIALS.length;i++){
    if(body.indexOf(IPHONE_SPECIALS[i][0])===0){
      var rem = body.slice(IPHONE_SPECIALS[i][0].length);
      return { model: 'iPhone '+IPHONE_SPECIALS[i][1], rest: rem };
    }
  }
  var numMatch = body.match(/^(\d{1,2})/);
  if(numMatch && (strippedPrefix || (parseInt(numMatch[1],10)>=6 && parseInt(numMatch[1],10)<=17))){
    var rest = body.slice(numMatch[0].length);
    var variant = '';
    for(var j=0;j<IPHONE_VARIANTS.length;j++){
      if(rest.indexOf(IPHONE_VARIANTS[j][0])===0){ variant = ' '+IPHONE_VARIANTS[j][1]; rest = rest.slice(IPHONE_VARIANTS[j][0].length); break; }
    }
    if(!strippedPrefix && !/^[0-9]*$/.test(rest)){ return null; }
    return { model: 'iPhone '+numMatch[1]+variant, rest: rest };
  }
  return null;
}

function trySamsung(compact){
  var m;
  if((m = compact.match(/^s(\d{1,2})/))){
    var rest = compact.slice(m[0].length);
    if(rest.indexOf('ultra')===0) return { model:'Galaxy S'+m[1]+' Ultra', rest: rest.slice(5) };
    if(rest.indexOf('plus')===0) return { model:'Galaxy S'+m[1]+' Plus', rest: rest.slice(4) };
    if(rest.indexOf('fe')===0) return { model:'Galaxy S'+m[1]+' FE', rest: rest.slice(2) };
    if(rest.indexOf('e')===0) return { model:'Galaxy S'+m[1]+'e', rest: rest.slice(1) };
    if(rest.indexOf('+')===0) return { model:'Galaxy S'+m[1]+'+', rest: rest.slice(1) };
    return { model:'Galaxy S'+m[1], rest: rest };
  }
  if((m = compact.match(/^note(\d{1,2})/))){
    var rest2 = compact.slice(m[0].length);
    if(rest2.indexOf('ultra')===0) return { model:'Galaxy Note'+m[1]+' Ultra', rest: rest2.slice(5) };
    if(rest2.indexOf('+')===0) return { model:'Galaxy Note'+m[1]+'+', rest: rest2.slice(1) };
    return { model:'Galaxy Note'+m[1], rest: rest2 };
  }
  if((m = compact.match(/^fold(\d)/))) return { model:'Galaxy Z Fold'+m[1], rest: compact.slice(m[0].length) };
  if((m = compact.match(/^flip(\d)/))) return { model:'Galaxy Z Flip'+m[1], rest: compact.slice(m[0].length) };
  if((m = compact.match(/^a(\d{1,3})/))) return { model:'Galaxy A'+m[1], rest: compact.slice(m[0].length) };
  return null;
}

function tryIpad(compact){
  var m = compact.match(/ipad(.*?)(\d{1,2})gen(.*)/);
  if(m) return { model: 'iPad ('+m[2]+'th Gen)', rest: m[3] };
  return null;
}

function parseBulkStockLine(raw){
  var flagged = /[\u274c\u2716\u2717]/.test(raw);
  var line = raw.replace(/[\u274c\u2716\u2717]/g, '');

  var connFirst = stripConnectivity(line);
  line = connFirst.text;
  var connTag = connFirst.tag;

  var priceInfo = extractPrice(line);
  if(!priceInfo){ return null; }

  var leadingText = cleanSeparators(line.slice(0, priceInfo.start));
  var trailingText = line.slice(priceInfo.end);

  var unavailable = flagged || /\bna\b/i.test(trailingText.replace(/[^a-zA-Z]/g,' '));

  var storage = '';
  var slash = extractSlashStorage(leadingText);
  if(slash){
    storage = slash.storage;
    leadingText = leadingText.slice(0,slash.start) + leadingText.slice(slash.end);
  } else {
    var unitStock = extractUnitStorage(leadingText);
    if(unitStock){
      storage = unitStock.storage;
      leadingText = leadingText.slice(0,unitStock.start) + leadingText.slice(unitStock.end);
    }
  }
  leadingText = cleanSeparators(leadingText);

  var connFromLead = stripConnectivity(leadingText);
  leadingText = cleanSeparators(connFromLead.text);
  if(connFromLead.tag) connTag = connFromLead.tag;

  var compact = leadingText.toLowerCase().replace(/[\s\-\u2013\u2014_.:]+/g,'');

  var result = tryIphone(compact) || trySamsung(compact) || tryIpad(compact);
  var model;
  if(result){
    model = result.model;
    var leftover = result.rest.replace(/[^0-9]/g,'');
    if(!storage && leftover){ storage = leftover+'GB'; }
  } else {
    var generic = leadingText;
    if(generic === generic.toUpperCase() || generic === generic.toLowerCase()){ generic = toTitleCase(generic); }
    model = generic || '(unrecognized)';
  }
  if(connTag) model = model + ' ('+connTag+')';

  return {
    raw: raw, model: model, storage: storage, price: priceInfo.value,
    include: !unavailable, flagged: unavailable, quantity: 1, recognized: !!result
  };
}

function parseBulkStock(text){
  const lines = text.split('\n').map(function(l){ return l.trim(); }).filter(Boolean);
  const rows = [], skipped = [];
  let sectionLabel = '';

  lines.forEach(function(raw){
    const parsed = parseBulkStockLine(raw);
    if(!parsed){
      if(raw.replace(/[^a-zA-Z]/g,'').length >= 3) sectionLabel = raw.trim();
      return;
    }
    if(!parsed.recognized) skipped.push({raw:raw});
    rows.push({
      raw: parsed.raw, model: parsed.model, storage: parsed.storage, price: parsed.price,
      include: parsed.include, flagged: parsed.flagged, quantity: parsed.quantity, sectionLabel: sectionLabel
    });
  });
  return { rows: rows, skipped: skipped };
}

function loadConfig(){
  if(HARDCODED_SUPABASE_URL && HARDCODED_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY){
    return { url: HARDCODED_SUPABASE_URL, key: HARDCODED_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY };
  }
  try{ const raw = localStorage.getItem(CONFIG_KEY); return raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : null; }
  catch(e){ return null; }
}
function saveConfig(url,key){
  try{ localStorage.setItem(CONFIG_KEY, JSON.stringify({url:url,key:key})); } catch(e){ /* ignore */ }
}

async function init(){
  const cfg = await loadConfig();
  if(!cfg){ state.stage='configure'; render(); return; }
  await connectSupabase(cfg.url, cfg.key, false);
}

async function connectSupabase(url, key, persist){
  try{
    sb = window.supabase.createClient(url, key);
    const { data, error } = await sb.auth.getSession();
    if(error) throw error;
    if(persist) await saveConfig(url, key);
    if(data.session){
      await loadAfterAuth();
    } else {
      state.stage = 'auth'; render();
    }
  } catch(e){
    state.stage = 'configure'; state.configError = e.message || String(e); render();
  }
}

async function loadAfterAuth(){
  try{
    const { data: { user } } = await sb.auth.getUser();
    const { data: profile, error: pErr } = await sb.from('dealers').select('*').eq('id', user.id).single();
    if(pErr) throw pErr;
    state.profile = profile; state.isAdmin = !!profile.is_admin;
    await refreshAll();
    state.stage = 'app';
    initPush();
    initRealtime();
    applyHashTab();
  } catch(e){
    state.stage = 'auth'; state.authError = 'Could not load your shop profile: ' + (e.message||e);
  }
  render();
}

async function refreshAll(){
  const [inv, sales, reqs, sups, dn, bc, rep, cons, cnp] = await Promise.all([
    sb.from('inventory').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id).order('created_at',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('sales').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id).order('date',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('requests').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id).order('date',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('suppliers').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id).order('created_at',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('dealer_network_view').select('*'),
    sb.from('broadcasts').select('*').order('created_at',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('dealer_reputation_view').select('*'),
    sb.from('consignments').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id).order('created_at',{ascending:false}),
    sb.from('consignment_payments').select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id).order('created_at',{ascending:false}),
  ]);
  state.inventory = inv.data || []; state.sales = sales.data || []; state.requests = reqs.data || [];
  state.suppliers = sups.data || []; state.dealerNetwork = dn.data || []; state.broadcasts = bc.data || [];
  state.consignments = cons.data || [];
  state.consignmentPayments = cnp.data || [];
  syncNetworkOrder();
  const repMap = {};
  (rep.data || []).forEach(function(r){ repMap[r.dealer_id] = r; });
  state.dealerReputation = repMap;
  const bcIds = state.broadcasts.map(function(b){return b.id;});
  if(bcIds.length){
    const br = await sb.from('broadcast_responses').select('*').in('broadcast_id', bcIds);
    state.broadcastResponses = br.data || [];
  } else { state.broadcastResponses = []; }

  if(state.isAdmin){
    const [ad, ai, as_] = await Promise.all([
      sb.from('dealers').select('*'),
      sb.from('inventory').select('*'),
      sb.from('sales').select('*'),
    ]);
    state.adminDealers = ad.data || []; state.adminInventory = ai.data || []; state.adminSales = as_.data || [];
  }
}

async function refreshOne(table, target, extraFilter){
  let q = sb.from(table).select('*').eq('dealer_id', state.profile.id);
  const { data, error } = await q;
  if(!error) state[target] = data || [];
}
async function toggleStatus(id){
  const item = state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
  if(!item) return;
  const newStatus = item.status==='In Stock' ? 'Sold' : 'In Stock';
  try{
    const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').update({status:newStatus}).eq('id', id);
    if(error) throw error;
    await refreshAll();
    showToast(item.status==='In Stock' ? 'Marked as out of stock' : 'Marked as in stock');
  } catch(e){ showToast('Update failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
}

function showToast(msg, err){ state.toast = msg; state.toastErr = !!err; render(); setTimeout(function(){ state.toast=null; render(); }, 3200); }
function setTab(t){ 
  state.tab = t; 
  state.modal=null; 
  if (window.location.hash !== '#tab=' + t) {
    history.replaceState(null, '', '#tab=' + t);
  }
  render(); 
}
function applyHashTab(){
  var hash = window.location.hash;
  if (hash.startsWith('#tab=')){
    var tab = hash.slice(5);
    var valid = ['dashboard','inventory','sales','calc','requests','network','admin'];
    if (valid.indexOf(tab) !== -1 && state.tab !== tab){
      state.tab = tab;
      render();
    }
  }
}
function openModal(name, payload){
  if(name==='addPhone' || name==='editPhone' || name==='addLaptop' || name==='editLaptop') state.photoModalRemovedUrls = [];
  if(name==='viewNetworkItem' || name==='viewStockItem') state.galleryIndex = 0;
  state.modal = {name:name, payload: payload||{}}; render();
}
function closeModal(){ state.modal = null; render(); }
function openBroadcastComposer(ids){
  if(!ids || !ids.length){ showToast('Select at least one phone first', true); return; }
  const items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return ids.indexOf(p.id)>-1; });
  state.broadcastComposer = { ids: ids, target: 'network', message: defaultBroadcastMessage(items), selectedContactIds: [] };
  openModal('sendBroadcastAdvert', {});
}

function isToday(d){ return d === todayISO(); }
function thisMonth(d){ if(!d) return false; const now=new Date(); const dd=new Date(d); return dd.getFullYear()===now.getFullYear() && dd.getMonth()===now.getMonth(); }

function computeKPIs(){
  const salesToday = state.sales.filter(function(s){ return isToday(s.date); });
  const salesMonth = state.sales.filter(function(s){ return thisMonth(s.date); });
  const profit = function(s){ return (Number(s.sale_price)||0) - (Number(s.cost)||0); };
  const inStock = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return p.status==='In Stock'; });
  const reserved = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return p.status==='Reserved'; });
  const stockValue = inStock.reduce(function(a,p){ return a+((Number(p.cost)||0)*(Number(p.quantity)||1)); },0);
  const warrantyList = state.sales.map(function(s){
    if(!s.date || !s.warranty_days) return null;
    const expiry = new Date(s.date); expiry.setDate(expiry.getDate()+Number(s.warranty_days));
    const daysLeft = daysBetween(todayISO(), expiry.toISOString().slice(0,10));
    return Object.assign({}, s, {daysLeft:daysLeft});
  }).filter(Boolean);
  const expiringSoon = warrantyList.filter(function(w){ return w.daysLeft>=0 && w.daysLeft<=7; }).length;
  const expired = warrantyList.filter(function(w){ return w.daysLeft<0; }).length;
  const pendingRequests = state.requests.filter(function(r){ return r.status==='Pending'; }).length;
  const openBroadcasts = state.broadcasts.filter(function(b){ return b.status==='Open'; }).length;
  const outstandingConsignments = state.consignments.filter(function(c){ return c.status!=='Settled' && c.status!=='Returned'; });
  const consignOwed = outstandingConsignments.reduce(function(a,c){ return a+consignmentBalance(c); },0);
  return {
    unitsToday: salesToday.length,
    revenueToday: salesToday.reduce(function(a,s){ return a+(Number(s.sale_price)||0); },0),
    profitToday: salesToday.reduce(function(a,s){ return a+profit(s); },0),
    unitsMonth: salesMonth.length,
    revenueMonth: salesMonth.reduce(function(a,s){ return a+(Number(s.sale_price)||0); },0),
    profitMonth: salesMonth.reduce(function(a,s){ return a+profit(s); },0),
    inStockCount: inStock.length, reservedCount: reserved.length, stockValue: stockValue,
    expiringSoon: expiringSoon, expired: expired, pendingRequests: pendingRequests, openBroadcasts: openBroadcasts,
    consignCount: outstandingConsignments.length, consignOwed: consignOwed
  };
}

// Total still owed to you on a consignment (what colleague should pay, minus what they've paid).
function consignmentBalance(c){
  const total = (Number(c.unit_price)||0) * (Number(c.quantity)||1);
  return total - (Number(c.amount_paid)||0);
}

function staffLeaderboard(){
  const map = {};
  state.sales.filter(function(s){ return thisMonth(s.date); }).forEach(function(s){
    const k = s.staff || 'Unassigned';
    if(!map[k]) map[k] = {staff:k, units:0, revenue:0, profit:0};
    map[k].units++; map[k].revenue += Number(s.sale_price)||0;
    map[k].profit += (Number(s.sale_price)||0)-(Number(s.cost)||0);
  });
  return Object.values(map).sort(function(a,b){ return b.profit-a.profit; });
}

function searchAll(q){
  if(!q || q.trim().length<1) return [];
  q = q.toLowerCase();
  const invHits = state.inventory.filter(function(p){
    return String(p.imei||'').includes(q) || String(p.imei2||'').includes(q) || String(p.model||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      String(p.color||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || String(p.supplier||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      String(p.brand||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || String(p.cpu||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || String(p.ram||'').toLowerCase().includes(q);
  }).map(function(p){ return {type:'phone', item:p}; });
  const saleHits = state.sales.filter(function(s){
    return String(s.customer_name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || String(s.customer_phone||'').includes(q);
  }).map(function(s){ return {type:'sale', item:s}; });
  return invHits.concat(saleHits).slice(0,8);
}

/* ---------- render root ---------- */
function render(){
  const app = document.getElementById('app');
  if(state.stage==='loading'){ app.innerHTML = '<div class="loading-screen"><div class="spinner"></div>booting dealer console…</div>'; return; }
  if(state.stage==='configure'){ app.innerHTML = renderConfigureScreen(); attachConfigureHandlers(); return; }
  if(state.stage==='auth'){ app.innerHTML = renderAuthScreen() + renderIosInstallBanner(); attachAuthHandlers(); return; }

  app.innerHTML =
    '<div class="rail-backdrop '+(state.mobileMenuOpen?'open':'')+'" id="railBackdrop"></div>' +
    '<div class="rail '+(state.mobileMenuOpen?'open':'')+'">' +
      '<button class="rail-close-btn" id="railCloseBtn" aria-label="Close menu">×</button>' +
      '<div class="rail-logo">PH</div>' +
      railItem('dashboard','Home') + railItem('inventory','Stock') + railItem('sales','Sales') +
      railItem('calc','Price') + railItem('requests','Asks', badgeCount(state.requests.filter(function(r){return r.status==='Pending';}).length)) +
      railItem('consign','Owed', badgeCount(state.consignments.filter(function(c){return c.status!=='Settled' && c.status!=='Returned';}).length)) +
      railItem('network','Network', badgeCount(state.broadcasts.filter(function(b){return b.status==='Open';}).length)) +
      (state.isAdmin ? railItem('admin','Admin') : '') +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="main">' +
      '<div class="topbar" style="position:relative;">' +
        '<button class="hamburger-btn" id="hamburgerBtn" aria-label="Open menu">'+ICONS.hamburger+'</button>' +
        '<div class="search-wrap"><span class="prompt">›</span>' +
        '<input id="globalSearch" placeholder="Search IMEI, model, or customer…" value="'+escapeAttr(state.searchQuery)+'"/></div>' +
        (state.searchQuery ? renderSearchDropdown() : '') +
        '<div class="topbar-right">' +
          '<span class="dot"></span> '+escapeHtml(state.profile.shop_name)+(state.isAdmin?' <span class="badge badge-admin">admin</span>':'') +
          '<span class="bell '+(state.pushStatus==='on'?'on':'')+'" id="notifBellBtn" title="Notification settings">'+ICONS.bell+'</span>' +
          '<span class="theme-toggle" id="themeSettingsBtn" title="Display theme">'+ICONS.theme+'</span>' +
          '<span class="gear" id="logoutBtn" title="Log out">'+ICONS.gear+'</span>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="content">'+renderTab()+'</div>' +
    '</div>' +
    (state.modal ? renderModal() : '') +
    renderIosInstallBanner() +
    (state.toast ? ('<div class="toast '+(state.toastErr?'err':'')+'">'+escapeHtml(state.toast)+'</div>') : '');
  attachHandlers();
}

/* ---------- configure (one-time, platform-wide) ---------- */
function renderConfigureScreen(){
  return '<div class="connect-wrap"><div class="connect-card">' +
    '<h2>Connect this app to Supabase</h2>' +
    '<p>One-time setup for the whole platform. Paste your Supabase project URL and anon (public) key — find both in your Supabase project under Settings → API.</p>' +
    (state.configError ? ('<div class="connect-status err">'+escapeHtml(state.configError)+'</div>') : '') +
    '<input id="cfgUrl" placeholder="https://xxxxx.supabase.co" value="'+escapeAttr(state.urlInput)+'"/>' +
    '<input id="cfgKey" class="mono" placeholder="anon public key (eyJ...)" value="'+escapeAttr(state.keyInput)+'"/>' +
    '<button class="btn btn-accent" id="cfgConnectBtn" style="width:100%;justify-content:center;" '+(state.configuring?'disabled':'')+'>'+(state.configuring?'Connecting…':'Connect')+'</button>' +
    '<div class="footer-note" style="padding-top:16px;">See SUPABASE_SETUP_GUIDE.md for how to create the project and run the schema.</div>' +
  '</div></div>';
}
function attachConfigureHandlers(){
  const u = document.getElementById('cfgUrl'), k = document.getElementById('cfgKey');
  if(u) u.addEventListener('input', function(e){ state.urlInput = e.target.value; });
  if(k) k.addEventListener('input', function(e){ state.keyInput = e.target.value; });
  const btn = document.getElementById('cfgConnectBtn');
  if(btn) btn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const url = (document.getElementById('cfgUrl').value||'').trim();
    const key = (document.getElementById('cfgKey').value||'').trim();
    if(!url || !key){ state.configError = 'Please fill in both fields.'; render(); return; }
    state.configuring = true; state.configError=null; render();
    await connectSupabase(url, key, true);
    state.configuring = false;
  });
}

/* ---------- auth (sign up / log in) ---------- */
function renderAuthScreen(){
  const signup = state.authMode==='signup';
  return '<div class="connect-wrap"><div class="connect-card">' +
    '<h2>'+(signup?'Register your shop':'Welcome back')+'</h2>' +
    '<div class="auth-tabs">' +
      '<div class="auth-tab '+(!signup?'active':'')+'" data-auth-mode="login">Log in</div>' +
      '<div class="auth-tab '+(signup?'active':'')+'" data-auth-mode="signup">Register</div>' +
    '</div>' +
    (state.authError ? ('<div class="connect-status err">'+escapeHtml(state.authError)+'</div>') : '') +
    (signup ? (
      '<input id="a-shop" placeholder="Shop name (e.g. Musa Electronics)"/>' +
      '<input id="a-phone" placeholder="Phone number"/>' +
      '<input id="a-location" placeholder="Location (e.g. Otigba Street)"/>'
    ) : '') +
    '<input id="a-email" placeholder="Email" type="email"/>' +
    '<input id="a-password" placeholder="Password" type="password"/>' +
    '<button class="btn btn-accent" id="authBtn" style="width:100%;justify-content:center;" '+(state.authBusy?'disabled':'')+'>' +
      (state.authBusy ? 'Please wait…' : (signup?'Create shop account':'Log in')) +
    '</button>' +
    (signup ? '<div class="footer-note">If email confirmation is on in your Supabase project, check your inbox after registering.</div>' : '') +
  '</div></div>';
}
function attachAuthHandlers(){
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-auth-mode]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.authMode = el.getAttribute('data-auth-mode'); state.authError=null; render(); });
  });
  const btn = document.getElementById('authBtn');
  if(btn) btn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const email = val('a-email'), password = val('a-password');
    const shopName = val('a-shop'), phoneField = val('a-phone'), locationField = val('a-location');
    if(!email || !password){ state.authError='Email and password are required.'; render(); return; }
    if(state.authMode==='signup' && !shopName){ state.authError='Shop name is required.'; render(); return; }
    state.authBusy = true; state.authError = null; render();
    try{
      if(state.authMode==='signup'){
        const shopSlug = slugify(shopName) + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6);
        const { data, error } = await sb.auth.signUp({
          email:email, password:password,
          options:{ data:{ shop_name:shopName, shop_slug:shopSlug, phone:phoneField, location:locationField } }
        });
        if(error) throw error;
        if(!data.session){
          state.authBusy = false;
          state.authError = 'Check your email to confirm your account, then log in.';
          state.authMode = 'login'; render(); return;
        }
      } else {
        const { error } = await sb.auth.signInWithPassword({ email:email, password:password });
        if(error) throw error;
      }
      state.authBusy = false;
      await loadAfterAuth();
    } catch(e){
      state.authBusy = false; state.authError = e.message || String(e); render();
    }
  });
}

function badgeCount(n){ return n>0 ? '<span style="position:absolute;margin-left:26px;margin-top:-30px;background:var(--accent);color:#10141C;font-size:9px;font-weight:700;border-radius:8px;padding:1px 5px;">'+n+'</span>' : ''; }
function pillBadge(n){ return n>0 ? '<span style="display:inline-block;margin-left:6px;background:var(--accent);color:#10141C;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;border-radius:8px;padding:1px 6px;">'+n+'</span>' : ''; }
function railItem(key, label, extra){
  return '<div class="rail-item '+(state.tab===key?'active':'')+'" data-tab="'+key+'" style="position:relative">'+ICONS[key]+'<span>'+label+'</span>'+(extra||'')+'</div>';
}

function renderSearchDropdown(){
  const results = searchAll(state.searchQuery);
  if(!results.length) return '<div class="search-results"><div class="search-row" style="color:var(--text-faint)">No matches for "'+escapeHtml(state.searchQuery)+'"</div></div>';
  return '<div class="search-results">' + results.map(function(r){
    if(r.type==='phone'){
      const p = r.item;
      const isLaptop = (p.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
      return '<div class="search-row" data-open-phone="'+p.id+'" data-open-item-type="'+(p.item_type||'Phone')+'">' +
        '<div><div class="sr-main">'+(isLaptop?'💻 ':'📱 ')+escapeHtml(itemLabel(p))+'</div>' +
        '<div class="sr-sub">'+(isLaptop?escapeHtml(p.storage||''):('IMEI '+escapeHtml(p.imei||'—')))+' · '+badge(p.status)+'</div></div>' +
        '<div class="sr-price">'+naira(p.price)+'</div></div>';
    } else {
      const s = r.item;
      return '<div class="search-row">' +
        '<div><div class="sr-main">'+escapeHtml(s.customer_name)+'</div>' +
        '<div class="sr-sub">'+escapeHtml(s.customer_phone)+' · bought '+escapeHtml(s.model)+'</div></div>' +
        '<div class="sr-price">'+naira(s.sale_price)+'</div></div>';
    }
  }).join('') + '</div>';
}

function badge(status){
  const map = {'In Stock':'badge-stock','Sold':'badge-sold','Reserved':'badge-reserved','In Repair':'badge-repair','Consigned':'badge-repair','Pending':'badge-reserved','Fulfilled':'badge-stock','Cancelled':'badge-sold','Open':'badge-open','Closed':'badge-closed','Out':'badge-reserved','Partially Paid':'badge-repair','Settled':'badge-stock','Returned':'badge-sold'};
  return '<span class="badge '+(map[status]||'badge-new')+'">'+escapeHtml(status)+'</span>';
}

const REP_TIER = {
  elite:   {label:'⭐ Elite dealer',    cls:'badge-admin'},
  trusted: {label:'✓ Trusted dealer',  cls:'badge-stock'},
  active:  {label:'Active',            cls:'badge-new'},
  new:     {label:'New',               cls:'badge-new'}
};
function formatResponseMinutes(mins){
  if(mins==null) return '';
  if(mins < 60) return Math.round(mins)+'m';
  if(mins < 1440) return Math.round(mins/60)+'h';
  return Math.round(mins/1440)+'d';
}
function reputationBadgeHTML(dealerId, opts){
  opts = opts || {};
  const r = state.dealerReputation[dealerId];
  if(!r || r.tier==='new') return opts.compact ? '' : '<span class="badge badge-new" title="No broadcast responses yet">New dealer</span>';
  const t = REP_TIER[r.tier] || REP_TIER.active;
  let extra = '';
  if(r.fulfillment_rate_pct!=null) extra += ' · '+r.fulfillment_rate_pct+'% fulfilled';
  if(r.avg_response_minutes!=null) extra += ' · ~'+formatResponseMinutes(r.avg_response_minutes)+' avg reply';
  return '<span class="badge '+t.cls+'" title="'+r.responses_count+' network responses'+escapeAttr(extra)+'">'+t.label+(opts.compact?'':escapeHtml(extra))+'</span>';
}

function renderTab(){
  if(state.tab==='dashboard') return renderDashboard();
  if(state.tab==='inventory') return renderInventory();
  if(state.tab==='sales') return renderSales();
  if(state.tab==='calc') return renderCalc();
  if(state.tab==='requests') return renderRequests();
  if(state.tab==='consign') return renderConsignments();
  if(state.tab==='network') return renderNetwork();
  if(state.tab==='admin') return renderAdmin();
  return '';
}

function renderDashboard(){
  const k = computeKPIs();
  const board = staffLeaderboard();
  return '<h1 class="page-title">Today on the floor</h1>' +
    '<p class="page-sub">'+new Date().toLocaleDateString('en-NG',{weekday:'long', year:'numeric', month:'long', day:'numeric'})+'</p>' +
    (state.pushStatus==='off' ? ('<div class="section"><div class="section-body" style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:14px;flex-wrap:wrap;">' +
      '<div>'+ICONS.bell.replace('<svg ', '<svg style="width:16px;height:16px;vertical-align:-3px;margin-right:6px;color:var(--accent)" ')+'<strong>Turn on phone alerts</strong> — get notified the moment a customer asks for a phone, a dealer broadcasts a need, or a warranty is about to expire, even with the app closed.</div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-accent" id="enablePushInline">Enable notifications</button>' +
    '</div></div>') : '') +
    '<div class="kpi-grid">' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Units sold today</div><div class="kpi-value">'+k.unitsToday+'</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Revenue today</div><div class="kpi-value accent">'+naira(k.revenueToday)+'</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Profit today</div><div class="kpi-value good">'+naira(k.profitToday)+'</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Phones in stock</div><div class="kpi-value">'+k.inStockCount+'</div><div class="kpi-delta">'+k.reservedCount+' reserved</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Stock value (cost)</div><div class="kpi-value">'+naira(k.stockValue)+'</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Warranty alerts</div><div class="kpi-value '+(k.expired>0?'warn':'')+'">'+(k.expiringSoon+k.expired)+'</div><div class="kpi-delta">'+k.expiringSoon+' expiring soon · '+k.expired+' expired</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Owed to you (consignment)</div><div class="kpi-value '+(k.consignOwed>0?'accent':'')+'">'+naira(k.consignOwed)+'</div><div class="kpi-delta">'+k.consignCount+' phone'+(k.consignCount===1?'':'s')+' out with colleagues</div></div>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-head"><h3>This month</h3></div>' +
      '<div class="section-body kpi-grid" style="margin:0;">' +
        '<div><div class="kpi-label">Units sold</div><div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:19px">'+k.unitsMonth+'</div></div>' +
        '<div><div class="kpi-label">Revenue</div><div class="kpi-value" style="font-size:19px">'+naira(k.revenueMonth)+'</div></div>' +
        '<div><div class="kpi-label">Profit</div><div class="kpi-value good" style="font-size:19px">'+naira(k.profitMonth)+'</div></div>' +
      '</div></div>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-head"><h3>Staff leaderboard — this month</h3></div>' +
      '<div class="section-body" style="padding:0;">' +
        (board.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Staff</th><th>Units</th><th>Revenue</th><th>Profit</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
          board.map(function(b){ return '<tr><td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(b.staff)+'</td><td class="mono">'+b.units+'</td><td class="mono">'+naira(b.revenue)+'</td><td class="mono" style="color:var(--success)">'+naira(b.profit)+'</td></tr>'; }).join('') +
        '</tbody></table>') : '<div class="empty">No sales logged yet this month.</div>') +
      '</div></div>' +
    ((k.pendingRequests>0 || k.openBroadcasts>0) ? ('<div class="section"><div class="section-body" style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:14px;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;">' +
      '<div>'+(k.pendingRequests>0?('<strong style="color:var(--accent)">'+k.pendingRequests+' customer request'+(k.pendingRequests>1?'s':'')+'</strong> waiting. '):'')+(k.openBroadcasts>0?('<strong style="color:var(--accent)">'+k.openBroadcasts+' open broadcast'+(k.openBroadcasts>1?'s':'')+'</strong> across the network.'):'')+'</div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;">' +
        (k.pendingRequests>0?'<button class="btn btn-sm" data-tab="requests">View requests</button>':'') +
        (k.openBroadcasts>0?'<button class="btn btn-sm" data-tab="network">View network</button>':'') +
      '</div></div></div>') : '') +
    (k.consignCount>0 ? ('<div class="section"><div class="section-body" style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:14px;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;">' +
      '<div>'+ICONS.consign.replace('<svg ', '<svg style="width:15px;height:15px;vertical-align:-3px;margin-right:6px;color:var(--accent)" ')+
        '<strong style="color:var(--accent)">'+naira(k.consignOwed)+'</strong> owed to you across '+k.consignCount+' colleague'+(k.consignCount>1?'s':'')+' holding phones on credit.</div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-tab="consign">View ledger</button>' +
    '</div></div>') : '');
}

function renderInventory(){
  const itemTab = state.inventoryItemTab === 'laptops' ? 'Laptop' : 'Phone';
  const noun = itemTab === 'Laptop' ? 'laptop' : 'phone';
  let items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return (p.item_type||'Phone') === itemTab; })
    .sort(function(a,b){ return (a.status==='In Stock'?0:1)-(b.status==='In Stock'?0:1); });
  const allOfType = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return (p.item_type||'Phone') === itemTab; });
  const phoneCount = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return (p.item_type||'Phone')==='Phone'; }).length;
  const laptopCount = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return p.item_type==='Laptop'; }).length;

  const subTabs = '<div class="pill-tabs">' +
      '<div class="pill-tab '+(state.inventoryItemTab==='phones'?'active':'')+'" data-inventory-item-tab="phones">📱 Phones'+pillBadge(phoneCount)+'</div>' +
      '<div class="pill-tab '+(state.inventoryItemTab==='laptops'?'active':'')+'" data-inventory-item-tab="laptops">💻 Laptops'+pillBadge(laptopCount)+'</div>' +
    '</div>';

  let header = '';
  if (state.inventorySupplierFilter){
    items = items.filter(function(p){ return p.supplier_id === state.inventorySupplierFilter; });
    const filterContact = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === state.inventorySupplierFilter; });
    const filterName = filterContact ? filterContact.name : state.supplierFilterName;
    header = '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:10px;">' +
      '<div><h1 class="page-title">Stock gotten from '+escapeHtml(filterName)+'</h1><p class="page-sub">'+items.length+' '+noun+(items.length===1?'':'s')+' tracked</p></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;"><button class="btn" data-clear-supplier-filter="1">← Back to all inventory</button></div>' +
    '</div>';
  } else {
    header = '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:10px;">' +
      '<div><h1 class="page-title">Inventory</h1><p class="page-sub">'+allOfType.length+' '+noun+'s tracked · '+allOfType.filter(function(p){return p.status==='In Stock';}).length+' in stock</p></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;">' +
        (items.some(function(p){return p.status==='In Stock';}) ? '<button class="btn" id="selectAllInStockBtn">Select all in stock</button>' : '') +
        (itemTab==='Phone' ? '<button class="btn" data-open-modal="bulkImport">📋 Paste stock list</button>' : '') +
        (itemTab==='Phone'
          ? '<button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="addPhone">'+ICONS.plus+' Add phone</button>'
          : '<button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="addLaptop">'+ICONS.plus+' Add laptop</button>') +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>';
  }
  const selectedCount = state.selectedInventoryIds.length;
  const selectionBar = selectedCount>0 ? ('<div class="section" style="margin-top:16px;border-color:var(--accent);"><div class="section-body" style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:12px;flex-wrap:wrap;">' +
      '<div><strong>'+selectedCount+'</strong> item'+(selectedCount===1?'':'s')+' selected</div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;"><button class="btn" id="clearSelectionBtn">Clear</button><button class="btn btn-accent" id="broadcastSelectedBtn">'+ICONS.broadcast.replace('<svg ', '<svg style="width:14px;height:14px;vertical-align:-2px;margin-right:4px;" ')+'Broadcast selected</button></div>' +
    '</div></div>') : '';

  const table = itemTab==='Phone' ? renderPhoneInventoryTable(items) : renderLaptopInventoryTable(items);

  return subTabs + header + selectionBar +
    '<div class="section" style="margin-top:16px;"><div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' + table + '</div></div>';
}

function renderPhoneInventoryTable(items){
  if(!items.length) return '<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No phones from this contact yet.</div></div>';
  return '<table><thead><tr><th></th><th>Photo</th><th>Model</th><th>IMEI</th><th>Qty</th><th>Storage / Color</th><th>Condition</th><th>Cost</th><th>Price</th><th>Profit</th><th>Status</th><th>Shelf</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
    items.map(function(p){ return '<tr>' +
      '<td><input type="checkbox" data-select-inventory="'+p.id+'" '+(state.selectedInventoryIds.indexOf(p.id)>-1?'checked':'')+'/></td>' +
      '<td>'+thumbHTML(p.image_url)+'</td>' +
      '<td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(p.model)+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.imei?escapeHtml(p.imei):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.quantity!=null?p.quantity:1)+'</td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.storage)+' · '+escapeHtml(p.color)+'</td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.condition)+(p.condition==='Used'?(' · '+p.battery+'% batt'):'')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.cost?naira(p.cost):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.price?naira(p.price):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono" style="color:var(--success)">'+(p.price?naira((Number(p.price)||0)-(Number(p.cost)||0)):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td><button class="btn btn-sm '+(p.status==='In Stock'?'btn-stock-toggle-on':'btn-stock-toggle-off')+'" data-toggle-status="'+p.id+'">'+(p.status==='In Stock'?'In Stock':'Out of Stock')+'</button></td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.shelf)+'</td>' +
      '<td style="display:flex;gap:6px;white-space:nowrap;">' +
        '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-open-modal="editPhone" data-id="'+p.id+'">Edit</button>' +
        '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-broadcast-single="'+p.id+'" title="Send as broadcast">📣</button>' +
      '</td>' +
    '</tr>'; }).join('') +
  '</tbody></table>';
}

function renderLaptopInventoryTable(items){
  if(!items.length) return '<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No laptops in inventory yet.</div></div>';
  return '<table><thead><tr><th></th><th>Photo</th><th>Brand / Model</th><th>Qty</th><th>CPU / RAM</th><th>Storage · Screen</th><th>Condition</th><th>Cost</th><th>Price</th><th>Profit</th><th>Status</th><th>Shelf</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
    items.map(function(p){ return '<tr>' +
      '<td><input type="checkbox" data-select-inventory="'+p.id+'" '+(state.selectedInventoryIds.indexOf(p.id)>-1?'checked':'')+'/></td>' +
      '<td>'+thumbHTML(p.image_url)+'</td>' +
      '<td class="strong">'+(p.brand?escapeHtml(p.brand)+' — ':'')+escapeHtml(p.model)+'<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-faint);font-weight:400;">'+escapeHtml(p.color||'')+'</div></td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.quantity!=null?p.quantity:1)+'</td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.cpu||'—')+'<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-faint);">'+escapeHtml(p.ram||'')+'</div></td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.storage||'—')+(p.screen_size?(' · '+escapeHtml(p.screen_size)):'')+(p.gpu?('<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-faint);">'+escapeHtml(p.gpu)+'</div>'):'')+'</td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.condition)+(p.condition==='Used' && p.battery!=null?(' · '+p.battery+'% batt'):'')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.cost?naira(p.cost):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono">'+(p.price?naira(p.price):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td class="mono" style="color:var(--success)">'+(p.price?naira((Number(p.price)||0)-(Number(p.cost)||0)):'<span style="color:var(--text-faint)">—</span>')+'</td>' +
      '<td><button class="btn btn-sm '+(p.status==='In Stock'?'btn-stock-toggle-on':'btn-stock-toggle-off')+'" data-toggle-status="'+p.id+'">'+(p.status==='In Stock'?'In Stock':'Out of Stock')+'</button></td>' +
      '<td>'+escapeHtml(p.shelf)+'</td>' +
      '<td style="display:flex;gap:6px;white-space:nowrap;">' +
        '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-open-modal="editLaptop" data-id="'+p.id+'">Edit</button>' +
        '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-broadcast-single="'+p.id+'" title="Send as broadcast">📣</button>' +
      '</td>' +
    '</tr>'; }).join('') +
  '</tbody></table>';
}

function renderSales(){
  const rows = state.sales.slice().sort(function(a,b){ return new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date); });
  return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;">' +
      '<div><h1 class="page-title">Sales log</h1><p class="page-sub">'+state.sales.length+' sales recorded</p></div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="logSale">'+ICONS.plus+' Log a sale</button>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' +
      (rows.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Phone</th><th>Customer</th><th>Sale price</th><th>Profit</th><th>Payment</th><th>Staff</th><th>Warranty</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
        rows.map(function(s){
          const expiry = new Date(s.date); expiry.setDate(expiry.getDate()+Number(s.warranty_days||0));
          const daysLeft = daysBetween(todayISO(), expiry.toISOString().slice(0,10));
          const wStatus = !s.warranty_days ? '—' : daysLeft<0 ? badge('Expired') : daysLeft<=7 ? ('<span class="badge badge-danger">'+daysLeft+'d left</span>') : (daysLeft+'d left');
          return '<tr>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+escapeHtml(s.date)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(s.model)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(s.customer_name)+'<br><span class="mono" style="color:var(--text-faint);font-size:11px">'+escapeHtml(s.customer_phone)+'</span></td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+naira(s.sale_price)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono" style="color:var(--success)">'+naira((Number(s.sale_price)||0)-(Number(s.cost)||0))+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(s.payment_method)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(s.staff)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+wStatus+'</td>' +
          '<td><button class="btn btn-sm" data-print-invoice="'+s.id+'">🧾 Invoice</button></td>' +
        '</tr>'; }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>') : ('<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No sales logged yet.</div></div>')) +
    '</div></div>';
}

function renderCalc(){
  const c = state.calcInputs;
  const recommended = Number(c.cost)+Number(c.target);
  const minimum = Number(c.cost)+Number(c.min);
  const actualProfit = Number(c.offer)-Number(c.cost);
  const accept = Number(c.offer) >= minimum;
  return '<h1 class="page-title">Smart profit calculator</h1>' +
    '<p class="page-sub">Price a phone you\'re sourcing from another dealer — before you quote the customer.</p>' +
    '<div class="section" style="max-width:640px;"><div class="section-body">' +
      '<div class="form-grid">' +
        '<div class="field mono"><label>Dealer / cost price (₦)</label><input type="number" id="calc-cost" value="'+c.cost+'"/></div>' +
        '<div class="field mono"><label>Your target profit (₦)</label><input type="number" id="calc-target" value="'+c.target+'"/></div>' +
        '<div class="field mono"><label>Minimum acceptable profit (₦)</label><input type="number" id="calc-min" value="'+c.min+'"/></div>' +
        '<div class="field mono"><label>Customer\'s negotiated offer (₦)</label><input type="number" id="calc-offer" value="'+c.offer+'"/></div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="calc-result">' +
        '<div class="row"><span>Recommended selling price</span><span class="v">'+naira(recommended)+'</span></div>' +
        '<div class="row"><span>Walk-away minimum price</span><span class="v">'+naira(minimum)+'</span></div>' +
        '<div class="row"><span>Actual profit at their offer</span><span class="v" style="color:'+(actualProfit>=0?'var(--success)':'var(--danger)')+'">'+naira(actualProfit)+'</span></div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="verdict '+(accept?'ok':'no')+'">'+(accept ? '✅ Accept — still profitable' : '⚠️ Below your minimum — reject or renegotiate')+'</div>' +
    '</div></div>';
}

function renderRequests(){
  const rows = state.requests.slice().sort(function(a,b){ return new Date(b.date)-new Date(a.date); });
  return '<h1 class="page-title">Customer requests</h1>' +
    '<p class="page-sub">Phones customers asked for that weren\'t in stock — submitted from your Customer App storefront.</p>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' +
      (rows.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Customer</th><th>Phone wanted</th><th>Budget</th><th>Status</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
        rows.map(function(r){ return '<tr>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+escapeHtml(r.date)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(r.customer_name)+'<br><span class="mono" style="color:var(--text-faint);font-size:11px">'+escapeHtml(r.customer_phone)+'</span></td>' +
          '<td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(r.model)+(r.storage?(' · '+escapeHtml(r.storage)):'')+(r.color?(' · '+escapeHtml(r.color)):'')+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+(r.budget?naira(r.budget):'—')+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+badge(r.status)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+(r.status==='Pending' ? ('<button class="btn btn-sm" data-fulfill-request="'+r.id+'">Mark fulfilled</button>') : '')+'</td>' +
        '</tr>'; }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>') : ('<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No customer requests yet.</div></div>')) +
    '</div></div>';
}

function renderConsignments(){
  const rows = state.consignments.slice().sort(function(a,b){
    const rank = function(c){ return (c.status==='Out'||c.status==='Partially Paid') ? 0 : 1; };
    const r = rank(a)-rank(b);
    if(r) return r;
    return new Date(b.created_at)-new Date(a.created_at);
  });
  const totalOwed = state.consignments.filter(function(c){ return c.status!=='Settled' && c.status!=='Returned'; })
    .reduce(function(a,c){ return a+consignmentBalance(c); },0);
  return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:10px;">' +
      '<div><h1 class="page-title">Owed to you</h1><p class="page-sub">Phones colleagues collected from you on credit, and what they still owe. Tap a row to see the full payment log. Total outstanding: <strong style="color:var(--accent)">'+naira(totalOwed)+'</strong></p></div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="addConsignment">'+ICONS.plus+' Log phone given out</button>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' +
      (rows.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Colleague</th><th>Phone</th><th>Qty</th><th>Unit price</th><th>Paid</th><th>Balance</th><th>Status</th><th>Date given</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
        rows.map(function(c){
          const balance = consignmentBalance(c);
          const canSettle = c.status!=='Settled' && c.status!=='Returned';
          return '<tr data-view-consignment="'+c.id+'" style="cursor:pointer;">' +
          '<td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(c.contact_name)+(c.contact_phone?('<br><span class="mono" style="color:var(--text-faint);font-size:11px">'+escapeHtml(c.contact_phone)+'</span>'):'')+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(c.model)+(c.storage?(' · '+escapeHtml(c.storage)):'')+(c.color?(' · '+escapeHtml(c.color)):'')+(c.imei?('<br><span class="mono" style="color:var(--text-faint);font-size:11px">IMEI '+escapeHtml(c.imei)+'</span>'):'')+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+(c.quantity||1)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+naira(c.unit_price)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+naira(c.amount_paid)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono" style="color:'+(balance>0?'var(--danger)':'var(--success)')+'">'+naira(balance)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+badge(c.status)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+escapeHtml(c.date_given)+'</td>' +
          '<td style="display:flex;gap:6px;white-space:nowrap;">' +
            (canSettle ? '<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" data-open-modal="logConsignmentPayment" data-id="'+c.id+'">Log payment</button>' : '') +
            '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-open-modal="editConsignment" data-id="'+c.id+'">Edit</button>' +
          '</td>' +
        '</tr>'; }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>') : ('<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No phones given out on credit yet. Log one when a colleague collects stock from you.</div></div>')) +
    '</div></div>';
}

function renderNetwork(){
  const openBroadcastCount = state.broadcasts.filter(function(b){ return b.status==='Open'; }).length;
  return '<h1 class="page-title">Dealer network</h1>' +
    '<p class="page-sub">Search every registered dealer\'s in-stock phones, request an urgent need, or catch stock adverts from other dealers.</p>' +
    '<div class="pill-tabs">' +
      '<div class="pill-tab '+(state.networkView==='search'?'active':'')+'" data-network-view="search">Search stock</div>' +
      '<div class="pill-tab '+(state.networkView==='broadcasts'?'active':'')+'" data-network-view="broadcasts">Broadcasts'+pillBadge(openBroadcastCount)+'</div>' +
      '<div class="pill-tab '+(state.networkView==='suppliers'?'active':'')+'" data-network-view="suppliers">My contacts</div>' +
    '</div>' +
    (state.networkView==='search' ? renderNetworkSearch() : '') +
    (state.networkView==='broadcasts' ? renderBroadcasts() : '') +
    (state.networkView==='suppliers' ? renderSuppliers() : '');
}

function uniqueNetworkDealers(){
  const seen = {}; const list = [];
  state.dealerNetwork.forEach(function(d){
    if(!seen[d.dealer_id]){ seen[d.dealer_id]=true; list.push({id:d.dealer_id, name:d.dealer_name}); }
  });
  return list.sort(function(a,b){ return String(a.name).localeCompare(String(b.name)); });
}

function renderDealerFilterDropdown(){
  const dealers = uniqueNetworkDealers();
  const q = state.dealerFilterQuery.toLowerCase();
  const selected = state.networkDealerFilter ? dealers.find(function(d){ return d.id===state.networkDealerFilter; }) : null;
  const filtered = q ? dealers.filter(function(d){ return String(d.name||'').toLowerCase().includes(q); }) : dealers;
  return '<div style="position:relative;max-width:280px;margin-bottom:12px;">' +
    '<input id="dealerFilterInput" autocomplete="off" placeholder="Filter by dealer…" value="'+escapeAttr(selected?selected.name:state.dealerFilterQuery)+'" '+(selected?'readonly':'')+' ' +
      'style="width:100%;background:var(--bg);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);padding:9px 30px 9px 12px;color:var(--text);font-family:var(--font-body);font-size:13px;outline:none;"/>' +
    (selected ? ('<button id="clearDealerFilterBtn" title="Clear dealer filter" style="position:absolute;right:6px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);background:none;border:none;color:var(--text-faint);cursor:pointer;font-size:17px;line-height:1;">×</button>') :
      '<span style="position:absolute;right:10px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);color:var(--text-faint);pointer-events:none;font-size:12px;">▾</span>') +
    (state.dealerFilterOpen && !selected ? (
      '<div style="position:absolute;top:calc(100% + 4px);left:0;right:0;background:var(--panel-2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);max-height:220px;overflow-y:auto;z-index:60;box-shadow:0 12px 28px rgba(0,0,0,.45);">' +
        (filtered.length ? filtered.map(function(d){ return '<div class="search-row" data-select-dealer-filter="'+d.id+'">'+
            '<span class="sr-main">'+escapeHtml(d.name)+(d.id===state.profile.id?' <span style="color:var(--text-faint);font-weight:400;">(you)</span>':'')+'</span>' +
          '</div>'; }).join('') :
          '<div style="padding:12px 14px;color:var(--text-faint);font-size:12.5px;">No dealers match</div>') +
      '</div>'
    ) : '') +
  '</div>';
}

function renderNetworkSearch(){
  const q = state.dealerSearchQuery.toLowerCase();
  const dealerFilterId = state.networkDealerFilter;
  const isFiltered = !!q || !!dealerFilterId;
  let list, showLoadMore = false, totalCount = 0;

  let base = dealerFilterId ? state.dealerNetwork.filter(function(d){ return d.dealer_id===dealerFilterId; }) : state.dealerNetwork;
  if(state.networkCategoryFilter !== 'All') base = base.filter(function(d){ return (d.item_type||'Phone') === state.networkCategoryFilter; });

  if(isFiltered){
    list = base.filter(function(d){ return !q || String(d.model||'').toLowerCase().includes(q) || String(d.brand||'').toLowerCase().includes(q); })
      .slice().sort(function(a,b){ return (Number(a.price)||0)-(Number(b.price)||0); });
  } else {
    const byId = {}; base.forEach(function(d){ byId[d.id] = d; });
    const ordered = state.networkOrder.map(function(id){ return byId[id]; }).filter(Boolean);
    totalCount = ordered.length;
    list = ordered.slice(0, state.networkVisibleCount);
    showLoadMore = ordered.length > state.networkVisibleCount;
  }

  const categoryPills = '<div class="pill-tabs" style="margin-bottom:12px;">' +
    ['All','Phone','Laptop'].map(function(c){ return '<div class="pill-tab '+(state.networkCategoryFilter===c?'active':'')+'" data-network-category-filter="'+c+'">'+(c==='All'?'All':(c==='Phone'?'📱 Phones':'💻 Laptops'))+'</div>'; }).join('') +
  '</div>';

  return '<div class="section"><div class="section-body">' +
      categoryPills +
      renderDealerFilterDropdown() +
      '<input id="dealerSearch" placeholder="e.g. S24 Ultra, iPhone 15, EliteBook…" value="'+escapeAttr(state.dealerSearchQuery)+'" ' +
      'style="width:100%;background:var(--bg);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);padding:10px 12px;color:var(--text);font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:13px;outline:none;margin-bottom:10px;"/>' +
      (!isFiltered && totalCount>0 ? ('<div style="font-size:11.5px;color:var(--text-faint);margin-bottom:14px;">Showing '+list.length+' of '+totalCount+' network listings, in random order — search above to find something specific.</div>') : '') +
      '<div class="table-scroll">' +
      (list.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Img</th><th>Model</th><th>Dealer</th><th>Price</th><th>Updated</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
        list.map(function(d,i){
          const isLaptop = (d.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
          const specLine = isLaptop
            ? ((d.brand?escapeHtml(d.brand)+' ':'')+escapeHtml(d.model)+(d.cpu?(' · '+escapeHtml(d.cpu)):'')+(d.ram?(' · '+escapeHtml(d.ram)):'')+(d.storage?(' · '+escapeHtml(d.storage)):''))
            : (escapeHtml(d.model)+(d.storage?(' · '+escapeHtml(d.storage)):'')+(d.color?(' · '+escapeHtml(d.color)):'')+(d.condition==='Used'?(' · '+d.battery+'% batt'):''));
          return '<tr data-view-network-item="'+d.id+'" style="cursor:pointer;">' +
          '<td>'+thumbHTML(d.image_url)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="strong">'+specLine+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(d.dealer_name)+(d.dealer_id===state.profile.id?' <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-faint)">(you)</span>':'')+'<br>'+reputationBadgeHTML(d.dealer_id)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono" style="color:'+(isFiltered && i===0?'var(--success)':'var(--text)')+'">'+naira(d.price)+(isFiltered && i===0?' <span style="font-size:10px">· lowest</span>':'')+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-faint)">'+new Date(d.updated_at).toLocaleDateString()+'</td>' +
          '<td><a class="linklike" href="tel:'+escapeAttr(d.dealer_phone)+'">'+escapeHtml(d.dealer_phone||'—')+'</a></td>' +
        '</tr>'; }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>') : ('<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No matches in the network yet. Try a request instead.</div></div>')) +
      '</div>' +
      (showLoadMore ? '<div style="text-align:center;margin-top:14px;"><button class="btn" id="networkLoadMoreBtn">Load 20 more</button></div>' : '') +
    '</div></div>';
}

function dealerName(id){
  if(id===state.profile.id) return 'You';
  const r = state.dealerReputation[id]; if(r && r.shop_name) return r.shop_name;
  const n = state.dealerNetwork.find(function(d){ return d.dealer_id===id; });
  return n ? n.dealer_name : 'A dealer';
}
function dealerPhone(id){
  const n = state.dealerNetwork.find(function(d){ return d.dealer_id===id; });
  return n ? n.dealer_phone : '';
}

function renderStockAdvertCard(b){
  const isMine = b.dealer_id === state.profile.id;
  const items = Array.isArray(b.items) ? b.items : (b.items ? (function(){ try{ return JSON.parse(b.items); }catch(e){ return []; } })() : []);
  const phone = dealerPhone(b.dealer_id);
  return '<div class="section">' +
    '<div class="section-head"><div><strong>'+ICONS.broadcast.replace('<svg ', '<svg style="width:13px;height:13px;vertical-align:-2px;margin-right:5px;color:var(--accent)" ')+
      (isMine ? 'Your stock advert' : escapeHtml(dealerName(b.dealer_id))+'\'s stock advert')+'</strong>' +
      '<div style="font-size:11.5px;color:var(--text-faint);margin-top:3px;">'+escapeHtml(b.date)+'</div></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;">'+badge(b.status)+
        (isMine && b.status==='Open'?('<button class="btn btn-sm" data-close-broadcast="'+b.id+'">Close</button>'):'') +
      '</div></div>' +
    '<div class="section-body">' +
      (b.message ? ('<div style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:13px;margin-bottom:12px;">'+escapeHtml(b.message)+'</div>') : '') +
      '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(150px,1fr));gap:10px;">' +
        items.map(function(it,idx){
          const isLaptop = (it.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
          const spec = isLaptop ? [it.cpu,it.ram,it.storage].filter(Boolean).join(' · ') : [it.storage,it.color].filter(Boolean).join(' ');
          return '<div data-view-stock-item="'+b.id+'" data-item-index="'+idx+'" style="background:var(--panel-2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:10px;cursor:pointer;">' +
          (it.image_url ? ('<img src="'+escapeAttr(it.image_url)+'" style="width:100%;height:84px;object-fit:cover;border-radius:6px;margin-bottom:6px;"/>') : '') +
          '<div class="strong" style="font-size:12.5px;">'+(isLaptop?'💻 ':'📱 ')+escapeHtml((isLaptop && it.brand ? it.brand+' ' : '')+it.model)+'</div>' +
          '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-faint);">'+escapeHtml(spec)+'</div>' +
          '<div class="mono" style="color:var(--accent);font-size:13px;margin-top:4px;">'+(it.price?naira(it.price):'—')+'</div>' +
        '</div>'; }).join('') +
      '</div>' +
      (!isMine && phone ? ('<div style="margin-top:14px;"><a class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" href="tel:'+escapeAttr(phone)+'">📞 Contact '+escapeHtml(dealerName(b.dealer_id))+'</a></div>') : '') +
    '</div></div>';
}

function renderBroadcasts(){
  const filter = state.networkBroadcastTypeFilter;
  const rows = state.broadcasts.slice()
    .filter(function(b){ return filter==='All' || (b.type||'Need')===filter; })
    .sort(function(a,b){ return new Date(b.created_at)-new Date(a.created_at); });

  const body = rows.map(function(b){
    if((b.type||'Need')==='Stock') return renderStockAdvertCard(b);
    const responses = state.broadcastResponses.filter(function(r){ return r.broadcast_id===b.id; }).sort(function(a,b2){ return (Number(a.price)||0)-(Number(b2.price)||0); });
    const isMine = b.dealer_id === state.profile.id;
    const canAccept = isMine && b.status==='Open';
    return '<div class="section">' +
      '<div class="section-head"><div><strong>'+escapeHtml(b.model)+'</strong> '+(b.storage?(' · '+escapeHtml(b.storage)):'')+' '+(b.color?(' · '+escapeHtml(b.color)):'')+(isMine?' <span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-faint)">(your request)</span>':'')+
      '<div style="font-size:11.5px;color:var(--text-faint);margin-top:3px;">'+escapeHtml(b.date)+' · '+escapeHtml(b.urgency)+'</div></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;">'+badge(b.status)+
        (isMine && b.status==='Open'?('<button class="btn btn-sm" data-close-broadcast="'+b.id+'">Close (no deal)</button>'):'') +
        (!isMine && b.status==='Open'?('<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" data-open-modal="respondBroadcast" data-id="'+b.id+'">Respond</button>'):'') +
      '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' +
        (responses.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Dealer</th><th>Reputation</th><th>Price</th><th>Qty</th><th>Contact</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
          responses.map(function(r,i){
            const accepted = b.accepted_response_id === r.id;
            return '<tr style="'+(accepted?'background:var(--success-dim);':'')+'"><td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(dealerName(r.dealer_id))+(i===0 && !b.accepted_response_id?' <span style="color:var(--success);font-size:10px">· best offer</span>':'')+'</td>' +
            '<td>'+reputationBadgeHTML(r.dealer_id, {compact:true})+'</td>' +
            '<td class="mono">'+naira(r.price)+'</td><td class="mono">'+escapeHtml(r.quantity)+'</td>' +
            '<td><a class="linklike" href="tel:'+escapeAttr(r.contact_phone)+'">'+escapeHtml(r.contact_phone)+'</a></td>' +
            '<td>'+(accepted ? '<span class="badge badge-stock">✓ Accepted</span>' : (canAccept ? '<button class="btn btn-sm btn-accent" data-accept-response="'+r.id+'" data-broadcast="'+b.id+'">Accept</button>' : ''))+'</td>' +
          '</tr>'; }).join('') +
        '</tbody></table>') : '<div class="empty" style="padding:20px;">No responses yet.</div>') +
      '</div></div>';
  }).join('');

  const openNeedCount = state.broadcasts.filter(function(b){ return b.status==='Open' && (b.type||'Need')==='Need'; }).length;
  const openStockCount = state.broadcasts.filter(function(b){ return b.status==='Open' && (b.type||'Need')==='Stock'; }).length;
  const pillCounts = { All: openNeedCount+openStockCount, Need: openNeedCount, Stock: openStockCount };

  return '<div class="sticky-subtabs" style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:10px;">' +
      '<div class="pill-tabs" style="margin:0;">' +
        ['All','Need','Stock'].map(function(f){ return '<div class="pill-tab '+(filter===f?'active':'')+'" data-broadcast-type-filter="'+f+'">'+(f==='All'?'All':(f==='Need'?'Need it':'For sale'))+pillBadge(pillCounts[f])+'</div>'; }).join('') +
      '</div>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="newBroadcast">'+ICONS.plus+' New request</button>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div style="margin-top:14px;">' +
    (body || ('<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No broadcasts yet. Send one when you need a phone urgently, or advertise stock straight from the Inventory tab.</div></div>')) +
    '</div>';
}

function renderSuppliers(){
  const rows = state.suppliers;
  return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:flex-end;margin-bottom:14px;"><button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="addSupplier">'+ICONS.plus+' Add contact</button></div>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' +
      (rows.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Name</th><th>Phone</th><th>Location</th><th>Supplies</th><th>Owed</th><th></th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
        rows.map(function(s){ return '<tr>' +
          '<td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(s.name)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+escapeHtml(s.phone)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(s.location)+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(s.supplies)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono" style="color:'+(Number(s.owed)>0?'var(--danger)':'var(--text-dim)')+'">'+naira(s.owed)+'</td>' +
          '<td style="display:flex;gap:6px;">' +
            '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-open-modal="editSupplier" data-id="'+s.id+'">Edit</button>' +
            '<button class="btn btn-sm btn-danger" data-delete-supplier="'+s.id+'">Delete</button>' +
            '<button class="btn btn-sm" data-view-supplier-stock="'+s.id+'">View stock</button>' +
          '</td>' +
        '</tr>'; }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>') : ('<div class="empty">'+ICONS.empty+'<div>No suppliers added yet.</div></div>')) +
    '</div></div>';
}

function renderAdmin(){
  const dealers = state.adminDealers;
  const invByDealer = {}; state.adminInventory.forEach(function(p){ (invByDealer[p.dealer_id]=invByDealer[p.dealer_id]||[]).push(p); });
  const salesByDealer = {}; state.adminSales.forEach(function(s){ (salesByDealer[s.dealer_id]=salesByDealer[s.dealer_id]||[]).push(s); });
  const totalDealers = dealers.length;
  const totalPhones = state.adminInventory.length;
  const totalRevenue = state.adminSales.reduce(function(a,s){ return a+(Number(s.sale_price)||0); },0);
  return '<h1 class="page-title">Platform overview</h1>' +
    '<p class="page-sub">Visible only to admin accounts — every dealer\'s activity, across the whole network.</p>' +
    '<div class="kpi-grid">' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Registered dealers</div><div class="kpi-value">'+totalDealers+'</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Total phones tracked</div><div class="kpi-value">'+totalPhones+'</div></div>' +
      '<div class="kpi"><div class="kpi-label">Total platform revenue</div><div class="kpi-value accent">'+naira(totalRevenue)+'</div></div>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="section"><div class="section-head"><h3>Dealers</h3></div><div class="section-body table-scroll" style="padding:0;">' +
      '<table><thead><tr><th>Shop</th><th>Location</th><th>Phone</th><th>Phones tracked</th><th>Sales</th><th>Revenue</th><th>Joined</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
      dealers.map(function(d){
        const inv = invByDealer[d.id]||[]; const sal = salesByDealer[d.id]||[];
        const rev = sal.reduce(function(a,s){ return a+(Number(s.sale_price)||0); },0);
        return '<tr><td class="strong">'+escapeHtml(d.shop_name)+(d.is_admin?' <span class="badge badge-admin">admin</span>':'')+'</td>' +
          '<td>'+escapeHtml(d.location)+'</td><td class="mono">'+escapeHtml(d.phone)+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+inv.length+'</td><td class="mono">'+sal.length+'</td>' +
          '<td class="mono">'+naira(rev)+'</td><td class="mono" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-faint)">'+new Date(d.created_at).toLocaleDateString()+'</td></tr>';
      }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>' +
    '</div></div>';
}

/* ---------- Modals ---------- */
function renderModal(){
  const m = state.modal;
  if(m.name==='addPhone' || m.name==='editPhone') return renderPhoneModal(m);
  if(m.name==='addLaptop' || m.name==='editLaptop') return renderLaptopModal(m);
  if(m.name==='logSale') return renderSaleModal();
  if(m.name==='addSupplier' || m.name==='editSupplier') return renderSupplierModal(m);
  if(m.name==='newBroadcast') return renderBroadcastModal();
  if(m.name==='respondBroadcast') return renderRespondModal(m);
  if(m.name==='bulkImport') return renderBulkImportModal();
  if(m.name==='notifSettings') return renderNotifModal();
  if(m.name==='themeSettings') return renderThemeModal();
  if(m.name==='addConsignment' || m.name==='editConsignment') return renderConsignmentModal(m);
  if(m.name==='viewConsignment') return renderConsignmentDetailModal(m);
  if(m.name==='logConsignmentPayment') return renderConsignmentPaymentModal(m);
  if(m.name==='sendBroadcastAdvert') return renderBroadcastComposerModal(m);
  if(m.name==='viewStockItem') return renderStockItemModal(m);
  if(m.name==='viewNetworkItem') return renderNetworkItemModal(m);
  return '';
}

function renderNetworkItemModal(m){
  const d = state.dealerNetwork.find(function(x){ return x.id === m.payload.id; });
  if(!d) return '';
  const isMine = d.dealer_id === state.profile.id;
  const isLaptop = (d.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
  const row = function(k,v){ return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);font-size:13.5px;"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);">'+k+'</span><span class="strong">'+v+'</span></div>'; };
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1" style="max-width:440px;">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>'+(isLaptop && d.brand ? escapeHtml(d.brand)+' ' : '')+escapeHtml(d.model)+'</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      renderImageGallery(imagesFor(d), state.galleryIndex) +
      (isLaptop ? (
        row('Processor', escapeHtml(d.cpu||'—')) +
        row('RAM', escapeHtml(d.ram||'—')) +
        row('Storage', escapeHtml(d.storage||'—')) +
        row('Screen', escapeHtml(d.screen_size||'—')) +
        (d.gpu ? row('Graphics', escapeHtml(d.gpu)) : '')
      ) : (
        row('Storage', escapeHtml(d.storage||'—'))
      )) +
      row('Color', escapeHtml(d.color||'—')) +
      row('Condition', escapeHtml(d.condition||'—')+(d.condition==='Used' && d.battery!=null?(' · '+d.battery+'% battery'):'')) +
      row('Price', '<span style="color:var(--accent);font-size:16px;">'+naira(d.price)+'</span>') +
      row('Dealer', escapeHtml(d.dealer_name)+(isMine?' <span style="color:var(--text-faint);">(you)</span>':'')) +
      row('Last updated', new Date(d.updated_at).toLocaleDateString()) +
    '</div>' +
    (!isMine && d.dealer_phone ? ('<div class="modal-foot"><a class="btn btn-accent" href="tel:'+escapeAttr(d.dealer_phone)+'" style="width:100%;justify-content:center;">📞 Contact '+escapeHtml(d.dealer_name)+'</a></div>') : '') +
  '</div></div>';
}

function renderStockItemModal(m){
  const b = state.broadcasts.find(function(x){ return x.id === m.payload.broadcastId; });
  if(!b) return '';
  const items = Array.isArray(b.items) ? b.items : (b.items ? (function(){ try{ return JSON.parse(b.items); }catch(e){ return []; } })() : []);
  const it = items[m.payload.itemIndex];
  if(!it) return '';
  const isMine = b.dealer_id === state.profile.id;
  const phone = dealerPhone(b.dealer_id);
  const isLaptop = (it.item_type||'Phone')==='Laptop';
  const row = function(k,v){ return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);font-size:13.5px;"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);">'+k+'</span><span class="strong">'+v+'</span></div>'; };
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1" style="max-width:440px;">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>'+(isLaptop && it.brand ? escapeHtml(it.brand)+' ' : '')+escapeHtml(it.model)+'</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      renderImageGallery(imagesFor(it), state.galleryIndex) +
      (isLaptop ? (
        row('Processor', escapeHtml(it.cpu||'—')) +
        row('RAM', escapeHtml(it.ram||'—')) +
        row('Storage', escapeHtml(it.storage||'—')) +
        row('Screen', escapeHtml(it.screen_size||'—')) +
        (it.gpu ? row('Graphics', escapeHtml(it.gpu)) : '')
      ) : row('Storage', escapeHtml(it.storage||'—'))) +
      row('Color', escapeHtml(it.color||'—')) +
      row('Condition', escapeHtml(it.condition||'—')) +
      row('Price', '<span style="color:var(--accent);font-size:16px;">'+(it.price?naira(it.price):'—')+'</span>') +
      (!isMine ? ('<div style="margin-top:14px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text-faint);">Listed by '+escapeHtml(dealerName(b.dealer_id))+'</div>') : '') +
    '</div>' +
    (!isMine && phone ? ('<div class="modal-foot"><a class="btn btn-accent" href="tel:'+escapeAttr(phone)+'" style="width:100%;justify-content:center;">📞 Contact '+escapeHtml(dealerName(b.dealer_id))+'</a></div>') : '') +
  '</div></div>';
}

function renderNotifModal(){
  const status = state.pushStatus;
  const statusLabel = {unsupported:'Not supported in this browser', off:'Off', prompting:'Waiting for permission…', on:'On for this device', denied:'Blocked in browser settings'}[status] || status;
  const iosNotStandalone = isIOSDevice() && !isStandaloneDisplay();
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1" style="max-width:460px;">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>Notifications</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      (iosNotStandalone ? ('<div class="notif-row"><div class="n-sub" style="color:var(--accent)">On iPhone/iPad, notifications only work once PhoneHub is added to your Home Screen and opened from that icon (not from Safari). Tap the Share button, then "Add to Home Screen", then reopen the app from the icon. Requires iOS 16.4 or later.</div></div>') : '') +
      '<div class="notif-row"><div><div class="n-label">Push notifications on this device</div>' +
        '<div class="n-sub">Status: '+escapeHtml(statusLabel)+'</div></div>' +
        (status==='on' ? '<button class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" id="disablePushBtn">Turn off</button>' :
          status==='denied' ? '' :
          '<button class="btn btn-accent btn-sm" id="enablePushBtn" '+(status==='prompting'?'disabled':'')+'>Enable</button>') +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="notif-row"><div class="n-sub">You\'ll be alerted for: new customer requests, dealer network broadcasts and responses, warranty phones expiring within 2 days, and phones down to their last unit. Alerts arrive even if this app isn\'t open, as long as your phone has data/wifi.</div></div>' +
