function renderConsignmentDetailModal(m){
  const c = state.consignments.find(function(x){ return x.id === m.payload.id; });
  if(!c) return '';
  const balance = consignmentBalance(c);
  const payments = (state.consignmentPayments||[]).filter(function(p){ return p.consignment_id===c.id; })
    .sort(function(a,b){ return new Date(b.created_at)-new Date(a.created_at); });
  const canSettle = c.status!=='Settled' && c.status!=='Returned';
  const row = function(k,v){ return '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);font-size:13.5px;"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);">'+k+'</span><span class="strong">'+v+'</span></div>'; };
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1" style="max-width:520px;">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>'+escapeHtml(c.contact_name)+' — '+escapeHtml(c.model)+'</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      row('Phone', escapeHtml(c.model)+(c.storage?(' · '+escapeHtml(c.storage)):'')+(c.color?(' · '+escapeHtml(c.color)):'')) +
      (c.imei ? row('IMEI', escapeHtml(c.imei)) : '') +
      row('Colleague', escapeHtml(c.contact_name)+(c.contact_phone?(' · <a class="linklike" href="tel:'+escapeAttr(c.contact_phone)+'">'+escapeHtml(c.contact_phone)+'</a>'):'')) +
      row('Quantity', c.quantity||1) +
      row('Unit price', naira(c.unit_price)) +
      row('Total owed', naira((Number(c.unit_price)||0)*(Number(c.quantity)||1))) +
      row('Amount paid', naira(c.amount_paid)) +
      row('Balance', '<span style="color:'+(balance>0?'var(--danger)':'var(--success)')+'">'+naira(balance)+'</span>') +
      row('Status', badge(c.status)) +
      row('Date given', escapeHtml(c.date_given)) +
      (c.due_date ? row('Due date', escapeHtml(c.due_date)) : '') +
      (c.notes ? row('Notes', escapeHtml(c.notes)) : '') +
      '<div style="margin-top:18px;"><h4 style="font-family:var(--font-display);font-size:13.5px;margin:0 0 10px;color:var(--text);">Payment log</h4>' +
      (payments.length ? ('<table><thead><tr><th>Date</th><th>Amount</th><th>Note</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
        payments.map(function(p){ return '<tr><td class="mono" style="font-size:11.5px;">'+new Date(p.created_at).toLocaleString()+'</td><td class="mono">'+naira(p.amount)+'</td><td style="color:var(--text-faint);font-size:12px;">'+escapeHtml(p.note||'—')+'</td></tr>'; }).join('') +
      '</tbody></table>') : '<div class="empty" style="padding:16px;">No payments logged yet.</div>') +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="modal-foot">' +
      (canSettle ? ('<button class="btn btn-danger" data-mark-consignment="Returned" data-id="'+c.id+'">Mark returned</button>') : '') +
      '<button class="btn" data-close-modal="1">Close</button>' +
      (canSettle ? ('<button class="btn btn-accent" data-open-modal="logConsignmentPayment" data-id="'+c.id+'">Log payment</button>') : '') +
    '</div></div></div>';
}

function renderConsignmentPaymentModal(m){
  const c = state.consignments.find(function(x){ return x.id === m.payload.id; });
  if(!c) return '';
  const balance = consignmentBalance(c);
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>Log payment — '+escapeHtml(c.contact_name)+'</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      '<p style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:13px;margin-top:0;">'+escapeHtml(c.model)+' — currently owes <strong style="color:var(--accent)">'+naira(balance)+'</strong>.</p>' +
      '<div class="field mono"><label>Amount received now (₦)</label><input type="number" id="cnp-amount" value=""/></div>' +
      '<div class="field"><label>Note (optional)</label><input id="cnp-note" placeholder="e.g. Cash handed at shop"/></div>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="modal-foot">' +
      '<button class="btn btn-danger" data-mark-consignment="Returned" data-id="'+c.id+'">Mark returned (no sale)</button>' +
      '<button class="btn" data-close-modal="1">Cancel</button>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-accent" data-log-consignment-payment="'+c.id+'">Log payment</button>' +
    '</div></div></div>';
}

function defaultBroadcastMessage(items){
  const shopName = state.profile ? state.profile.shop_name : 'our shop';
  const lines = items.map(function(p){ return '• '+itemLabel(p)+' — '+(p.price?naira(p.price):'price on request'); });
  return 'New stock available at '+shopName+':\n\n'+lines.join('\n')+'\n\nReply or call to grab it!';
}

function renderBroadcastComposerModal(m){
  const ids = state.broadcastComposer.ids || [];
  const items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return ids.indexOf(p.id)>-1; });
  if(!items.length) return '';
  const target = state.broadcastComposer.target;
  const shopName = state.profile ? state.profile.shop_name : '';
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1" style="max-width:640px;">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>'+ICONS.broadcast.replace('<svg ', '<svg style="width:16px;height:16px;vertical-align:-3px;margin-right:6px;" ')+'Send as broadcast</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:8px;margin-bottom:16px;">' +
        items.map(function(p){ return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;background:var(--panel-2);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:20px;padding:5px 12px 5px 5px;">'+
          thumbHTML(p.image_url)+'<span style="font-size:12px;">'+escapeHtml(itemLabel(p))+' — '+(p.price?naira(p.price):'no price')+'</span></div>'; }).join('') +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="pill-tabs" style="margin-bottom:16px;">' +
        '<div class="pill-tab '+(target==='network'?'active':'')+'" data-broadcast-target="network">📡 Open market (all dealers)</div>' +
        '<div class="pill-tab '+(target==='contacts'?'active':'')+'" data-broadcast-target="contacts">💬 My saved contacts</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      (target==='network' ? (
        '<p style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:13px;">Every registered dealer on the network will instantly see these phones as a stock advert — no WhatsApp group needed.</p>' +
        '<div class="field full"><label>Note (optional)</label><textarea id="bc-message" rows="3" placeholder="e.g. Fresh UK arrivals, negotiable">'+escapeHtml(state.broadcastComposer.message)+'</textarea></div>'
      ) : (
        '<p style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:13px;">Pick which saved contacts to notify. Since they may not be on PhoneHub yet, this opens a pre-filled WhatsApp message straight to their saved number.</p>' +
        (state.suppliers.length ? ('<div style="max-height:160px;overflow-y:auto;border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:var(--radius-sm);padding:8px 12px;margin-bottom:14px;">' +
          state.suppliers.map(function(s){ return '<label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;padding:6px 0;font-size:13px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);">' +
            '<input type="checkbox" data-broadcast-contact="'+s.id+'" '+(state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.indexOf(s.id)>-1?'checked':'')+'/>' +
            '<span class="strong">'+escapeHtml(s.name)+'</span><span class="mono" style="color:var(--text-faint);font-size:11px;">'+escapeHtml(s.phone||'no phone saved')+'</span>' +
          '</label>'; }).join('') +
        '</div>') : '<div class="empty">No saved contacts yet — add one under Network → My contacts.</div>') +
        '<div class="field full"><label>Message</label><textarea id="bc-message" rows="5" style="font-size:12.5px;">'+escapeHtml(state.broadcastComposer.message)+'</textarea></div>' +
        (state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.length ? ('<div style="margin-top:6px;"><div style="font-size:11.5px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-bottom:8px;">Tap each contact to open their WhatsApp chat with the message above:</div>' +
          '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px;">' +
          state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.map(function(id){
            const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
            if(!s) return '';
            const digits = (s.phone||'').replace(/[^0-9+]/g,'');
            const waText = encodeURIComponent(state.broadcastComposer.message || defaultBroadcastMessage(items));
            return '<a class="btn btn-sm" target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://wa.me/'+escapeAttr(digits)+'?text='+waText+'">💬 Open WhatsApp — '+escapeHtml(s.name)+'</a>';
          }).join('') +
          '</div></div>') : '')
      )) +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="modal-foot">' +
      '<button class="btn" data-close-modal="1">Close</button>' +
      (target==='network' ? '<button class="btn btn-accent" id="sendNetworkBroadcastBtn">Send to network</button>' : '<button class="btn btn-accent" id="logContactBroadcastBtn">Save to broadcast history</button>') +
    '</div></div></div>';
}

function renderBroadcastModal(){
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>Broadcast an urgent need</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body">' +
      '<p style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:13px;margin-top:0;">Every registered dealer will see this instantly.</p>' +
      '<div class="form-grid">' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Phone model</label><input id="b-model" placeholder="iPhone 15 Pro Max"/></div>' +
        '<div class="field"><label>Storage / color</label><input id="b-variant" placeholder="256GB, Natural Titanium"/></div>' +
        '<div class="field full"><label>Urgency / note</label><input id="b-urgency" placeholder="Need today — customer waiting in shop"/></div>' +
      '</div>' +
    '</div>' +
    '<div class="modal-foot"><button class="btn" data-close-modal="1">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-accent" data-save-broadcast="1">Send broadcast</button></div>' +
  '</div></div>';
}

function renderRespondModal(m){
  const b = state.broadcasts.find(function(x){ return x.id===m.payload.id; });
  if(!b) return '';
  return '<div class="overlay" data-close-overlay="1"><div class="modal" data-stop="1">' +
    '<div class="modal-head"><h3>Respond: '+escapeHtml(b.model)+'</h3><button class="close-x" data-close-modal="1">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body"><div class="form-grid">' +
      '<div class="field mono"><label>Your price (₦)</label><input type="number" id="rb-price"/></div>' +
      '<div class="field"><label>Quantity available</label><input type="number" id="rb-qty" value="1"/></div>' +
      '<div class="field full"><label>Contact phone</label><input id="rb-phone" value="'+escapeAttr(state.profile.phone)+'"/></div>' +
    '</div></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-foot"><button class="btn" data-close-modal="1">Cancel</button><button class="btn btn-accent" data-save-response="'+b.id+'">Send response</button></div>' +
  '</div></div>';
}

/* ---------- event wiring ---------- */
function attachHandlers(){
  const app = document.getElementById('app');
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-tab]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.inventorySupplierFilter = null; state.supplierFilterName = '';
    state.mobileMenuOpen = false;
    setTab(el.getAttribute('data-tab'));
  }); });
  const hamburgerBtn = document.getElementById('hamburgerBtn');
  if(hamburgerBtn) hamburgerBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.mobileMenuOpen = true; render(); });
  const railCloseBtn = document.getElementById('railCloseBtn');
  if(railCloseBtn) railCloseBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.mobileMenuOpen = false; render(); });
  const railBackdrop = document.getElementById('railBackdrop');
  if(railBackdrop) railBackdrop.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.mobileMenuOpen = false; render(); });
  const logoutBtn = document.getElementById('logoutBtn');
  if(logoutBtn) logoutBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){ await sb.auth.signOut(); state.stage='auth'; state.profile=null; render(); });

  const notifBellBtn = document.getElementById('notifBellBtn');
  if(notifBellBtn) notifBellBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal('notifSettings'); });

  const themeSettingsBtn = document.getElementById('themeSettingsBtn');
  if(themeSettingsBtn) themeSettingsBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal('themeSettings'); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-set-theme]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ setTheme(el.getAttribute('data-set-theme')); }); });
  
  const enablePushInline = document.getElementById('enablePushInline');
  if(enablePushInline) enablePushInline.addEventListener('click', enablePush);
  const enablePushBtn = document.getElementById('enablePushBtn');
  if(enablePushBtn) enablePushBtn.addEventListener('click', enablePush);
  const disablePushBtn = document.getElementById('disablePushBtn');
  if(disablePushBtn) disablePushBtn.addEventListener('click', disablePush);

  const gs = document.getElementById('globalSearch');
  if(gs){
    gs.addEventListener('input', function(e){
      state.searchQuery = e.target.value; render();
      const el = document.getElementById('globalSearch'); el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.searchQuery.length;
    });
  }
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-open-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.searchQuery='';
    const type = el.getAttribute('data-open-item-type')==='Laptop' ? 'editLaptop' : 'editPhone';
    openModal(type,{id:el.getAttribute('data-open-phone')});
  }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-open-modal]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ openModal(el.getAttribute('data-open-modal'), {id:el.getAttribute('data-id')}); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-modal]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', closeModal); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-overlay]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', closeModal); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-stop]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){ e.stopPropagation(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-network-view]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.networkView = el.getAttribute('data-network-view'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-inventory-item-tab]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.inventoryItemTab = el.getAttribute('data-inventory-item-tab');
    state.selectedInventoryIds = [];
    state.inventorySupplierFilter = null; state.supplierFilterName = '';
    render();
  }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-type-filter]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.networkBroadcastTypeFilter = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-type-filter'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-network-category-filter]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.networkCategoryFilter = el.getAttribute('data-network-category-filter'); render(); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-toggle-status]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ toggleStatus(el.getAttribute('data-toggle-status')); }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-stock-item]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    openModal('viewStockItem', { broadcastId: el.getAttribute('data-view-stock-item'), itemIndex: Number(el.getAttribute('data-item-index')) });
  }); });

  /* ---- Image gallery navigation (network item / stock item detail modals) ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-gallery-prev]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    e.stopPropagation();
    const total = Number(el.getAttribute('data-gallery-total'))||1;
    state.galleryIndex = ((state.galleryIndex||0) - 1 + total) % total;
    render();
  }); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-gallery-next]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    e.stopPropagation();
    const total = Number(el.getAttribute('data-gallery-total'))||1;
    state.galleryIndex = ((state.galleryIndex||0) + 1) % total;
    render();
  }); });
  const galleryWrap = document.getElementById('galleryWrap');
  if(galleryWrap){
    let touchStartX = null;
    galleryWrap.addEventListener('touchstart', function(e){ touchStartX = e.touches[0].clientX; }, {passive:true});
    galleryWrap.addEventListener('touchend', function(e){
      if(touchStartX==null) return;
      const dx = e.changedTouches[0].clientX - touchStartX;
      const total = Number(galleryWrap.getAttribute('data-gallery-total'))||1;
      if(Math.abs(dx) > 40 && total>1){
        state.galleryIndex = dx<0 ? ((state.galleryIndex||0)+1)%total : ((state.galleryIndex||0)-1+total)%total;
        render();
      }
      touchStartX = null;
    });
  }

  /* ---- "Owed to you" row click -> detail dialog ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    if(e.target.closest('button')) return;
    openModal('viewConsignment', { id: el.getAttribute('data-view-consignment') });
  }); });

  /* ---- Inventory selection + "send as broadcast" ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-select-inventory]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-select-inventory');
    const idx = state.selectedInventoryIds.indexOf(id);
    if(el.checked && idx===-1) state.selectedInventoryIds.push(id);
    else if(!el.checked && idx>-1) state.selectedInventoryIds.splice(idx,1);
    render();
  }); });
  const clearSelectionBtn = document.getElementById('clearSelectionBtn');
  if(clearSelectionBtn) clearSelectionBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.selectedInventoryIds = []; render(); });
  const selectAllInStockBtn = document.getElementById('selectAllInStockBtn');
  if(selectAllInStockBtn) selectAllInStockBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.selectedInventoryIds = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return p.status==='In Stock'; }).map(function(p){ return p.id; });
    render();
  });
  const broadcastSelectedBtn = document.getElementById('broadcastSelectedBtn');
  if(broadcastSelectedBtn) broadcastSelectedBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ openBroadcastComposer(state.selectedInventoryIds.slice()); });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-single]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){ openBroadcastComposer([el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-single')]); }); });

  /* ---- Broadcast composer (send stock as a broadcast) ---- */
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-target]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.broadcastComposer.target = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-target'); render();
  }); });
  const bcMessage = document.getElementById('bc-message');
  if(bcMessage) bcMessage.addEventListener('input', function(e){
    state.broadcastComposer.message = e.target.value; render();
    const el = document.getElementById('bc-message'); if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.broadcastComposer.message.length; }
  });
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-broadcast-contact]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast-contact');
    const idx = state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.indexOf(id);
    if(el.checked && idx===-1) state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.push(id);
    else if(!el.checked && idx>-1) state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds.splice(idx,1);
    render();
  }); });
  const sendNetworkBroadcastBtn = document.getElementById('sendNetworkBroadcastBtn');
  if(sendNetworkBroadcastBtn) sendNetworkBroadcastBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const ids = state.broadcastComposer.ids;
    const items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return ids.indexOf(p.id)>-1; });
    if(!items.length){ showToast('Nothing to broadcast', true); return; }
    const itemsPayload = items.map(function(p){ return {
      inventory_id:p.id, item_type:p.item_type||'Phone', model:p.model, brand:p.brand, storage:p.storage, color:p.color,
      condition:p.condition, price:p.price, cpu:p.cpu, ram:p.ram, screen_size:p.screen_size, gpu:p.gpu,
      image_url:p.image_url, image_urls: imagesFor(p)
    }; });
    const data = {
      dealer_id: state.profile.id, type:'Stock', status:'Open',
      model: items.length===1 ? items[0].model : (items.length+' items'),
      items: itemsPayload, message: state.broadcastComposer.message || null
    };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      state.selectedInventoryIds = []; state.broadcastComposer = {ids:[], target:'network', message:'', selectedContactIds:[]};
      closeModal(); showToast('Stock advert sent to the network');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Broadcast failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  });
  const logContactBroadcastBtn = document.getElementById('logContactBroadcastBtn');
  if(logContactBroadcastBtn) logContactBroadcastBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const ids = state.broadcastComposer.ids;
    const items = state.inventory.filter(function(p){ return ids.indexOf(p.id)>-1; });
    const contactIds = state.broadcastComposer.selectedContactIds;
    if(!contactIds.length){ showToast('Select at least one saved contact', true); return; }
    const names = contactIds.map(function(id){ const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; }); return s?s.name:''; }).filter(Boolean);
    const itemsPayload = items.map(function(p){ return {
      inventory_id:p.id, item_type:p.item_type||'Phone', model:p.model, brand:p.brand, storage:p.storage, color:p.color,
      condition:p.condition, price:p.price, cpu:p.cpu, ram:p.ram, screen_size:p.screen_size, gpu:p.gpu,
      image_url:p.image_url, image_urls: imagesFor(p)
    }; });
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('stock_broadcast_log').insert({
        dealer_id: state.profile.id, contact_names: names.join(', '), items: itemsPayload, message: state.broadcastComposer.message || null
      });
      if(error) throw error;
      showToast('Saved — tap each contact above to open WhatsApp with the message');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Could not save: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  });

  const dealerSearch = document.getElementById('dealerSearch');
  if(dealerSearch) dealerSearch.addEventListener('input', function(e){
    state.dealerSearchQuery = e.target.value; render();
    const el = document.getElementById('dealerSearch'); if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.dealerSearchQuery.length; }
  });

  const dealerFilterInput = document.getElementById('dealerFilterInput');
  if(dealerFilterInput){
    dealerFilterInput.addEventListener('focus', function(){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
      if(!state.dealerFilterOpen){
        state.dealerFilterOpen = true; render();
        const el = document.getElementById('dealerFilterInput');
        if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = el.value.length; }
      }
    });
    dealerFilterInput.addEventListener('input', function(e){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
      state.dealerFilterQuery = e.target.value; state.dealerFilterOpen = true; render();
      const el = document.getElementById('dealerFilterInput'); if(el){ el.focus(); el.selectionStart = el.selectionEnd = state.dealerFilterQuery.length; }
    });
    dealerFilterInput.addEventListener('blur', function(){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer) clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer);
      dealerFilterBlurTimer = setTimeout(function(){ dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; state.dealerFilterOpen = false; render(); }, 150);
    });
  }
  app.querySelectorAll('[data-select-dealer-filter]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e){ e.preventDefault(); });
    el.addEventListener('click', function(){
      if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
      state.networkDealerFilter = el.getAttribute('data-select-dealer-filter');
      state.dealerFilterQuery = ''; state.dealerFilterOpen = false; render();
    });
  });
  const clearDealerFilterBtn = document.getElementById('clearDealerFilterBtn');
  if(clearDealerFilterBtn) clearDealerFilterBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    if(dealerFilterBlurTimer){ clearTimeout(dealerFilterBlurTimer); dealerFilterBlurTimer = null; }
    state.networkDealerFilter = null; state.dealerFilterQuery = ''; render();
  });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-network-item]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    if(e.target.closest('a')) return;
    openModal('viewNetworkItem', { id: el.getAttribute('data-view-network-item') });
  }); });

  const networkLoadMoreBtn = document.getElementById('networkLoadMoreBtn');
  if(networkLoadMoreBtn) networkLoadMoreBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.networkVisibleCount += 20; render();
  });

  const fSupplierId = document.getElementById('f-supplier-id');
  if(fSupplierId) fSupplierId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === fSupplierId.value; });
    const fSupplier = document.getElementById('f-supplier');
    if(s && fSupplier) fSupplier.value = s.name;
  });
  const lSupplierId = document.getElementById('l-supplier-id');
  if(lSupplierId) lSupplierId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === lSupplierId.value; });
    const lSupplier = document.getElementById('l-supplier');
    if(s && lSupplier) lSupplier.value = s.name;
  });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-remove-existing-image]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    const url = el.getAttribute('data-remove-existing-image');
    state.photoModalRemovedUrls = state.photoModalRemovedUrls || [];
    state.photoModalRemovedUrls.push(url);
    render();
  }); });
  function wirePhotoPreview(inputId){
    const input = document.getElementById(inputId);
    if(!input) return;
    input.addEventListener('change', function(){
      const preview = document.getElementById('new-photo-preview');
      if(!preview) return;
      preview.innerHTML = '';
      Array.from(input.files||[]).forEach(function(file){
        const img = document.createElement('img');
        img.className = 'photo-preview'; img.style.width='72px'; img.style.height='72px';
        img.src = URL.createObjectURL(file);
        preview.appendChild(img);
      });
    });
  }
  wirePhotoPreview('f-images');
  wirePhotoPreview('l-images');

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-phone');
    const data = {
      item_type: 'Phone',
      imei: val('f-imei')||null, imei2: val('f-imei2')||null, model: val('f-model'), storage: val('f-storage'),
      color: val('f-color'), condition: val('f-condition'), battery: Number(val('f-battery')),
      supplier: val('f-supplier'), supplier_id: val('f-supplier-id')||null, purchase_date: todayISO(), cost: Number(val('f-cost')), price: Number(val('f-price')),
      status: val('f-status'), shelf: val('f-shelf'), notes: val('f-notes')
    };
    if(!data.model){ showToast('Phone model is required', true); return; }
    const existingPhone = id ? state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; }) : null;
    const existingImages = imagesFor(existingPhone);
    const removed = state.photoModalRemovedUrls || [];
    let keptImages = existingImages.filter(function(u){ return removed.indexOf(u)===-1; });
    const fImagesEl = document.getElementById('f-images');
    const newFiles = fImagesEl && fImagesEl.files ? Array.from(fImagesEl.files) : [];
    try{
      if(newFiles.length){
        showToast('Uploading '+newFiles.length+' photo'+(newFiles.length===1?'':'s')+'…');
        for(let i=0;i<newFiles.length;i++){
          const url = await uploadPhoneImage(newFiles[i]);
          keptImages.push(url);
        }
      }
      data.image_urls = keptImages;
      data.image_url = keptImages.length ? keptImages[0] : null;
      if(id){ const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').update(data).eq('id', id); if(error) throw error; }
      else{ data.dealer_id = state.profile.id; const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').insert(data); if(error) throw error; }
      await refreshAll();
      state.photoModalRemovedUrls = [];
      closeModal(); showToast(id?'Phone updated':'Phone added to inventory');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-laptop]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-laptop');
    const data = {
      item_type: 'Laptop',
      brand: val('l-brand')||null, model: val('l-model'), cpu: val('l-cpu')||null, ram: val('l-ram')||null,
      storage: val('l-storage'), screen_size: val('l-screen')||null, gpu: val('l-gpu')||null,
      color: val('l-color'), condition: val('l-condition'), battery: val('l-battery')?Number(val('l-battery')):null,
      supplier: val('l-supplier'), supplier_id: val('l-supplier-id')||null, purchase_date: todayISO(), cost: Number(val('l-cost')), price: Number(val('l-price')),
      status: val('l-status'), shelf: val('l-shelf'), notes: val('l-notes')
    };
    if(!data.model){ showToast('Laptop model is required', true); return; }
    const existingLaptop = id ? state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; }) : null;
    const existingImages = imagesFor(existingLaptop);
    const removed = state.photoModalRemovedUrls || [];
    let keptImages = existingImages.filter(function(u){ return removed.indexOf(u)===-1; });
    const lImagesEl = document.getElementById('l-images');
    const newFiles = lImagesEl && lImagesEl.files ? Array.from(lImagesEl.files) : [];
    try{
      if(newFiles.length){
        showToast('Uploading '+newFiles.length+' photo'+(newFiles.length===1?'':'s')+'…');
        for(let i=0;i<newFiles.length;i++){
          const url = await uploadPhoneImage(newFiles[i]);
          keptImages.push(url);
        }
      }
      data.image_urls = keptImages;
      data.image_url = keptImages.length ? keptImages[0] : null;
      if(id){ const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').update(data).eq('id', id); if(error) throw error; }
      else{ data.dealer_id = state.profile.id; const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').insert(data); if(error) throw error; }
      await refreshAll();
      state.photoModalRemovedUrls = [];
      closeModal(); showToast(id?'Laptop updated':'Laptop added to inventory');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-delete-phone]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-delete-phone');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').delete().eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Phone removed');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Delete failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-sale]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const inventoryId = val('s-inventory-id');
    if(!inventoryId){ showToast('Select a phone to sell', true); return; }
    const price = Number(val('s-price'));
    if(!price){ showToast('Enter a sale price', true); return; }
    try{
      const { data, error } = await sb.rpc('sell_phone', {
        p_inventory_id: inventoryId, p_sale_price: price, p_customer_name: val('s-name'), p_customer_phone: val('s-phone'),
        p_payment_method: val('s-payment'), p_staff: val('s-staff'), p_warranty_days: Number(val('s-warranty'))||0,
        p_accessories: val('s-accessories'), p_notes: '',
        p_imei: val('s-imei')||null, p_quantity: Number(val('s-quantity'))||1
      });
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Sale logged — invoice downloading');
      const savedSale = Array.isArray(data) ? data[0] : data;
      if(savedSale) generateInvoicePDF(savedSale);
    } catch(e){ showToast('Sale failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-supplier]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-supplier');
    const name = val('sup-name');
    if(!name){ showToast('Name is required', true); return; }
    const data = { name:name, phone:val('sup-phone'), whatsapp:val('sup-phone'), location:val('sup-location'), supplies:val('sup-supplies'), owed:Number(val('sup-owed'))||0 };
    try{
      if(id){
        const { error } = await sb.from('suppliers').update(data).eq('id', id);
        if(error) throw error;
        closeModal(); showToast('Contact updated');
      } else {
        data.dealer_id = state.profile.id;
        const { error } = await sb.from('suppliers').insert(data);
        if(error) throw error;
        closeModal(); showToast('Contact added');
      }
      await refreshAll();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-delete-supplier]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-delete-supplier');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('suppliers').delete().eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Contact deleted');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Delete failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-view-supplier-stock]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-view-supplier-stock');
    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === id; });
    if(!s) return;
    state.inventorySupplierFilter = s.id;
    state.supplierFilterName = s.name;
    setTab('inventory');
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-clear-supplier-filter]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    state.inventorySupplierFilter = null;
    state.supplierFilterName = '';
    render();
  }); });

  /* ---- Consignments (phones out with colleagues on credit) ---- */
  const cnContactId = document.getElementById('cn-contact-id');
  if(cnContactId) cnContactId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === cnContactId.value; });
    if(s){
      const nameEl = document.getElementById('cn-name'), phoneEl = document.getElementById('cn-phone');
      if(nameEl) nameEl.value = s.name;
      if(phoneEl) phoneEl.value = s.phone || '';
    }
  });
  const cnInventoryId = document.getElementById('cn-inventory-id');
  if(cnInventoryId) cnInventoryId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const p = state.inventory.find(function(x){ return x.id === cnInventoryId.value; });
    if(p){
      const set = function(id,v){ const el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.value = v||''; };
      set('cn-model', p.model); set('cn-storage', p.storage); set('cn-color', p.color); set('cn-imei', p.imei);
      if(!val('cn-price') && p.price) set('cn-price', p.price);
    }
  });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-save-consignment');
    const contactName = val('cn-name');
    const model = val('cn-model');
    if(!contactName){ showToast('Colleague name is required', true); return; }
    if(!model){ showToast('Phone model is required', true); return; }
    const data = {
      contact_id: val('cn-contact-id')||null, contact_name: contactName, contact_phone: val('cn-phone'),
      inventory_id: val('cn-inventory-id')||null, model: model, storage: val('cn-storage'), color: val('cn-color'), imei: val('cn-imei')||null,
      quantity: Number(val('cn-quantity'))||1, unit_price: Number(val('cn-price'))||0, amount_paid: Number(val('cn-paid'))||0,
      date_given: val('cn-date')||todayISO(), due_date: val('cn-due')||null, notes: val('cn-notes')
    };
    const total = data.unit_price*data.quantity;
    data.status = data.amount_paid<=0 ? 'Out' : (data.amount_paid>=total ? 'Settled' : 'Partially Paid');
    try{
      if(id){ const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').update(data).eq('id', id); if(error) throw error; }
      else { data.dealer_id = state.profile.id; const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').insert(data); if(error) throw error; }
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast(id?'Consignment updated':'Logged — you\'ll see it under Owed');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Save failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-delete-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-delete-consignment');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').delete().eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Consignment removed');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Delete failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-log-consignment-payment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-log-consignment-payment');
    const c = state.consignments.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
    if(!c) return;
    const amount = Number(val('cnp-amount'))||0;
    if(amount<=0){ showToast('Enter an amount received', true); return; }
    const newPaid = (Number(c.amount_paid)||0) + amount;
    const total = (Number(c.unit_price)||0)*(Number(c.quantity)||1);
    const newStatus = newPaid >= total ? 'Settled' : 'Partially Paid';
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').update({ amount_paid:newPaid, status:newStatus }).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      const { error: payErr } = await sb.from('consignment_payments').insert({
        consignment_id: id, dealer_id: state.profile.id, amount: amount, note: val('cnp-note')||null
      });
      if(payErr) throw payErr;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast(newStatus==='Settled' ? 'Fully paid — marked as settled' : 'Payment logged');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-mark-consignment]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const status = el.getAttribute('data-mark-consignment');
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-id');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('consignments').update({ status:status }).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Marked as '+status.toLowerCase());
    } catch(e){ showToast('Failed: '+(e.message||e), true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-print-invoice]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-print-invoice');
    const sale = state.sales.find(function(s){ return s.id===id; });
    if(sale) generateInvoicePDF(sale); else showToast('Could not find that sale', true);
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-fulfill-request]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-fulfill-request');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('requests').update({status:'Fulfilled'}).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      showToast('Request marked fulfilled'); render();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Update failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-broadcast]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const model = val('b-model');
    if(!model){ showToast('Enter a phone model', true); return; }
    const data = { dealer_id: state.profile.id, type:'Need', model:model, storage:val('b-variant'), urgency: val('b-urgency')||'Normal', status:'Open' };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Broadcast sent to the network');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Broadcast failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-close-broadcast]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const id = el.getAttribute('data-close-broadcast');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').update({status:'Closed'}).eq('id', id);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      showToast('Broadcast closed'); render();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Update failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-accept-response]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const responseId = el.getAttribute('data-accept-response');
    const broadcastId = el.getAttribute('data-broadcast');
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcasts').update({ accepted_response_id: responseId, status: 'Closed' }).eq('id', broadcastId);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      showToast('Marked as accepted — this dealer\'s reputation just went up'); render();
    } catch(e){ showToast('Could not accept: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  app.querySelectorAll('[data-save-response]').forEach(function(el){ el.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const broadcastId = el.getAttribute('data-save-response');
    const price = Number(val('rb-price'));
    if(!price){ showToast('Enter your price', true); return; }
    const data = { broadcast_id: broadcastId, dealer_id: state.profile.id, price:price, quantity:Number(val('rb-qty'))||1, contact_phone: val('rb-phone') };
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('broadcast_responses').insert(data);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      closeModal(); showToast('Response sent');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  }); });

  const biParseBtn = document.getElementById('bi-parse-btn');
  if(biParseBtn) biParseBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){
    const text = val('bi-text');
    state.bulkImportText = text;
    state.bulkImportCondition = val('bi-condition');
    state.bulkImportSupplier = val('bi-supplier');
    state.bulkImportSupplierId = val('bi-supplier-id') || null;
    const parsed = parseBulkStock(text);
    state.bulkImportRows = parsed.rows; state.bulkImportSkipped = parsed.skipped;
    if(!state.bulkImportRows.length){ showToast('No recognizable stock lines found in that paste', true); return; }
    render();
  });
  const biBackBtn = document.getElementById('bi-back-btn');
  if(biBackBtn) biBackBtn.addEventListener('click', function(){ state.bulkImportRows = []; render(); });

  const biSupplierId = document.getElementById('bi-supplier-id');
  if(biSupplierId) biSupplierId.addEventListener('change', function(){
    const s = state.suppliers.find(function(x){ return x.id === biSupplierId.value; });
    const biSupplier = document.getElementById('bi-supplier');
    if(s && biSupplier) biSupplier.value = s.name;
  });

  document.querySelectorAll('[data-bi-include]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('change', function(){ state.bulkImportRows[Number(el.getAttribute('data-bi-include'))].include = el.checked; });
  });
  document.querySelectorAll('[data-bi-field]').forEach(function(el){
    el.addEventListener('input', function(){
      const i = Number(el.getAttribute('data-bi-row')), f = el.getAttribute('data-bi-field');
      state.bulkImportRows[i][f] = el.value;
    });
  });

  const biImportBtn = document.getElementById('bi-import-btn');
  if(biImportBtn) biImportBtn.addEventListener('click', async function(){
    const toInsert = state.bulkImportRows.filter(function(r){ return r.include; }).map(function(r){
      return {
        dealer_id: state.profile.id, model: r.model, storage: r.storage, color: '',
        condition: state.bulkImportCondition, battery: state.bulkImportCondition==='Used' ? 100 : null,
        quantity: Number(r.quantity)||1, supplier: state.bulkImportSupplier || (r.sectionLabel||''),
        supplier_id: state.bulkImportSupplierId || null,
        purchase_date: todayISO(),
        cost: Number(r.price)||0, price: null, status: 'In Stock', shelf: '', notes: 'Bulk imported: '+r.raw
      };
    });
    if(!toInsert.length){ showToast('No rows selected to import', true); return; }
    try{
      const { error } = await sb.from('inventory').insert(toInsert);
      if(error) throw error;
      await refreshAll();
      state.bulkImportRows = []; state.bulkImportText=''; state.bulkImportSupplierId='';
      closeModal(); showToast(toInsert.length+' phones imported');
    } catch(e){ showToast('Import failed: '+e.message, true); render(); }
  });

  ['calc-cost','calc-target','calc-min','calc-offer'].forEach(function(id){
    const el = document.getElementById(id);
    if(el) el.addEventListener('input', function(){
      state.calcInputs = { cost: val('calc-cost')||0, target: val('calc-target')||0, min: val('calc-min')||0, offer: val('calc-offer')||0 };
      render();
    });
  });

  window.addEventListener('hashchange', applyHashTab);
}

applyTheme();
init();
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>

======================================================================================================================================================

README.md

# PhoneHub Pro

Business management platform for Computer Village phone dealers — inventory, sales, profit calculator, and a shared dealer network, backed by Supabase.

## Structure

- `/seller/` — Seller App (dealer registration, inventory, bulk stock import, sales, dealer network, admin oversight)
- `/customer/` — Customer App (shop browsing, phone requests, warranty lookup)
- `schema.sql` — Supabase/Postgres schema. Run this once in your Supabase project's SQL Editor before using the apps. (Already includes optional-IMEI support — you do NOT need `migration_optional_imei.sql` on a fresh project; that file is only for upgrading an older deployment.)
- `SUPABASE_SETUP_GUIDE.md` — step-by-step setup instructions.

## Live URLs (once GitHub Pages is enabled)

- Landing page: `https://<your-username>.github.io/<repo-name>/`
- Seller App: `https://<your-username>.github.io/<repo-name>/seller/`
- Customer App: `https://<your-username>.github.io/<repo-name>/customer/`

## Updating the apps

Both apps are single static HTML files. To ship a change: edit the file, commit, push — GitHub Pages redeploys automatically within a minute or two.

## What's new in this package

- **Bulk stock import** ("📋 Paste stock list" button on the Inventory tab of the Seller App) — dealers can paste their existing WhatsApp/notes-style stock lists (e.g. `Ip14 pro 128–635k`) and the app parses model, storage, and price automatically, with a review step before importing. Cost price is left blank on import since these lists only show selling price — remind dealers to fill that in per phone afterward so profit numbers are accurate.

======================================================================================================================================================

schema.sql

-- ============================================================
-- PhoneHub Pro — Supabase Schema (Phase 2, multi-tenant)
-- ============================================================
-- Run this whole file once in Supabase: Dashboard > SQL Editor > New query > paste > Run.
-- Safe to re-run top-to-bottom on a fresh project.
-- ============================================================

-- Needed for gen_random_uuid()
create extension if not exists "pgcrypto";

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 1. DEALERS  (one row per registered seller, linked to their auth account)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists dealers (
  id uuid primary key references auth.users(id) on delete cascade,
  shop_name text not null,
  shop_slug text unique not null,        -- used in the customer app's shareable link, e.g. /shop/musa-electronics
  phone text,
  whatsapp text,
  location text,
  is_admin boolean not null default false,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);

alter table dealers enable row level security;

-- Security-definer helper: checks admin status while bypassing dealers' own RLS,
-- so policies that need to check "is this caller an admin?" don't recursively
-- re-trigger the dealers table's RLS (which would otherwise infinite-loop).
create or replace function is_admin()
returns boolean
language sql
security definer
set search_path = public
stable
as $$
  select coalesce((select d.is_admin from dealers d where d.id = auth.uid()), false);
$$;

-- Dealers can see & edit their own profile row.
create policy "dealers_select_own" on dealers for select
  using (id = auth.uid());
create policy "dealers_update_own" on dealers for update
  using (id = auth.uid());

-- Admins (you) can see every dealer's profile.
create policy "dealers_select_admin" on dealers for select
  using (is_admin());

-- Auto-create a dealer profile row whenever someone signs up.
-- Expects shop_name / phone / shop_slug passed in as auth signup metadata.
create or replace function handle_new_dealer()
returns trigger
language plpgsql
security definer set search_path = public
as $$
begin
  insert into dealers (id, shop_name, shop_slug, phone, location)
  values (
    new.id,
    coalesce(new.raw_user_meta_data->>'shop_name', 'New Shop'),
    coalesce(new.raw_user_meta_data->>'shop_slug', 'shop-' || substr(new.id::text, 1, 8)),
    new.raw_user_meta_data->>'phone',
    new.raw_user_meta_data->>'location'
  );
  return new;
end;
$$;

drop trigger if exists on_auth_user_created on auth.users;
create trigger on_auth_user_created
  after insert on auth.users
  for each row execute function handle_new_dealer();

-- Public, read-only directory so the Customer App can resolve a shop_slug to a dealer
-- without exposing anything private. Runs as the (trusted) view owner, so it works
-- even though the requester (a customer) isn't logged in.
create or replace view public_shops
  with (security_invoker = false) as
  select id, shop_name, shop_slug, location from dealers;
grant select on public_shops to anon, authenticated;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 2. INVENTORY
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists inventory (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  imei text,
  imei2 text,
  model text not null,
  storage text,
  color text,
  condition text check (condition in ('New','Used')),
  battery int,
  supplier text,
  purchase_date date,
  cost numeric,
  price numeric,
  status text not null default 'In Stock' check (status in ('In Stock','Reserved','Sold','In Repair','Consigned')),
  quantity int not null default 1,
  shelf text,
  notes text,
  image_url text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
alter table inventory add column if not exists image_url text;

-- Multi-image support: image_urls holds every photo for a phone (in display
-- order); image_url is kept in sync as the first photo, for any older code
-- path that still reads the single-image column.
alter table inventory add column if not exists image_urls jsonb not null default '[]'::jsonb;
update inventory set image_urls = jsonb_build_array(image_url)
  where image_url is not null and jsonb_array_length(image_urls) = 0;

-- Laptop support: inventory now holds both phones and laptops, distinguished
-- by item_type. Laptops reuse the shared fields above (model, color, condition,
-- battery, cost, price, status, quantity, shelf, notes, photos, supplier, IMEI
-- left blank) plus a few laptop-only spec columns below. Keeping laptops in the
-- same table means they automatically flow through sales, the dealer network,
-- broadcasts, consignments ("Owed to you"), and the Customer App catalog —
-- nothing else needs a parallel table.
alter table inventory add column if not exists item_type text not null default 'Phone';
alter table inventory drop constraint if exists inventory_item_type_check;
alter table inventory add constraint inventory_item_type_check check (item_type in ('Phone','Laptop'));
alter table inventory add column if not exists brand text;       -- laptop brand, e.g. HP, Dell, Apple
alter table inventory add column if not exists cpu text;         -- e.g. Intel Core i7-1165G7
alter table inventory add column if not exists ram text;         -- e.g. 16GB
alter table inventory add column if not exists screen_size text; -- e.g. 15.6"
alter table inventory add column if not exists gpu text;         -- optional, e.g. RTX 3050

create index if not exists idx_inventory_dealer on inventory(dealer_id);
create index if not exists idx_inventory_item_type on inventory(item_type);
create index if not exists idx_inventory_model on inventory using gin (to_tsvector('simple', model));

alter table inventory enable row level security;

create policy "inventory_all_own" on inventory for all
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid())
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());

create policy "inventory_select_admin" on inventory for select
  using (is_admin());

-- Cross-dealer search, for logged-in dealers only. Deliberately excludes cost/supplier
-- so no dealer can see another dealer's margins — only what a buyer needs to know.
drop view if exists dealer_network_view;
create or replace view dealer_network_view
  with (security_invoker = false) as
  select
    i.id, i.dealer_id, d.shop_name as dealer_name, d.phone as dealer_phone,
    i.item_type, i.model, i.storage, i.color, i.condition, i.battery, i.price, i.updated_at,
    i.brand, i.cpu, i.ram, i.screen_size, i.gpu,
    i.image_url, i.image_urls
  from inventory i
  join dealers d on d.id = i.dealer_id
  where i.status = 'In Stock';
grant select on dealer_network_view to authenticated;

-- Public storefront catalog for the Customer App (one dealer's in-stock phones
-- and laptops only, no cost/supplier/IMEI exposed).
drop view if exists public_catalog;
create or replace view public_catalog
  with (security_invoker = false) as
  select id, dealer_id, item_type, model, storage, color, condition, battery, price, status,
         brand, cpu, ram, screen_size, gpu, image_url, image_urls
  from inventory
  where status = 'In Stock';
grant select on public_catalog to anon, authenticated;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 3. SALES
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists sales (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  date date not null default current_date,
  imei text,
  model text,
  cost numeric,
  sale_price numeric,
  customer_name text,
  customer_phone text,
  payment_method text,
  staff text,
  warranty_days int default 0,
  quantity int not null default 1,
  accessories text,
  notes text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
create index if not exists idx_sales_dealer on sales(dealer_id);
create index if not exists idx_sales_customer_phone on sales(customer_phone);

alter table sales enable row level security;

create policy "sales_all_own" on sales for all
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid())
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());

create policy "sales_select_admin" on sales for select
  using (is_admin());

-- Lets a customer look up THEIR OWN purchase/warranty history by phone number,
-- without exposing anyone else's sales. Only the fields they need, nothing private.
create or replace function lookup_my_purchases(p_phone text)
returns table (model text, date date, sale_price numeric, warranty_days int, shop_name text)
language sql
security definer set search_path = public
as $$
  select s.model, s.date, s.sale_price, s.warranty_days, d.shop_name
  from sales s join dealers d on d.id = s.dealer_id
  where regexp_replace(s.customer_phone, '\s', '', 'g') = regexp_replace(p_phone, '\s', '', 'g');
$$;
grant execute on function lookup_my_purchases(text) to anon, authenticated;

-- Records a sale and marks the phone Sold, atomically, for the CURRENT dealer only.
-- Runs with the caller's own privileges (not security definer), so normal RLS
-- still applies — a dealer can only ever sell their own in-stock phones.
-- Matches by inventory id (not IMEI) since IMEI is optional and multiple
-- IMEI-less phones would otherwise be indistinguishable.
drop function if exists sell_phone(uuid,numeric,text,text,text,text,int,text,text);

create or replace function sell_phone(
  p_inventory_id uuid, p_sale_price numeric, p_customer_name text, p_customer_phone text,
  p_payment_method text, p_staff text, p_warranty_days int, p_accessories text, p_notes text,
  p_imei text default null, p_quantity int default 1
)
returns sales
language plpgsql
as $$
declare
  v_phone inventory%rowtype;
  v_sale sales%rowtype;
  v_remaining int;
begin
  select * into v_phone from inventory
    where id = p_inventory_id and dealer_id = auth.uid() and status = 'In Stock'
    limit 1;

  if v_phone.id is null then
    raise exception 'No in-stock phone found for that selection';
  end if;

  if p_quantity is null or p_quantity < 1 then
    p_quantity := 1;
  end if;

  if v_phone.quantity < p_quantity then
    raise exception 'Only % in stock — cannot sell %', v_phone.quantity, p_quantity;
  end if;

  insert into sales (dealer_id, imei, model, cost, sale_price, customer_name, customer_phone,
                      payment_method, staff, warranty_days, accessories, notes, quantity)
  values (auth.uid(), coalesce(p_imei, v_phone.imei), v_phone.model, v_phone.cost, p_sale_price, p_customer_name, p_customer_phone,
          p_payment_method, p_staff, p_warranty_days, p_accessories, p_notes, p_quantity)
  returning * into v_sale;

  v_remaining := v_phone.quantity - p_quantity;

  update inventory
    set quantity = v_remaining,
        status = case when v_remaining <= 0 then 'Sold' else 'In Stock' end,
        updated_at = now()
    where id = v_phone.id;

  return v_sale;
end;
$$;
grant execute on function sell_phone(uuid,numeric,text,text,text,text,int,text,text,text,int) to authenticated;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 4. REQUESTS  (customer waiting-list asks, submitted from the Customer App)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists requests (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  date date not null default current_date,
  customer_name text,
  customer_phone text,
  model text not null,
  storage text,
  color text,
  budget numeric,
  status text not null default 'Pending' check (status in ('Pending','Fulfilled','Cancelled')),
  notes text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
create index if not exists idx_requests_dealer on requests(dealer_id);

alter table requests enable row level security;

-- Anyone (a customer, not logged in) can submit a request to a specific shop.
create policy "requests_insert_anyone" on requests for insert
  with check (true);

-- Only the shop it was sent to (or an admin) can read/manage it.
create policy "requests_select_own" on requests for select
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid());
create policy "requests_update_own" on requests for update
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid());
create policy "requests_select_admin" on requests for select
  using (is_admin());

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 5. SUPPLIERS  (each dealer's own private colleague/supplier contacts)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists suppliers (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  name text not null,
  phone text,
  whatsapp text,
  location text,
  supplies text,
  notes text,
  owed numeric default 0,
  due date,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
alter table suppliers enable row level security;
create policy "suppliers_all_own" on suppliers for all
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid())
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());
create policy "suppliers_select_admin" on suppliers for select
  using (is_admin());

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 5b. INVENTORY <-> SUPPLIERS  (link phones to a tracked contact by id, not name)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
alter table inventory add column if not exists supplier_id uuid references suppliers(id) on delete set null;
create index if not exists idx_inventory_supplier_id on inventory(supplier_id);

-- One-time backfill: match existing inventory.supplier text to a contact with
-- the same name (case/whitespace-insensitive), for the same dealer.
update inventory i
set supplier_id = s.id
from suppliers s
where i.supplier_id is null
  and i.supplier is not null
  and s.dealer_id = i.dealer_id
  and lower(trim(i.supplier)) = lower(trim(s.name));

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 6. BROADCASTS + RESPONSES  (network-wide "need this phone urgently", or a
--    "Stock" advert for one or more inventory items being offered for sale)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists broadcasts (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,   -- who's asking / advertising
  date date not null default current_date,
  type text not null default 'Need' check (type in ('Need','Stock')),
  model text not null,        -- for type='Stock' with multiple items, a summary label (e.g. "3 phones")
  storage text,
  color text,
  urgency text,
  items jsonb not null default '[]'::jsonb,   -- type='Stock': [{inventory_id, model, storage, color, condition, price, image_url, image_urls}, ...]
  message text,                                -- optional free-text note shown with a Stock advert
  status text not null default 'Open' check (status in ('Open','Closed')),
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
alter table broadcasts enable row level security;

-- Every registered dealer can see every open broadcast — that's the point of the network.
create policy "broadcasts_select_all" on broadcasts for select
  using (auth.uid() is not null);
create policy "broadcasts_insert_own" on broadcasts for insert
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());
create policy "broadcasts_update_own" on broadcasts for update
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid());

create table if not exists broadcast_responses (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  broadcast_id uuid not null references broadcasts(id) on delete cascade,
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,   -- who's responding
  price numeric,
  quantity int default 1,
  contact_phone text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
alter table broadcast_responses enable row level security;

create policy "broadcast_responses_select_all" on broadcast_responses for select
  using (auth.uid() is not null);
create policy "broadcast_responses_insert_own" on broadcast_responses for insert
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 6b. CONSIGNMENTS  ("Owed to you" — phones colleagues collected from you on
--     credit, and what they still owe. A private ledger, not network-visible.)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists consignments (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  contact_id uuid references suppliers(id) on delete set null,
  contact_name text not null,
  contact_phone text,
  inventory_id uuid references inventory(id) on delete set null,
  model text not null,
  storage text,
  color text,
  imei text,
  quantity int not null default 1,
  unit_price numeric not null default 0,
  amount_paid numeric not null default 0,
  status text not null default 'Out' check (status in ('Out','Partially Paid','Settled','Returned')),
  date_given date not null default current_date,
  due_date date,
  notes text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now(),
  updated_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
create index if not exists idx_consignments_dealer on consignments(dealer_id);
alter table consignments enable row level security;

create policy "consignments_all_own" on consignments for all
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid())
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());
create policy "consignments_select_admin" on consignments for select
  using (is_admin());

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 6c. CONSIGNMENT PAYMENTS  (payment log behind each "Owed to you" entry —
--     powers the detail dialog opened by clicking a row)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists consignment_payments (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  consignment_id uuid not null references consignments(id) on delete cascade,
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  amount numeric not null,
  note text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
create index if not exists idx_consignment_payments_consignment on consignment_payments(consignment_id);
alter table consignment_payments enable row level security;

create policy "consignment_payments_all_own" on consignment_payments for all
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid())
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());
create policy "consignment_payments_select_admin" on consignment_payments for select
  using (is_admin());

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 6d. STOCK BROADCAST LOG  (private record of stock adverts sent straight to
--     saved contacts via WhatsApp — never visible to other dealers)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
create table if not exists stock_broadcast_log (
  id uuid primary key default gen_random_uuid(),
  dealer_id uuid not null references dealers(id) on delete cascade,
  contact_names text,
  items jsonb not null default '[]'::jsonb,
  message text,
  created_at timestamptz not null default now()
);
alter table stock_broadcast_log enable row level security;

create policy "stock_broadcast_log_all_own" on stock_broadcast_log for all
  using (dealer_id = auth.uid())
  with check (dealer_id = auth.uid());

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 7. REALTIME  (required for the seller app's live broadcast updates)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
alter publication supabase_realtime add table broadcasts;
alter publication supabase_realtime add table broadcast_responses;

-- ------------------------------------------------------------
-- 8. STORAGE  (phone photos — public read, dealers can only manage their own folder)
-- ------------------------------------------------------------
insert into storage.buckets (id, name, public)
  values ('phone-images', 'phone-images', true)
  on conflict (id) do nothing;

-- Anyone can view phone photos (needed for the public Customer App catalog).
create policy "phone_images_public_read" on storage.objects for select
  using (bucket_id = 'phone-images');

-- A logged-in dealer can only upload/replace/delete files inside a folder
-- named after their own dealer id, e.g. phone-images/<dealer_id>/xyz.jpg
create policy "phone_images_insert_own" on storage.objects for insert
  with check (bucket_id = 'phone-images' and (storage.foldername(name))[1] = auth.uid()::text);
create policy "phone_images_update_own" on storage.objects for update
  using (bucket_id = 'phone-images' and (storage.foldername(name))[1] = auth.uid()::text);
create policy "phone_images_delete_own" on storage.objects for delete
  using (bucket_id = 'phone-images' and (storage.foldername(name))[1] = auth.uid()::text);

-- ============================================================
-- After running this file:
-- 1. Sign up your own account through the Seller App (this creates your dealer row).
-- 2. Run:  update dealers set is_admin = true where shop_slug = 'your-shop-slug';
--    (or `where id = 'your-auth-user-id'` — find it in Authentication > Users)
-- ============================================================

SUPABASE_SETUP_GUIDE.md

# PhoneHub Pro — Supabase Setup Guide
### Real multi-tenant database, free tier, ready for your first 10–50 dealers

---

## Step 1 — Create your Supabase project

1. Go to [supabase.com](https://supabase.com) → sign up (free) → **New project**.
2. Pick a name (e.g. "phonehub-pro"), a database password (save it somewhere), and a region close to Nigeria (e.g. an EU region is usually the lowest latency option currently offered).
3. Wait ~2 minutes for it to provision.

## Step 2 — Run the schema

1. In your project, open the **SQL Editor** (left sidebar).
2. Click **New query**, paste in the entire contents of **schema.sql**, and click **Run**.
3. You should see a series of "CREATE TABLE / CREATE POLICY / CREATE VIEW" success messages with no errors. This creates every table, security rule, and the two special database functions (`sell_phone`, `lookup_my_purchases`) that both apps depend on.

> Note: `schema.sql` in this package already has IMEI as optional and `sell_phone` matching by inventory ID. You do **not** need to separately run `migration_optional_imei.sql` on a fresh project — that file exists only to upgrade an older deployment that used an earlier version of the schema.

## Step 3 — Turn off email confirmation (recommended for testing)

By default, Supabase requires users to click an email confirmation link before they can log in. For fast testing with your first dealers, turn this off:

1. **Authentication → Providers → Email**.
2. Turn off **"Confirm email"**.
3. Save.

(You can turn this back on later once you want production-grade signups.)

## Step 4 — Get your API keys

1. **Settings → API**.
2. Copy the **Project URL** (looks like `https://xxxxx.supabase.co`) and the **anon public** key (a long string starting with `eyJ...`). Do NOT use the `service_role` key in the apps — that key bypasses all security rules and must never go in client-facing code.

## Step 5 — Connect both apps

1. Open the **Seller App** — first launch asks for these two values. Paste them in and click Connect.
2. You'll land on a Register/Log in screen. **Register your own shop first** — this is how you'll test as a dealer.
3. Open the **Customer App** — it asks for the same two values once. After that, it shows a shop picker listing every registered dealer.

> If you've deployed this for real and don't want every visitor to see the "Connect" screen, paste your project URL and anon key directly into the `HARDCODED_SUPABASE_URL` / `HARDCODED_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY` constants near the top of each app's `<script>` — both files already have a placeholder for this.

## Step 6 — Make yourself admin

1. After registering in the Seller App, go back to Supabase's **SQL Editor** and run:
   ```sql
   update dealers set is_admin = true where shop_slug = 'your-shop-slug-here';
   ```
   (Find your exact `shop_slug` by running `select shop_name, shop_slug from dealers;` first.)
2. Refresh/re-log into the Seller App — you'll now see an **Admin** tab showing every dealer, their stock counts, and total platform revenue.

## Deploying with GitHub Pages

1. Create a new GitHub repo and push the contents of this folder (keep the `seller/` and `customer/` subfolders intact).
2. Repo → **Settings → Pages** → set source to the `main` branch, root folder.
3. Wait a minute or two — your site will be live at `https://<your-username>.github.io/<repo-name>/`.

## Everyday use

- **Each dealer registers their own account** — their inventory, sales, and customer requests are automatically private to them (enforced by the database itself, not just app-level logic).
- **Inventory → "📋 Paste stock list"** lets a dealer paste their existing WhatsApp/notes-style stock list in bulk instead of typing each phone in one at a time.
- **Dealer Network tab → Search stock** shows every registered dealer's in-stock phones (price, model, condition) so any dealer can find who has what — without ever seeing each other's cost prices.
- **Broadcasts** are visible to every dealer instantly — no WhatsApp groups, no ban risk.
- **Customer App** — anyone who picks a shop sees only that shop's real-time catalog; submitting a request writes straight into that dealer's Seller App "Asks" tab. "My purchases" searches across *all* shops by phone number, so a customer only needs to remember their own number, not which shop they bought from.

## Cost & limits at this stage

Supabase's free tier includes 500MB database storage and 50,000 monthly active users — far beyond what 10–50 dealers and their customers will use. You will not need a paid plan until you're seeing real scale (many hundreds of dealers or heavy daily traffic), at which point upgrading is a plan change, not a rebuild.

If you hit Supabase's auth email rate limit (2/hour on the shared testing SMTP) while testing signups, either wait ~30–60 minutes for it to clear, or set up free custom SMTP (Resend's free tier gives 3,000 emails/month, no card needed; Brevo is another good option) under **Authentication → Settings → SMTP Settings** — this removes the cap entirely once you're onboarding real dealers.

## What's next (Phase 4 ideas, once this is proven)

- WhatsApp/SMS delivery for warranty reminders and broadcast alerts (needs a paid messaging API — Meta Cloud API or Twilio — this is the one piece that genuinely can't be free)
- Invoice/receipt PDF generation
- A dealer reputation/verification layer (fulfillment rate, response time) now that broadcasts have real responders
- Paid plans / monetization once dealers are asking to pay

======================================================================================================================================================

seller\sw.js

// PhoneHub Pro — Seller service worker
// Handles incoming Web Push events so alerts show up (with sound + vibration)
// even when the app isn't open, and routes taps back into the app.

self.addEventListener('install', function(event){
  self.skipWaiting();
});

self.addEventListener('activate', function(event){
  event.waitUntil(self.clients.claim());
});

self.addEventListener('push', function(event){
  var data = {};
  try{ data = event.data ? event.data.json() : {}; }
  catch(e){ data = { title: 'PhoneHub Pro', body: event.data ? event.data.text() : '' }; }

  var title = data.title || 'PhoneHub Pro';
  var options = {
    body: data.body || '',
    icon: './icon-192.png',
    badge: './icon-192.png',
    // Default device notification sound plays automatically unless silent:true —
    // the Web Notification API doesn't support a custom .mp3, but vibration +
    // the OS's own alert tone is what gets a dealer's attention even screen-off.
    silent: false,
    vibrate: [250, 100, 250, 100, 250],
    tag: data.tag || ('phonehub-' + (data.type || 'alert')),
    renotify: true,
    requireInteraction: data.type === 'request' || data.type === 'broadcast',
    data: { url: data.url || './', type: data.type || 'alert' }
  };

  event.waitUntil(self.registration.showNotification(title, options));
});

self.addEventListener('notificationclick', function(event){
  event.notification.close();
  var targetPath = (event.notification.data && event.notification.data.url) || './';
  var notifType = (event.notification.data && event.notification.data.type) || 'alert';

  if (targetPath === './' || targetPath === '.' || targetPath === ''){
    var typeToPath = {
      request: './#tab=requests',
      broadcast: './#tab=network',
      warranty: './#tab=sales',
      stock: './#tab=inventory',
      response: './#tab=network'
    };
    targetPath = typeToPath[notifType] || './';
  }

  event.waitUntil(
    self.clients.matchAll({ type: 'window', includeUncontrolled: true }).then(function(clientList){
      for (var i = 0; i < clientList.length; i++){
        var client = clientList[i];
        if ('focus' in client){
          client.focus();
          if ('navigate' in client) { try { client.navigate(targetPath); } catch(e){} }
          return;
        }
      }
      if (self.clients.openWindow) return self.clients.openWindow(targetPath);
    })
  );
});
